# 1. Product OLD

**text-only, tree-style UX outline**, 

This is the **master product documentation**. It includes:

- **Header & Footer Always Visible Elements (For ALL Users)**
*(Public visitors, Home-Hunters, Owners — everyone sees these)*
    
    ---
    
    # **Header Navigation (Always Visible)**
    
    ```
    [NoAgent]   [Services & Pricing]   [About]   [List Your Place]  
    ```
    
    - **Header Link Routing Guide (Designer + Developer Notes)**
        
        ---
        
        ## **1. Purpose (1 sentence)**
        
        A clean, always-visible top navigation bar that uses Dashfolio+ defaults and leads users to core public pages and the “List Your Place” onboarding flow.
        
        ---
        
        # **2. Header Layout (Updated)**
        
        ### **LEFT**
        
        ### **🏡 NoAgent**
        
        - Permanent link to **Home** (/)
        - **Always displayed in NoAgent(#F8D22A)**
        - Hover: same yellow, no underline
        - No logo image needed — text only
        
        ---
        
        ### **CENTER NAVIGATION**
        
        *(Normal Dashfolio font + white text)*
        
        - **Services & Pricing**
        - **About**
        - Hover: slightly darker yellow (Dashfolio default hover behavior)
        
        ---
        
        ### **RIGHT CTA**
        
        **[ List Your Place ]**
        
        - Primary button
        - Fill color: NoAgent **Yellow**
        - Hover: slightly darker yellow (Dashfolio default hover behavior)
        
        ---
        
        # **3. Colors & Typography**
        
        - Typography: **Dashfolio+ default** (Plus Jakarta Sans)
        - Header background: **Dashfolio dark**
        - Default link color: **White**
        - Hover color (non-brand text): **Yalla Yellow**
        
        > Only the “NoAgent” brand text is ALWAYS yellow.
        > 
        
        ---
        
        # **4. Header → Page Routing (Designer + Developer Notes)**
        
        ### **Yalla.House**
        
        - **Route:** /
        - **What opens:** The public landing page
        - **Used by:** Everyone (Owners, Home-hunters, Public)
        
        ---
        
        ### **Services & Pricing**
        
        - **Route:** /services
        - **Page type:** **One Wireframe**
        - **Contents (simple boxes):**
            - 360° Scan
            - Floorplan creation
            - Professional photos
            - Legal support
            - For Sale board (Sign)
            - Advertising packages (Rightmove / Zoopla etc.)
            - Hands-on support
            - Pricing tiers
        - **Design:**
            - Cards/boxes
            - Short descriptions
            - “Add to my Listing” buttons (later phase)
        
        ---
        
        ### **About**
        
        - **Route:** /about
        - **Page type:** **Single page**
        - **Contents:**
            - Short mission (“No fees. No commission.”)
            - Why Yalla.House exists
            - Founder info (optional)
            - Trust symbols / data protection
        
        ---
        
        ### **List Your Place**
        
        - **Route:** /list
        - **Flow:**
            1. Shows login prompt (if user not logged in)
            2. After login → jumps directly to **WF-O2 (My Listings)**
            3. Starts at **First-Time Wizard** (Step 1 – Basics)
        - **Design:**
            
            Dashfolio “form panel” style with progress bar. See  WF Owner 2 
            
        
        ---
        
        # **5. Developer Summary**
        
        - Use Dashfolio header component
        - Insert our nav labels
        - Set brand text color = #F8D22A
        - Set CTA color = #F8D22A
        - Ensure routing works as defined
        - Do NOT add login button (login lives in sidebar only)
        
        ---
        
    
    ---
    
    # **FOOTER (Always Visible)**
    
    ```jsx
    								                   NoAgent FOOTER
    ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    
    COLUMN 1 — Brand & Company           COLUMN 2 — Policies           COLUMN 3 — Legal & Compliance        COLUMN 4 — Contact
    ────────────────────────────────     ───────────────────────────    ───────────────────────────────       ──────────────────────────────
    No.Agent                             Privacy Policy                GDPR & Safety Statement              Support (mailto:support@noagent.global)
    “No fees. No commission.”            Terms of Service              Imprint                              WhatsApp (chat link)
    Company No: 1234                     Cookie Policy                 Security & Data Protection           
    Registered in England & Wales.                                                                          
    ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    © 2026 NoAgent — A UKConsultant Project. All rights reserved.
    ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    ```
    
    - **Footer Link Routing Guide (Designer + Developer Notes)**
        
        ---
        
        **COLUMN 1 — Brand & Company**
        
        ### **NoAgent (Logo / Text)**
        
        - **Action:** Always routes to **Home Page** (/).
        - **Designer note:**
            
            Use standard Dashfolio+ header style. Hover = Yalla yellow.
            
        - **Developer note:**
            
            Set as a global navigation home link. No other behavior.
            
        
        ---
        
        ## **COLUMN 2 — Policies (all use a shared layout)**
        
        ### **Privacy Policy**
        
        - **Action:** Opens dedicated policy page (/privacy-policy). Hoe do we do this country specific ?
        - **Designer note:**
            
            *Uses the unified “Legal Page Wireframe”—simple headline, left-nav anchors, clean text layout.*
            
        - **Developer note:**
            
            Anchor-ready sections (#data, #rights, etc.).
            
            SEO index allowed.
            
        
        ### **Terms of Service**
        
        - **Action:** Opens (/terms).
        - Designer/Developer rules:
            
            Same template as Privacy Policy. No custom design per page.
            
        
        ### **Cookie Policy**
        
        - **Action:** Opens (/cookies).
        - Designer/Developer rules:
            
            Same shared “Legal Page” template. No new wireframe needed.
            
            Cookie banner must link to this page.
            
        
        > Developer note:
        > 
        
        > All Policies share one React/Framer template (3 pages, 1 component). Reuse banner, spacing, typography.
        > 
        
        ---
        
        ## **COLUMN 3 — Legal & Compliance**
        
        ### **GDPR & Safety**
        
        - **Action:** Scrolls to GDPR section inside /privacy-policy
            
            → **Anchor link:** /privacy-policy#gdpr
            
        - **Designer note:**
            
            No new page. Just a highlighted section inside Privacy Policy.
            
        - **Developer note:**
            
            Must support scrolling to anchors even on mobile.
            
        
        ### **Imprint (DE only)**
        
        - **Action:** Opens /imprint
        - Designer note:
            
            Only appears once Germany rollout is active. Same “Legal Page” template.
            
        - Developer note:
            
            Controlled by country toggle in admin (show_imprint = true/false).
            
        
        ### **Security & Data Protection**
        
        - **Action:** Opens /security
        - Designer note:
            
            Reuse “Legal Page” layout.
            
        - Developer note:
            
            Simple static content page; no integrations needed.
            
        
        ---
        
        ## **COLUMN 4 — Contact**
        
        ### **Support**
        
        - **Action:** mailto:support@noagent.global
        - Designer note:
            
            Simple link—no modal.
            
            Keep consistent with other footer links (white text + yellow hover).
            
        - Developer note:
            
            Use mailto: with subject prefilled:
            
            ?subject=Support Request - NoAgent
            
        
        ### **WhatsApp**
        
        - **Action:** Opens WhatsApp chat
            
            → https://wa.me/<NUMBER>
            
        - Designer note:
            
            Use text-only, no icon in footer.
            
        - Developer note:
            
            Must open WhatsApp on mobile or WhatsApp Web on desktop.
            
        
        ---
        
        # **🔧 Developer Routing Summary (one-line per link)**
        
        | **Link** | **Route** | **Template** | **Special Rules** |
        | --- | --- | --- | --- |
        | NoAgent | / | Home | Always visible |
        | Privacy Policy | /privacy-policy | Legal template | Anchor-ready |
        | Terms of Service | /terms | Legal template | — |
        | Cookie Policy | /cookies | Legal template | Linked from cookie banner |
        | GDPR & Safety | /privacy-policy#gdpr | Legal template | Anchor scroll |
        | Imprint | /imprint | Legal template | Conditional (DE only) |
        | Security | /security | Legal template | — |
        | Support | mailto:support@noagent.global | — | Subject prefill |
        | WhatsApp | wa.me/<number> | — | Auto-detect device |
        
        ---
        
        # **🎨 Designer Summary**
        
        - All **Policies**, **Legal**, and **Imprint** pages use **one unified legal-page layout**.
        - Footer links are text-only, white → yellow on hover.
        - Layout = simple, minimalist, no extra icons, no images.
        - Must visually match Dashfolio+ dark theme.

    ### **PERMISSIONS SUMMARY**
    
    | **Area** | **Logged-Out Public** | **Home-Hunter** | **Owner** | **Admin** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Header | ✔ | ✔ | ✔ | ✔ |
    | Footer | ✔ | ✔ | ✔ | ✔ |
    | Owner Sidebar | ✘ | ✘ | ✔ | ✔ |
    | Owner Profile Menu | ✘ | ✘ | ✔ | ✔ |
    | Home-Hunter Sidebar | ✘ | ✔ | ✘ | ✔ |
    
    This ensures clean separation between user roles.
    
    ---
    
- **WF-ACC — Unified Account Settings (Owner + Home-Hunter)**
    
    > WF-ACC is a single, role-aware Account Settings page for Owners and Home-Hunters, with auto-detected country, shared identity & security sections, and role-specific blocks for billing, integrations, services (Owners) and buying position, documents, and purchased surveys (Home-Hunters).
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ---
    
    ## **1. Designer Checklist**
    
    - Use **Dashfolio+ dark** layout, standard form styles.
    - Page structure = **single column**, split into sections:
        1. Personal Details
        2. Contact Information
        3. Notifications
        4. Security
        5. GDPR & Data
        6. **Owner-only: Billing, Integrations, Services**
        7. **Home-Hunter-only: Buying Position, Documents, Purchased Surveys**
    - Sections should be **collapsible** for long pages.
    - Show **success state** after save (small “Saved ✓” status).
    - Use **Yalla Yellow** only for:
        - Primary buttons
        - Important labels (e.g. Verified)
    - Mobile: same content, stacked.
    
    ---
    
    ## **2. Developer Checklist**
    
    - Single page, single route:
        
        GET /account/settings / POST /account/settings
        
    - **Role-aware rendering**:
        - If role === "owner" → show Owner section.
        - If role === "homeHunter" → show HH section.
    - Auto-detect **country** on first login via GeoIP:
        - Default to **United Kingdom** if nothing detected.
    - All labels must use **i18n** (language-ready).
    - Each section saves **independently** (partial updates).
    - Integrate:
        - Stripe (billing)
        - Twilio/WhatsApp (phone verification, later)
        - Internal services for “services & add-ons” and “purchased surveys”.
    
    ---
    
    ## **3. Journey Summary (Short)**
    
    - **Owners** use this page to:
        - Keep contact info up to date
        - Manage billing & plan
        - See/add services (photos, signs, EPC, surveys, etc.)
        - Manage integrations (Google Calendar, WhatsApp)
    - **Home-Hunters** use this page to:
        - Complete their profile
        - Set buying position (Cash / Mortgage etc.)
        - Manage notification preferences
        - See purchased surveys
        - Upload docs later (ID, proof of income)
    
    This page feeds trust + smoother offers + less friction.
    
    ---
    
    ## **4. Where This Page Sits**
    
    **For both roles:**
    
    - Accessible from:
        - Sidebar “Account Settings” (top)
        - Profile/avatar dropdown (if used)
        - “Complete your profile” prompts in:
            - Booking confirmation
            - Offer / Application flow
    
    ---
    
    ## **5. Purpose**
    
    - Give **one central place** to manage:
        - Identity
        - Contact details
        - Notifications
        - Security
        - Country / locale
        - Role-specific tools:
            - Owner: billing, integrations, services
            - HH: buying status, docs, surveys
    - Reduce support load and confusion.
    
    ---
    
    ## **6. What This Page Should Solve**
    
    - Owners know:
        - Which plan they’re on
        - Which services they’ve ordered
        - What’s connected (Calendar, WhatsApp)
    - Home-Hunters know:
        - How “strong” they look to Owners
        - Which surveys they’ve unlocked
    - Both:
        - Can keep email/phone current → fewer failed messages
        - Can manage notifications & privacy
        - Have one place to manage their account
    
    ---
    
    ## **7. Layout & Sections (Designer Spec)**
    
    ### **7.1 Header**
    
    **Title:** Account Settings
    
    **Subtitle:** Manage your profile, services and preferences.
    
    ---
    
    ### **7.2 Section 1 — Personal Details (Shared)**
    
    Fields:
    
    - First Name
    - Last Name
    - Preferred Name (optional)
    - **Country**
        - Dropdown:
            - Auto-filled from GeoIP on first load
            - MVP: United Kingdom as default
        - Copy for designers:
            
            > “Auto-detected & editable. For MVP, only UK is active; more countries can be added later with no layout change.”
            > 
    
    ---
    
    ### **7.3 Section 2 — Contact Information (Shared)**
    
    Fields:
    
    - Email
        - Show “Verified ✓” or “Verify” link
    - Phone
        - with “Verified / Not Verified” chip
    - Preferred Contact Method:
        - Email
        - SMS
        - WhatsApp
    
    Small hint:
    
    > “We only share your details when it’s needed to progress your viewing or offer.”
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ### **7.4 Section 3 — Notifications (Shared)**
    
    Toggles:
    
    - Viewing reminders
    - New messages
    - Offer / Application updates
    - Price changes for saved places *(only shown if role = homeHunter)*
    - Service & billing notifications *(only shown if role = owner)*
    - “Tips & product news” (marketing opt-in)
    
    ---
    
    ### **7.5 Section 4 — Security (Shared)**
    
    - Change Password
    - 2FA (placeholder, Phase 2)
    - “Log out of all devices” (Phase 2)
    
    ---
    
    ### **7.6 Section 5 — GDPR & Data (Shared)**
    
    - **Request Data Export** (button)
    - **Delete Account** (button)
    - Link: “Read our GDPR & Safety policy”
    
    ---
    
    ## **8. Owner-only Block (Conditional)**
    
    > Show only when role === "owner"
    > 
    
    ### **8.1 Billing & Subscription**
    
    - Current plan:
        - e.g. “Starter / Pro / Full Service”
    - Renewal date & charge:
        - e.g. “Next billing: 12 Apr 2026 — £29/month”
    - Buttons:
        - [Update Payment Method]
        - [Download Invoices]
        - [Upgrade Plan]
    
    ---
    
    ### **8.2 Integrations**
    
    List:
    
    - Google Calendar — Connected / Not Connected
    - WhatsApp (Twilio) — Connected / Setup Pending
    - Airtable / Internal CRM — Connected / Not Connected
    
    Buttons per integration:
    
    - [Connect] / [Disconnect] / [Configure]
    
    ---
    
    ### **8.3**
    
    ### **Your Services & Add-ons (Owner Services)**
    
    This ties into Admin **Tasks & Fulfilment**.
    
    Show per listing:
    
    **Example block**
    
    > Your Services for 12 King Street
    > 
    - ✓ Professional Photos — Completed (12 Mar)
    - ✓ Floorplan — Delivered (PDF)
    - ⧗ For Sale Sign — Scheduled (18 Mar, 10:00)
    - ○ Pre-Sale Survey — Not ordered
    
    > 
    > 
    
    > [Order More Services]
    > 
    
    Designer notes:
    
    - Use a simple card per **Place** with a list of service items.
    - Status pills: Not ordered / Ordered / Scheduled / Completed.
    
    Developer model (concept):
    
    ```
    {
      "serviceId": "srv1",
      "ownerId": "o1",
      "propertyId": "p1",
      "type": "photos | floorplan | sign | epc | presale_survey",
      "status": "not_ordered | ordered | scheduled | completed",
      "scheduledFor": "2026-03-18T10:00:00Z"
    }
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **9. Home-Hunter-only Block (Conditional)**
    
    > Show only when role === "homeHunter"
    > 
    
    ### **9.1 Buying Position**
    
    Dropdown:
    
    - Cash Buyer
    - Mortgage in Principle
    - Mortgage in Progress
    - Just Browsing
    
    Hint:
    
    > “Owners are more likely to accept offers from buyers with a clear buying position.”
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ### **9.2 Documents (Phase 2, but space reserved)**
    
    Slots:
    
    - ID (passport / driving licence)
    - Proof of address
    - Mortgage in Principle (upload)
    - Proof of income (for renting)
    
    Statuses: “Not uploaded / Uploaded / Verified”.
    
    ---
    
    ### **9.3**
    
    ### **Purchased Surveys**
    
    This ties to WF-H4/H5 and Admin WF-A6 (Survey Marketplace).
    
    List:
    
    > Your Surveys
    > 
    - 12 King Street — RICS Level 2 — Purchased on 5 Mar
        
        > [Download Report]
        > 
        
        > [View Property]
        > 
    
    > 
    > 
    
    > If none:
    > 
    
    > “You haven’t unlocked any surveys yet.”
    > 
    
    > [See available surveys when viewing places]
    > 
    
    Developer model (concept):
    
    ```
    {
      "surveyId": "sv1",
      "userId": "hh1",
      "propertyId": "p1",
      "type": "level_2 | level_3 | valuation_only",
      "purchasedAt": "2026-03-05T10:00:00Z",
      "downloadUrl": "..."
    }
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **10. Developer Requirements (Key Points)**
    
    - Use **GeoIP** at first login to set country, fallback to "United Kingdom":
    
    ```
    const defaultCountry = request.geo?.country || "United Kingdom";
    ```
    
    - 
    - Only show extra countries in dropdown later when ready (DE, etc.).
    - Use **role-based rendering** for Owner vs Home-Hunter sections.
    - Connect **Owner Services** to:
        - Orders created from Services & Pricing page
        - Admin task board (WF-A4)
    - Connect **Purchased Surveys** to:
        - Survey marketplace logic (WF-A6, HH flows)
    - All labels must use **translation keys** (i18n-ready).
    
    ---
    
    ## **11. KPIs (for Admin / Founder)**
    
    - % of users with:
        - Verified phone
        - Completed personal details
        - Set buying position (HH)
        - Active integrations (Owner)
    - Services per Owner per listing
    - Surveys purchased per Home-Hunter
    - Correlation:
        - Profile completeness → Offer acceptance
        - Survey purchases → Offer conversions
    
    ---
    
    ## **12. Permission Logic (Summary Table)**
    
    | **Area** | **Guest** | **Home-Hunter** | **Owner** | **Admin** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

    | HH documents & surveys | ✖ | ✔ | ✖ | ✔ |

- Wireframes (Owner, Home-hunter, Admin, Public)
    
    This section contains all wireframes for the full NoAgent product. To keep this structured and easy to navigate. We have four **groups**:
    
    Each group includes:, Purpose summary (Why these pages exist), **UX journey explanation**, Low-fidelity wireframes (Dashfolio+ structure), Dummy Text
    
    - **🧩 WF O1- 4 +1 Wireframes & UX (Owner)** (selling / renting a place)
        - Global Summary
            1. **OWNER GLOBAL SUMMARY(short, 1-page)**
            2. **Extended Full Specification (for internal documentation + engineering)**
            
            ---
            
            ## **OWNER GLOBAL SUMMARY (Short Version, 1 Page)**
            
            ### **1. OWNER SIDEBAR (Final Frozen Structure)**
            
            ```
            OWNER WORKSPACE (Private)
              • Dashboard
              • My Places (Listings)
              • Inquiries
              • Calendar
              • Documents (Auto-sync from listings)
            
            PUBLIC LINKS (Public)
              • Your Public Property Page(s)
              • Services & Pricing
              • About Yalla.House
            
            ACCOUNT (top of sidebar)
              • Account Settings
              • Billing & Subscription
              • Log Out
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ### **2. END-TO-END OWNER JOURNEY**
            
            **Step 0 — Arrives via homepage → “List Your Place”**
            
            → If not logged in: Login/Signup → taken to WF-O2 Wizard.
            
            **Step 1 — Creates Draft (WF-O2)**
            
            Postcode → Address → Sale/Rent → Price → Photos (optional) → Publish.
            
            **Step 2 — Dashboard (WF-O1)**
            
            They see:
            
            - Views / Inquiries / Bookings
            - Lead sources (Rightmove / Yalla / WhatsApp / Signboard QR)
            - Next viewings
            - Messages waiting
            - Performance insights (“Your place is 20% above average views”)
            
            **Step 3 — Bookings (WF-O4)**
            
            Owner sets availability:
            
            - Group viewing windows
            - Private windows
                
                Auto-confirm ON by default.
                
            
            **Step 4 — Inquiries (WF-O3)**
            
            Messaging hub → reply, send quick replies, see HH profile preview.
            
            **Step 5 — Public Page (WF-O5)**
            
            Live listing, map, description, floorplans, calendar, message form.
            
            **Step 6 — Manage listing**
            
            Update price, status, media, documents.
            
            ---
            
            ### **3. OWNER WIREFRAME SET (WF-O1 → WF-O5)**
            
            - **WF-O1 — Dashboard**
                
                KPIs, lead sources, top actions, quick stats, upcoming viewings.
                
            - **WF-O2 — My Places**
                
                Listing table + First-Time Wizard (Basics → Price → Extras → Publish).
                
            - **WF-O3 — Inquiries**
                
                Inbox + Thread View + HH verified info + Viewing link.
                
            - **WF-O4 — Calendar**
                
                Availability editor + auto-confirm logic + reschedule rules.
                
            - **WF-O5 — Public Property Page**
                
                Public-facing page with CTA: Book Viewing / Message Owner.
                
            
            ---
            
            ### **4. OWNER DATA MODEL (Short)**
            
            **Place Table**
            
            - placeID
            - ownerID
            - address, postcode, geo
            - sale/rent
            - price/rent/month
            - beds, baths, size_sqm, size_sqft
            - description
            - photos[]
            - floorplan
            - EPC
            - status: draft/live/under_offer/sold/rented
            - lead_sources: counts
            - calendar_slots[]
            - createdAt / updatedAt
            
            **Inquiry Table**
            
            - inquiryID
            - placeID
            - ownerID
            - hunterID
            - message thread
            - status
            
            **Viewings Table**
            
            - viewingID
            - placeID
            - hunterID
            - ownerID
            - slot
            - status (auto-confirmed, cancelled, rescheduled)
            
            ---
            
            ### **5. KPI MODEL (Short)**
            
            - Views (total + 7d)
            - Inquiries
            - Bookings
            - Show-ups (later)
            - Offer rate (Phase 2)
            - Lead sources
            - Conversion funnel
            
            ---
            
            ### **6. CROSS-CONNECTIONS**
            
            WF-O1 pulls from:
            
            - Place views (O5 tracking)
            - Inquiry threads (O3)
            - Calendar bookings (O4)
            - Offer data (Phase 2, not MVP)
            
            WF-O5 feeds:
            
            - Views
            - Lead source tracking
            - Inquiries
            - Bookings
            
            ---
            
            # **EXTENDED FULL SPECIFICATION (DETAILED)**
            
            Below is the **complete internal Owner Global Summary**
            
            ---
            
            # **1. OWNER SIDEBAR (Final — MVP + Future Safe)**
            
            ### **Logged-in version (Owner)**
            
            ```
            ──────────────────────────
            PROFILE AREA (top, small)
              • Profile & Settings
              • Billing & Subscription
              • Log Out
            ──────────────────────────
            
            OWNER WORKSPACE (Private)
              → Dashboard
              → My Places
              → Inquiries
              → Calendar
              → Documents
            
            PUBLIC LINKS (Public)
              → Public Property Page(s)
              → Services & Pricing
              → About
            
            ──────────────────────────
            NoAgent BRAND (Footer of sidebar)
            ──────────────────────────
            ```
            
            ### **Logged-out version (Visitor / Home-Hunter)**
            
            ```
            ──────────────────────────
            LOGIN / SIGN UP
            ──────────────────────────
            Find a Place (Search)   (Phase 2)
            ──────────────────────────
            About
            Services & Pricing
            ──────────────────────────
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **2. OWNER USER JOURNEY (Extended)**
            
            ### **Stage 1 — Discovery**
            
            - Arrives from Google, ads, Rightmove, friend referral.
            - Sees Header CTA “List Your Place”.
            
            ### **Stage 2 — Sign-up**
            
            - Email + phone verification
            - Landed on WF-O2 (no listings yet).
            
            ### **Stage 3 — First-Time Listing Wizard (WF-O2)**
            
            1. Basics (Address, type)
            2. Price (Sale / Rent)
            3. Extras (optional)
            4. Ready → Publish
            
            ### **Stage 4 — Dashboard (WF-O1)**
            
            - High-level KPIs
            - Guidance messages
            - How many people saw your place
            - Where views came from
            - Next upcoming viewing
            
            ### **Stage 5 — Calendar (WF-O4)**
            
            - Set availability
            - Private or group slots
            - Auto-confirm default
            
            ### **Stage 6 — Inquiries (WF-O3)**
            
            - HH messages
            - Quick replies
            - Verified info shown if HH verified
            
            ### **Stage 7 — Public Page (WF-O5)**
            
            - Listings live
            - Book viewings available
            - HH can message owner
            
            ### **Stage 8 — Lifecycle**
            
            - Price adjustments
            - Media improvements
            - Managing offers (Phase 2)
            - Mark sold/let
            
            ---
            
            # **3. WIREFRAME SET (WF-O1 → WF-O5)**
            
            (Already created individually; here is the consolidated spec.)
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-O1 — Dashboard**
            
            ### **(Owner Command Center)**
            
            - KPIs
            - Traffic sources
            - Next viewing
            - Messages waiting
            - Listing performance
            - Tips (“Add photos for +40% engagement”)
            - Link to My Places
            
            **Developer Notes:**
            
            Uses joined tables: place → viewings → inquiries → tracking logs.
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-O2 — My Places**
            
            Listing table, create/edit listings, First-Time Wizard.
            
            **Developer Notes:**
            
            Needs placeID, status logic, document linking, price formatting, address lookup.
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-O3 — Inquiries**
            
            Inbox + thread, buyer details, quick replies.
            
            **Developer Notes:**
            
            Real-time or polling updates, message log, read/unread flags.
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-O4 — Calendar**
            
            Availability editor, viewing list, auto-confirm logic.
            
            **Developer Notes:**
            
            Calendar slots array, timezone, ICS/Google Calendar sync.
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-O5 — Public Property Page**
            
            Photos, description, floorplan, map, CTA to book, CTA to message.
            
            **Developer Notes:**
            
            Tracking events, dynamic rendering, SEO tags.
            
            ---
            
            # **4. OWNER DATA MODEL (Extended)**
            
            Here is the full data model you can paste into Notion or Airtable.
            
            ---
            
            ### **TABLE: Owners**
            
            - ownerID (PK)
            - fname, lname
            - email
            - phone
            - isVerified
            - country
            - subscriptionTier
            - createdAt, updatedAt
            
            ---
            
            ### **TABLE: Places**
            
            - placeID (PK)
            - ownerID (FK)
            - address, postcode
            - lat, lng
            - saleOrRent
            - price
            - rentPerMonth
            - currency
            - tenure
            - beds
            - baths
            - sizeSqm
            - sizeSqft
            - description
            - status
            - photos[]
            - floorplanFile
            - epcFile
            - createdAt
            - updatedAt
            
            ---
            
            ### **TABLE: Viewings**
            
            - viewingID
            - placeID
            - ownerID
            - hunterID
            - slotStart
            - slotEnd
            - type: group/private
            - status: confirmed/cancelled/rescheduled
            
            ---
            
            ### **TABLE: Inquiries**
            
            - inquiryID
            - threadID
            - placeID
            - ownerID
            - hunterID
            - message[]
            - status
            - createdAt
            
            ---
            
            ### **TABLE: TrackingEvents**
            
            - eventID
            - placeID
            - hunterID
            - eventType: view / click / mapOpen / bookCTA / messageCTA / QRscan
            - timestamp
            - source: rightmove / yalla / whatsapp / signboard / unknown
            
            ---
            
            # **5. OFFER HANDLING (Phase 2, but pre-framed)**
            
            **Owner sees:**
            
            - Offers list
            - Amount
            - Buyer verified? (Yes/No)
            - Financial position (cash / mortgage ready / in progress)
            
            **Dev:**
            
            Needs offer table + status transitions.
            
            ---
            
            # **6. CALENDAR LOGIC (OWNER-SIDE)**
            
            **Owner sets slots:**
            
            - Private: 1 HH
            - Group: unlimited HH
            - Auto-confirm: ON by default
            
            **HH booking experience:**
            
            Instant confirmation
            
            → Unless owner manually reschedules.
            
            ---
            
            # **7. MESSAGING LOGIC**
            
            - Internal HH ↔ Owner messaging
            - “Send Quick Reply”
            - Expands to support attachments later
            - Status changes (inquiry → viewing → follow-up)
            
            ---
            
            # **8. DEPENDENCIES**
            
            - Stripe (billing)
            - Twilio WhatsApp (inquiries + confirmations)
            - Google Calendar (owner + HH sync)
            - Rightmove feed (Phase 2)
            - Airtable backend (MVP)
            - Framer frontend (MVP)
            
            ---
            
        
        ```jsx
         OWNER PROFILE (Separate Right-Top Menu, NOT in Sidebar)
            Account Settings - Billing & Subscription Log Out   
        
        SIDEBAR - OWNER WORKSPACE
        │
        ├── O1. Dashboard
        │     ├── KPI Overview
        │     ├── Funnel (Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Offers → Deal)
        │     ├── Active Listings Snapshot
        │     ├── Recent Activity (Inquiry, Viewing, Offer)
        │     └── Quick Actions (Manage Listings, Calendar)
        │
        ├── O2. My Listings
        │     ├── Listings Table (Thumbnail / Status / Price / Views)
        │     ├── Create New Listing (First-Time Wizard)
        │     │      ├── Step 1 — Basics (Address, Type)
        │     │      ├── Step 2 — Price (Sale or Rent)
        │     │      ├── Step 3 — Extras (Photos, Beds/Baths)
        │     │      └── Step 4 — Ready to Publish
        │     └── Manage Listing
        │            ├── Details Tab
        │            ├── Photos & Media Tab
        │            ├── Documents Tab (EPC, Floorplan, Ownership)
        │            └── Publication Status (Draft / Live / Under Offer / Sold)
        │
        ├── O3. Inquiries & Offers (Messaging Hub)
        │     ├── Inbox (3) (New / Replied / Offers / Archived)
        │     ├── Conversation View
        │     ├── Buyer Profile Overview (Verification level)
        │     ├── Offer Comparison Table
        │     └── Integrated messaging + attachments
        │
        ├── O4. Calendar (Viewings Manager)
        │     ├── Upcoming Viewings
        │     ├── Past Viewings
        │     ├── Group Viewing Slots (multiple attendees)
        │     ├── Private Viewing Slots
        │     ├── Add / Edit timeslots
        │     ├── Calendar Sync (Google)
        │     └── Directions & visitor notes
        │
        └── O5. Public Property Page (Preview + Visitor Page)
               ├── Photo Carousel
               ├── Key Facts (Price, Beds, Size)
               ├── Description
               ├── Floorplan & Docs (public-only)
               ├── Map & StreetView
               ├── “Arrange a Visit” Calendar CTA
               ├── “Message Owner” CTA
               ├── Survey Marketplace (if available)
               └── SEO: area info, history, tags
            
            (Sidebar background = Dashfolio dark)        │
        │  (Hover state = Yalla Yellow #F8D22A)  
        ```
        
        - **🧩 WF-O1 — Owner Dashboard (Command Center)**
            
            > One clean page that shows: performance, buyer quality, viewing pipeline, and actions.
            > 
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **1. Designer Checklist**
            > 
            > - Keep Dashfolio+ layout: header (fixed), sidebar (owner version), dark theme, Yalla Yellow accents.
            > - Dashboard = modular grid with **4 KPI cards**, **2 charts**, **2 list widgets**.
            > - Buyer chips: *Verified*, *Cash*, *Mortgage Ready*, or rental equivalents *Employment Ready / Student / Guarantor Ready*.
            > - Separate Sale vs Rent visually only by **green/blue chip**.
            > - Show icons for Inbox, WhatsApp, Viewing.
            > - Mobile → simple stacked layout.
            > - Include CTA buttons: “Add New Place”, “Manage Listings”, “View Calendar”.
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **2. Developer Checklist**
            > 
            > - Compute KPIs via backend (no client-side math).
            > - Include **inquiry aggregation**:
            >     
            >     totalInquiries, verifiedInquiries, whatsappOnlyInquiries.
            >     
            > - Include funnel counts:
            >     - Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Offers/Applications → Converted.
            > - Include rental funnel when propertyType = “rent”.
            > - Pass arrays for charts in compact form.
            > - Provide recentActivity[] sorted descending.
            > - Include availability for *Open House windows* (WF-O4).
            > - Fire events: dashboard_loaded, widget_clicked, chart_viewed.
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **3. Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
            > 
            > 1. Owner logs in → Dashboard opens immediately.
            > 2. Sees at a glance:
            >     - How many people looked
            >     - How many contacted
            >     - How many verified
            >     - Viewings booked
            >     - Offers/Applications
            > 3. Checks recent activity.
            > 4. Moves to inquiries or calendar depending on need.
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
            > 
            > **Entry from:**
            > 
            > - Sidebar
            > - Header “List your Place” (after 1st property)
            > - WF-O2 (after saving listing)
            > - After booking confirmation emails (optional)
            > 
            > **Exit to:**
            > 
            > - WF-O2 (manage listings)
            > - WF-O3 (inquiries)
            > - WF-O4 (calendar)
            > - WF-ACC (account)
            > 
            > Dashboard = **daily home base**.
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **5. Purpose**
            > 
            > To give the Owner **100% clarity** on the status of their sale/rental.
            > 
            > To highlight **buyer quality** (verification + buying/renting position).
            > 
            > To make next actions obvious (reply, schedule viewings, adjust listing).
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            > 
            > - “Is my listing performing well?”
            > - “Are buyers verified?”
            > - “Where are the viewings coming from?”
            > - “How many people contacted me?”
            > - “Do I need to reply to anyone?”
            > - **Rental version:** “How many applications do I have?”
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **7. Components the Designer Must Build**
            > 
            > ## **7.1 KPI Row (4 Cards)**
            > 
            > 1. **Total Views (7 days)**
            > 2. **Inquiries (verified vs total)**
            > 3. **Viewings (upcoming + completed)**
            > 4. **Offers / Applications**
            >     - Sale = Offers
            >     - Rent = Applications
            > 
            > Each card has:
            > 
            > - Large number
            > - Subtext
            > - Tiny trend arrow (+X% vs last week)
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ## **7.2 Funnel Chart (Sale or Rent Auto-Switch)**
            > 
            > Sale Version:
            > 
            > Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Offers → Accepted Offer
            > 
            > Rent Version:
            > 
            > Views → Inquiries → Viewings → Applications → Approved
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ## **7.3 Source Breakdown Pie Chart**
            > 
            > Sources:
            > 
            > - Yalla.House
            > - Rightmove
            > - Zoopla
            > - WhatsApp
            > - QR Code Signboard
            > - Direct Share (Messenger/SMS)
            > - “Unknown” fallback
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ## **7.4 Recent Activity Feed**
            > 
            > Items include:
            > 
            > - “New verified inquiry from Sarah L. (Cash Buyer)”
            > - “3 WhatsApp contacts yesterday”
            > - “Viewing scheduled by Omar (Sat 11am)”
            > - “Offer submitted: £612,500 (awaiting reply)”
            > - Rental equivalent: “Application received from Jessica K. (Employment verified)”
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ## **7.5 Quick Actions**
            > 
            > - Add New Place
            > - Manage Listings
            > - View Calendar
            > - Get More Views (upgrade upsell—Phase 2)
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **8. Developer Requirements (Deep)**
            > 
            > ### **8.1 API response shape**
            > 
            > ```
            > OwnerDashboardData {
            >   kpis: {
            >     totalViews7d: number
            >     inquiries: number
            >     verifiedInquiries: number
            >     whatsappOnly: number
            >     viewingsUpcoming: number
            >     viewingsCompleted: number
            >     offers: number // sale only
            >     applications: number // rent only
            >   }
            > 
            >   funnel: {
            >     views: number
            >     inquiries: number
            >     viewings: number
            >     offersOrApplications: number
            >     converted: number
            >   }
            > 
            >   sources: {
            >     rightmove: number
            >     zoopla: number
            >     yalla: number
            >     whatsapp: number
            >     qrcode: number
            >     direct: number
            >     unknown: number
            >   }
            > 
            >   recentActivity: ActivityEvent[]
            > }
            > ```
            > 
            > ### **8.2 ActivityEvent schema**
            > 
            > ```
            > ActivityEvent {
            >   id: string
            >   type: "inquiry" | "viewing" | "offer" | "application" | "whatsapp" | "system"
            >   timestamp: number
            >   title: string
            >   meta?: Record<string, any>
            > }
            > ```
            > 
            > ### **8.3 Logic**
            > 
            > - Funnel auto-switches to Rent version if listing is rent.
            > - If multiple listings exist → aggregate across all.
            > - If Owner has 0 listings → show onboarding tile instead of KPIs.
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **9. KPI Definitions**
            > 
            > Clear and developer-safe:
            > 
            > | **KPI** | **Definition** |
            > | --- | --- |
            > | Views | Sum of property page loads (unique optional) |
            > | Inquiries | All inquiries from inbox + WhatsApp (timestamp only for WhatsApp) |
            > | Verified Inquiries | Buyer passed phone verification |
            > | Viewings | Confirmed viewing events (private + open house) |
            > | Offers | Sale: number of submitted offers |
            > | Applications | Rent: number of applications |
            > | Converted | Offers accepted OR rental application approved |
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **10. Funnel Logic (With Numbers + %)**
            > 
            > Examples the system should compute:
            > 
            > - Inquiry Rate = Inquiries ÷ Views
            > - Viewing Rate = Viewings ÷ Inquiries
            > - Offer Rate = Offers ÷ Viewings
            > - Conversion Rate = Converted ÷ Offers
            > 
            > Rental version uses Applications instead of Offers.
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **11. Rental Logic (Integrated)**
            > 
            > - KPI #4 switches from **Offers → Applications**.
            > - Funnel switches to **Applications → Approved**.
            > - Recent activity includes “Rental Application Received”.
            > - Renter position chips appear in activity.
            > - Viewing logic identical.
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > # **12. Dummy Content (Design Mock)**
            > 
            > ### **KPIs**
            > 
            > - Views: **1,247** (↑ 18%)
            > - Inquiries: **36** (22 verified)
            > - Viewings: **4 upcoming**
            > - Offers: **1 active**
            > 
            > Rental version:
            > 
            > - Applications: **3**
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ### **Funnel (Sale Example)**
            > 
            > - 4,562 Views
            > - 123 Inquiries
            > - 17 Viewings
            > - 3 Offers
            > - 1 Accepted
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ### **Funnel (Rent Example)**
            > 
            > - 4,112 Views
            > - 98 Inquiries
            > - 14 Viewings
            > - 4 Applications
            > - 2 Approved
            > 
            > ---
            > 
            > ### **Recent Activity**
            > 
            > - “New inquiry from **Sarah L. (Verified, Cash Buyer)**”
            > - “**WhatsApp contact** from 07:44 today (no inbox messages)”
            > - “Viewing booked by **Omar R.** — Sat 9 Nov at 12:00”
            > - “**Offer submitted** £612,500”
            > 
            > Rental version example:
            > 
            > - “**Application received** — Jessica K. (Employment Verified)”
            > 
            > ---
            >

        - **🧩 WF-O2 — My Listings (Owner Workspace)**
            
            ---
            
            > The Owner’s central table to manage all properties + access all listing-level tools.
            > 
            
            ---
            
            # **1. Purpose**
            
            This page must allow an Owner to:
            
            - See all their listings (Sale + Rent)
            - Continue setup (for Drafts)
            - Manage details + media + pricing
            - See performance at a glance
            - Enter the funnel (O3 Inquiries → O4 Calendar → O5 Public Page)
            - Quickly identify **buyer quality** indicators (Cash, Verified, Apps, Offers)
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Page Entry Points**
            
            Owner reaches this page from:
            
            - Sidebar → “My Listings”
            - O1 Dashboard → “Manage Listings”
            - After creating first Draft from the Wizard (WF-O2-Setup)
            - After uploading photos, adding price, etc.
            
            ---
            
            # **3. Page Structure (Designer Layout)**
            
            Use existing **Dashfolio+ table layout**, dark mode, Yalla Yellow accents.
            
            ### **3.1 Table Columns**
            
            | **Column** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | **Thumbnail** | First image or placeholder. |
            | **Address / Title** | “12 King Street, London E2” (click → WF-O2-Detail). |
            | **Type** | Sale / Rent. |
            | **Status** | Draft / Live / Under Offer / Sold / Let Agreed / Rented. |
            | **Price** | Price (Sale) / Rent per month (Rent). |
            | **Buyer Demand** | Mini chips (e.g., 12 inquiries / 7 verified). |
            | **Viewings** | Upcoming + completed. |
            | **Offers/Apps** | Sale: Offers count; Rent: Applications count. |
            | **Source Mix** | Small 3-dot pie preview (Yalla/Rightmove/WhatsApp). |
            | **Actions** | “Continue Setup”, “Manage”, “Preview”. |
            
            ---
            
            # **4. Row Logic**
            
            ### **4.1 DRAFT**
            
            Show yellow “Draft” tag + big button:
            
            ➡ **Continue Setup** (WF-O2-Setup: Price → Photos → Extras → Publish)
            
            ### **4.2 LIVE (SALE)**
            
            “Manage” opens tabs:
            
            - Details
            - Photos
            - Price
            - Documents
            - Inquiries (filtered list from O3)
            - Viewings
            - Offers
            
            ### **4.3 LIVE (RENT)**
            
            Tabs include:
            
            - Details
            - Photos
            - Rent
            - Documents
            - Inquiries
            - Viewings
            - **Applications**
            - Tenant Requirements (employment, guarantor, etc.)
            
            ---

            Designer: small button cluster.
            
            - **Add New Place**
            - **View Dashboard (O1)**
            
            ---

            Large welcoming card:
            
            🏡 *“Let’s list your first place!”*
            
            → Button: **Start a New Listing**
            
            ---
            
            # **7. Expanded Row Preview (Optional for Phase 2)**

            - Views 7d
            - 3 most recent inquiries
            - Next viewing
            - 1 active offer/application
            
            (**NOT required for MVP.**)
            
            ---
            
            # **8. Filters + Sorting (MVP)**
            
            ### **Filters:**
            
            - All / Sale / Rent
            - Status: Draft, Live, Under Offer, Sold, Let Agreed
            - Has Offers / Has Applications
            - Verified Buyer Activity
            
            ### **Sorting:**
            
            - By newest
            - By most inquiries
            - By most viewings
            - By offers/applications
            
            ---
            
            # **9. Updated Data Model (Owner Listings Table)**
            
            Additions include rental logic + buyer verification.
            
            ```
            Listing {
              id: string
              ownerId: string
            
              address: string
              postcode: string
              lat: number
              lng: number
            
              listingType: "sale" | "rent"
              status: "draft" | "live" | "under_offer" | "sold" | "let_agreed" | "rented"
            
              price: number                // sale
              rentPerMonth?: number        // rent
              deposit?: number             // rent
              tenancyMinMonths?: number    // rent
            
              photos: string[]
              documents: string[]
            
              stats: {
                views7d: number
                inquiries: number
                verifiedInquiries: number
                whatsappInquiries: number
                viewings: number
                offers: number
                applications: number // rent
              }
            
              sources: {
                yalla: number
                rightmove: number
                zoopla: number
                whatsapp: number
                qrcode: number
                direct: number
                unknown: number
              }
            
              createdAt: number
              updatedAt: number
            }
            ```

            # **10. Updated Buyer/Renter Summary Chips**
            
            Displayed per row:
            
            - **Verified**: (✓ Verified)
            - **Cash Buyer**
            - **Mortgage Ready**
            - **Employment Verified (Rent)**
            - **Guarantor Ready (Rent)**

            # **12. Developer Implementation Notes**
            
            - Must aggregate all inquiries + WhatsApp pings + funnel events via listingId.
            - Must support **sale** vs **rent** display logic.
            - Tab counts come from queries:
                - offersCount
                - applicationsCount
                - upcomingViewingsCount
            - Action buttons fire events:
                - listing_viewed
                - listing_manage_clicked
                - listing_preview_clicked
            - Image uploads via CDN (placeholder for MVP).
            - Source mix uses system tracking (UTM + referrer + QR unique ID).
