            ---
            
        - **🧩 WF-O3 — Inquiries (Owner Messaging Hub)**
            
            **Owner’s central place**
            
            > inquiries, messages, WhatsApp handoffs, viewings context, and
            > 
            > 
            > *buyer verification info*
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ## **1. Designer Checklist**
            
            - Use **Owner sidebar** (Dashboard / My Listings / Inquiries / Calendar / Documents / Settings).
            - Two-panel layout (desktop):
                - Left: **Inquiries list**
                - Right: **Conversation / details panel**
            - Show **per-inquiry badges**:
                - Buyer name
                - Property (short address)
                - **Verified badge** (if buyer passed gate)
                - Buying position (Cash / Mortgage ready / etc.)
                - Last contact channel icon (Inbox / WhatsApp / Viewing)
                - Unread bubble (if any)
            - Add **filters**:
                - All / New / Replied / Viewings / Offers / Archived
                - Filter by **Verified only**
            - In conversation view, show:
                - Buyer header (name + verified + buying position)
                - Property summary
                - Message thread (Yalla inbox only)
                - Side panel with key info (phone, email, last viewing, last WhatsApp contact)
                - Buttons: “Reply”, “Propose viewing time”, “Mark as resolved”
            - State for buyers who only contacted via WhatsApp:
                - No inbox messages, but banner: “This buyer contacted via WhatsApp — conversation not stored.”
            - Mobile: single-column, list → tap → slide-over conversation.
            
            ---
            
            ## **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            - Update **Inquiries list endpoint** to include:
                - Buyer name
                - Buyer phoneVerified (boolean)
                - Buyer buyingPosition
                - lastChannel (inbox / whatsapp / viewing)
                - unreadCount
            - Ensure every Inquiry row **links to**:
                - HomeHunter (buyer)
                - Property
                - Messages (if inbox used)
                - Viewings (if any)
            - Fire analytics events:
                - owner_opened_inquiry
                - owner_replied_inquiry
                - owner_marked_inquiry_resolved
            - Respect HomeHunter.phoneVerified — don’t show “Verified” if false.
            - Support filter: ?verifiedOnly=true.
            
            ---
            
            ## **3. Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            1. Owner logs in → clicks **Inquiries**.
            2. Sees **all incoming interest** per listing, sorted by **newest activity**.
            3. Can quickly scan:
                - Who is verified
                - Who is cash / mortgage ready
                - Who came via WhatsApp vs inbox
                - Who has booked a viewing
            4. Clicks an inquiry → sees:
                - Conversation thread (if any)
                - Buyer context (verification + status)
                - Viewings linked
            5. Can reply, propose a time, or mark enquiry as done.
            
            ---
            
            ## **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
            
            **Entry points:**
            
            - From Dashboard (“New inquiries” widget → “View all”)
            - From My Listings (click “View inquiries” for a specific place)
            - From Calendar (click on viewing → “Open inquiry”)
            - From notification badge in sidebar (Inquiries (3))
            
            **Exit points:**
            
            - To Calendar (when proposing viewings)
            - To My Listings (if Owner wants to edit price or description)
            - To Buyer detail (Admin in future – but for Owner, just buyer summary panel)
            
            WF-O3 is the **daily-use screen** for Owners.
            
            ---
            
            ## **5. Purpose**
            
            - Give Owners a **clean, actionable overview** of interest.
            - Show **buyer quality at a glance** (verified + buying position).
            - Clarify which channel is used: Yalla inbox vs WhatsApp vs direct viewing.
            - Connect messaging with **calendar and offers**.
            - Reduce noise, increase trust.
            
            ---
            
            ## **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            For Owners:
            
            - “Who’s serious vs browsing?”
            - “Have I already replied?”
            - “Did this person book a viewing yet?”
            - “Did they contact via WhatsApp as well?”
            
            For the system:
            
            - Central place to manage **all** interest events.
            - Fully compatible with the **buyer gate**: only verified buyers appear here.
            
            ---
            
            ## **7. Layout Outline (Desktop)**
            
            ### **7.1 Left Panel — Inquiries List**
            
            **Top bar:**
            
            - Title: Inquiries
            - Filter pills:
                - All
                - New
                - Replied
                - Viewings
                - Offers
                - Archived
                - **Verified only** (toggle)
            
            **Search:**
            
            - Search by buyer name, email, or property address.
            
            **List row (each inquiry):**
            
            - Buyer Name: Alex Turner
            - Badges:
                - Verified (green tick) if phoneVerified === true
                - Cash, Mortgage ready, etc.
            - Secondary line:
                
                “Interested in 12 King Street” – 2 days ago
                
            - Icons:
                - Inbox bubble (if in-app messages exist)
                - WhatsApp logo (if WhatsApp contact triggered)
                - Calendar icon (if viewing scheduled)
            - Right side:
                - New / Replied
                - Unread count (e.g. 3)
            
            Click row → open Conversation Panel.
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.2 Right Panel — Conversation & Details**
            
            **Header:**
            
            - Buyer Name + Verified chip if true
            - Buying Position (chip)
            - Small line: Enquiry for 12 King Street (For Sale)
            
            **Info strip:**
            
            - Phone (obfuscated): +44 •••• 1234
            - Email: alex@example.com
            - Last contact: Inbox / WhatsApp / Viewing only
            - Last activity: 3 hours ago
            
            **Body area:**
            
            - **Case 1 — Inbox conversation exists**
                
                Chat-style thread:
                
                - Owner messages (aligned right)
                - Buyer messages (left)
                - Date dividers
                - At top, small note:
                    
                    Some contact may also happen via WhatsApp. Only Yalla messages are shown here.
                    
                
                At bottom:
                
                - Reply box (textarea)
                - Actions:
                    - Send reply (primary)
                    - Propose viewing slot (opens calendar selector)
                    - Mark as resolved (changes status)
            - **Case 2 — WhatsApp-only contact**
                - Empty thread area with message:
                    
                    > “This buyer contacted you via WhatsApp.
                    > 
                    
                    > We don’t store the conversation, but you can see their profile and viewing history.”
                    > 
                - Show buttons:
                    - Log note (Owner adds manual note)
                    - Mark as contacted / Resolved
            - **Case 3 — Viewing passed**
                - Above thread, small banner:
                    
                    > “Viewing on 12 Oct at 11:30 — Completed.
                    > 
                    
                    > Add notes or update this buyer’s status.”
                    > 
            
            ---
            
            ## **8. Developer Requirements (Logic)**
            
            ### **8.1 Inquiry Data to Fetch**
            
            Each inquiry row needs:
            
            ```
            InquiryListItem {
              id: string
              propertyId: string
              buyerId: string
            
              buyerName: string
              buyerBuyingPosition: "cash" | "mortgage_ready" | "mortgage_in_progress" | "just_browsing"
              buyerPhoneVerified: boolean
            
              propertyTitle: string // e.g. "12 King Street"
              propertyType: "sale" | "rent"
            
              lastChannel: "inbox" | "whatsapp" | "viewing"
              lastActivityAt: timestamp
              status: "new" | "replied" | "viewing" | "offer" | "archived"
              unreadCount: number
            }
            ```
            
            ### **8.2 Messages**
            
            ```
            InquiryMessage {
              id: string
              inquiryId: string
              sender: "owner" | "buyer" | "system"
              channel: "inbox"
              body: string
              createdAt: timestamp
              readAt?: timestamp
            }
            ```
            
            WhatsApp is **not** stored, but:
            
            - We log lastChannel = "whatsapp"
            - We may store lastWhatsappAt: timestamp (optional)
            
            > Data model change (note):
            > 
            
            > Inquiry now has lastChannel and buyerBuyingPosition and buyerPhoneVerified in the list DTO (read-model). Backend can derive them from HomeHunter.
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ## **9. Funnel & Events (Integration with H1 Gate)**
            
            - Every inquiry **must be linked** to a verified buyer (gate ensures that).
            - Events:
                - owner_opened_inquiry
                - owner_replied_inquiry
                - owner_opened_whatsapp_only_inquiry
                - owner_marked_inquiry_resolved
            
            These feed into **Admin Analytics (A9)**.
            
            ---
            
            ## **10. Dummy Content (for Design Mock)**
            
            **List example rows:**
            
            1. 
                - Sarah L. · Verified · Cash
                - “12 King Street”
                - New · Inbox · 2 unread
            2. 
                - Omar R. · Verified · Mortgage ready
                - “45 Oak Road”
                - Viewing booked · WhatsApp icon
            3. 
                - Jade W. · Just browsing
                - “7 Maple Avenue”
                - Replied · No unread
            
            ---
            
            If you like, next we can:
            
            - Update **Owner Dashboard (O1)** KPI cards to show:
                - Verified vs unverified buyers
                - Funnel conversion per listing
            - Or adjust **Admin A2/A3** to surface buyer verification flags more prominently.
            
            ---
            
            ## **11. Rental Logic (Fully Supported)**
            
            WF-O3 works for **Sale** *and* **Rent** listings with NO separate screens needed.
            
            The UI and data model already adapt perfectly when the listing is for rent.
            
            ### **1. Inquiry Source (Rent vs Sale)**
            
            - Each inquiry row includes propertyType: "rent" or "sale".
            - The chip next to the property name becomes:
                - **“For Rent”** (green/blue chip)
                - **“For Sale”** (default chip)
            
            ### **2. Buyer Fields adapt to Rental Terms**
            
            For rentals, buyer attributes become:
            
            - RentingPosition instead of BuyingPosition:
                - ✔️ “Employed — Docs Ready”
                - ✔️ “Student — Guarantor Ready”
                - ✔️ “Self-employed — Docs Ready”
                - ✔️ “Just browsing”
            
            These appear exactly like Sale chips (same UI).
            
            ### **3. Verification Gate works the same**
            
            Renters must still verify their phone number before they can send an inquiry.
            
            ### **4. Communication flow identical**
            
            Owners for rental listings see the exact same:
            
            - Inquiry list
            - Inbox conversations
            - WhatsApp-only notices
            - Viewings scheduling logic
            
            No structure changes required.
            
            ### **5. Viewings identical**
            
            A rental viewing is handled the same as a sale viewing.
            
            ### **6. Offers tab becomes “Applications”**
            
            Owner sidebar already supports this under WF-O3 filters:
            
            - Offers → for Sale
            - Applications → for Rent
            
            Same screen, different label (automatic).
            
            ### **7. Dummy Content (Rental Examples)**
            
            **Rental Inquiry row:**
            
            - Jessica K. · Verified · Employed (Docs Ready)
            - “Flat — 14 Baker Street · For Rent”
            - New · Inbox · 1 unread
            
            **Rental conversation header:**
            
            - Applicant type: Employed
            - Income verified? — Not yet
            - Guarantor needed? — Unknown
            
            ---
            
            ---
            
        - **🧩 WF-O4 — Calendar (Owner Viewings Manager)**
            
            > WF-O4 is the Owner’s viewing manager — an integrated calendar for private viewings and open houses, with filters, event details, and links to messages and listings.
            > 
            
            Alright, let’s tune **WF-O4** so it matches the new rule:
            
            > If a slot exists and is bookable, a Home-Hunter booking is automatically confirmed.
            > 
            
            > Owner only *reschedules cancels*
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ## **1. Designer Checklist**
            
            - Dashfolio+ dark theme, Yalla Yellow for:
                - “Add Viewing Block” buttons
                - “Today” indicator
                - “Confirmed” badges
            - Two main components:
                - **Calendar view** (Week/Month)
                - **Selected day list** of slots and bookings
            - Clearly distinguish:
                - **Open-house block** (multi-buyer)
                - **Private viewing** (one buyer)
            - Visually indicate:
                - Slots with **confirmed bookings** (always auto-confirmed)
                - Slots that are **full**
                - **Cancelled** blocks
            - No UI element for “Approve / Confirm viewing”.
            
            ---
            
            ## **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            - Endpoints:
                - GET /owner/calendar?from=&to=
                - POST /owner/calendar/slots (create open-house or private slot)
                - PATCH /owner/calendar/slots/{slotID} (time change, cancel)
                - GET /owner/calendar/slots/{slotID}/bookings
            - Data structures:
                - viewing_slots:
                    - slotID, ownerID, placeID
                    - slotType: OPEN_HOUSE | PRIVATE
                    - startTime, endTime
                    - capacity (int, default 1 for PRIVATE)
                    - status: active, full, cancelled
                - viewing_bookings:
                    - bookingID, slotID, hunterID (nullable if manual)
                    - status: confirmed, cancelled, no_show, attended (later)
            - Booking logic:
                - When HH books a valid slot → create viewing_booking with status confirmed (auto).
                - If capacity reached (OPEN_HOUSE) → slot → full.
            - Optional: one-way sync to Google Calendar.
            
            ---
            
            ## **3. Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            Owner uses WF-O4 to:
            
            - See **all upcoming viewings** across all places
            - Publish **availability** (open houses + private slots)
            - Check **who is coming when**
            - Cancel or reschedule if needed
            
            Typical flows:
            
            - From Dashboard (O1) → “Viewings this week” → O4
            - From Inquiries (O3) → “View in Calendar” → O4 with correct day/slot focussed
            
            Owner never “approves” bookings — they’re already confirmed.
            
            ---
            
            ## **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
            
            ```
            Sidebar → Calendar (WF-O4)
                           ↓
                  Monthly / Weekly View
                           ↓
               Select Day → See All Slots
                           ↓
             Inspect bookings • Message • Cancel/Change
            ```
            
            WF-O4 ties into:
            
            - WF-H1 (bookings created here)
            - WF-O3 (threads show the system message)
            - WF-O1 (KPIs and funnel)
            
            ---
            
            ## **5. Purpose**
            
            - Give Owners a **clear, simple overview** of viewings.
            - Allow them to publish “when I’m available”.
            - Trust the system to auto-confirm bookings.
            - Avoid double-booking and confusion.
            
            ---
            
            ## **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - “What viewings do I have today / this week?”
            - “Who is coming and for which place?”
            - “Which slots are open-house, which are private?”
            - “Are any slots full or cancelled?”
            - “How do I cancel/change one?”
            
            ---
            
            ## **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
            
            ### **7.1 Top: Calendar Strip**
            
            - Toggle: **Week / Month**
            - Day cells with:
                - Date
                - Small counter: 3 viewings
                - Different marker if any slot is cancelled.
            
            Clicking a day → scrolls to / loads that day’s list.
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.2 Middle: Selected Day — Slot List**
            
            For each slot:
            
            **Open-house Slot Card**
            
            > 11:00–13:00 — 12 King Street (OPEN-HOUSE)
            > 
            
            > 5 confirmed · Capacity 10
            > 
            
            > Status: ✅ Active
            > 
            
            > [View Bookings] [Edit Slot] [Cancel Slot]
            > 
            
            **Private Slot Card**
            
            > 15:30–16:00 — 22 Yoxley Drive (PRIVATE)
            > 
            
            > 1 Home-Hunter · Status: ✅ Confirmed
            > 
            
            > [View Booking] [Message] [Cancel]
            > 
            
            Buttons at top of list:
            
            - **➕ Add Viewing Block**
                - Opens modal:
                    - Property (dropdown)
                    - Type: Open-house / Private
                    - Date & time
                    - Capacity (for open-house)
                    - Optional note: “Key at neighbour, please ring first”
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.3 Slot Detail Modal**
            
            Clicking “View Bookings / View Booking” opens a modal:
            
            For OPEN-HOUSE:
            
            - Property: address + thumbnail
            - Time range
            - Status: Active / Full / Cancelled
            - List of all bookings:
            
            | **Name** | **Buying Position** | **Status** | **Contact** |
            | --- | --- | --- | --- |
            | Sarah L. | Mortgage Ready | Confirmed | +44… |
            | Omar R. | Just Browsing | Confirmed | +44… |
            
            Actions:
            
            - **Message All** (opens WF-O3 thread, pre-filled)
            - **Cancel Entire Block** (sends messages to all HH)
            - **Mark as Completed** (Phase 2: for analytics)
            
            For PRIVATE:
            
            - Same, but only one Home-Hunter and buttons:
                - **Message Home-Hunter**
                - **Cancel Viewing**
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.4 Auto-Confirmation UX (Important)**
            
            On the UI, it must be obvious that:
            
            - Slots are “Availability I published”
            - Bookings are “People who took those times” and are **already confirmed**.
            
            For each booking line:
            
            > Status: ✅ Confirmed (auto)
            > 
            
            No “Confirm” buttons anywhere.
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.5 Google Calendar Note (small top-right block)**
            
            > Google Calendar
            > 
            
            > Connected ✅ (or “Not Connected ❌”)
            > 
            
            > “Events are pushed automatically for each slot.”
            > 
            
            (MVP: one-way push only.)
            
            ---
            
            ## **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            ### **Auto-confirmation Core Rule**
            
            - When POST /viewings/book is called and slot is valid:
                - Create viewing_booking with status = "confirmed".
                - Send confirmation to HH (WhatsApp + email).
                - Send calendar event to Owner.
                - Insert system message into inquiry_thread for that HH + placeID:
            
            > “Viewing booked and confirmed: [date/time] (Open-house / Private).”
            > 
            - Do **not** await Owner action.
            
            ### **Slot Safeguards**
            
            - PRIVATE: if confirmed booking exists → reject new bookings.
            - OPEN-HOUSE: bookings count must not exceed capacity.
            - If Owner cancels slot →
                - Set slot status = "cancelled"
                - Set all future bookings status = "cancelled"
                - Send cancellation messages to all affected HH.
            
            ---
            
            ## **9. KPI Definitions (Calendar)**
            
            WF-O4 drives:
            
            - Viewings per week
            - Private vs Open-house ratio
            - Average HH per open-house
            - Cancellation rate
            - Conversion from viewing → offer (later)
            
            These KPIs appear on WF-O1 & Admin analytics (A9), not as charts here.
            
            ---
            
            ## **10. Conversion Funnel (Calendar View)**
            
            ```
            Slot created (availability)
              ↓
            Booking auto-confirmed
              ↓
            Viewing attended (later tracking)
              ↓
            Offer / Application (Phase 2)
            ```
            
            WF-O4 handles the **Slot created → Booking confirmed** step.
            
            ---
            
            ## **11. ID Logic**
            
            Each crucial entity:
            
            - slotID (viewing_slots)
            - bookingID (viewing_bookings)
            - placeID
            - ownerID
            - hunterID
            
            WF-O4 must always load data using ownerID + date range.
            
            ---
            
            ## **12. Developer Tooling Overview**
            
            - Background jobs:
                - Reminder notifications (e.g. 24h before viewing)
                - Post-viewing follow-ups (Phase 2)
            - Integrations:
                - Google Calendar
                - Twilio (WhatsApp)
                - Email provider
            - All events sent to analytics for O1/A9.
            
            ---
            
            ## **13. Dummy Content (for Designer)**
            
            Calendar view (week):
            
            - Fri 11 April — “2 viewings”
            - Sat 12 April — “3 viewings”
            - Sun 13 April — “0 viewings”
            
            Selected Sat 12 April list:
            
            > 11:00–13:00 — 12 King Street (OPEN-HOUSE)
            > 
            
            > 4 confirmed · Capacity 10 · Status: ✅ Active
            > 
            
            > 15:30–16:00 — 22 Yoxley Drive (PRIVATE)
            > 
            
            > 1 confirmed · Status: ✅ Active
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ## **14. Rental Logic (Integrated)**
            
            Identical calendar mechanics.
            
            Only text around “Offer” later changes to “Application” elsewhere; calendar stores pure viewing data.
            
            ---
            
        - **🧩 WF-O5 — Public Property Page**
            
             WF-O5 is the public property page: full address, photos, key facts, docs, map, and a primary ‘Arrange a Visit’ CTA for everyone, plus ‘Message Owner’ only for logged-in Home-Hunters.
            
            ---
            
            (Owner Preview + Visitor View)**
            
            This is the *most important* public-facing page because **90% of our traffic arrives here from Rightmove / Zoopla / QR signs / WhatsApp links**.
            
            ---
            
            This is the page Home-Hunters land on from:
            
            ✔ Rightmove “Call redirect”
            
            ✔ WhatsApp viewing request link
            
            ✔ QR sign outside the house
            
            ✔ Social share
            
            ✔ Owner shares link directly
            
            This page must **convert** visitors into:
            
            - Booking a **viewing**,
            - Sending an **inquiry**,
            - Creating an account,
            - Eventually making an **offer** (Phase 2).
            
            ---
            
            # **1. Designer Checklist**
            
            - Use dark Dashfolio+ theme (no deviations).
            - Very strong visual hierarchy:
                - Photos first
                - Key data second
                - Viewings CTA extremely prominent
            - All CTAs in **Yalla Yellow**.
            - Sidebar **NOT visible** for visitors (only visible for logged-in Owners).
            - Mobile-first mindset — 80% of traffic comes via WhatsApp link or Rightmove mobile users.
            - Add “sticky CTA bar” on mobile:
                - **Arrange a Visit**
                - **Message Owner**
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            - Single route:
                
                /place/{placeSlug}
                
                (Owner preview uses same route with edit buttons visible if logged in)
                
            - Inputs required:
                - property
                - placeID
                - photos[]
                - floorplans[]
                - EPC file url (optional)
                - description
                - price OR rent
                - status (Live only for public)
            - Viewing logic:
                - Pull available slots from viewing_slots table
                - Only show “Arrange a Visit” if:
                    - listing = Live
                    - owner has at least 1 open or private slot
                - If no slots → CTA changes to “Request a Viewing”
            - Inquiry logic:
                - Create inquiry thread (guest or logged in)
            - Tracking:
                - page view event
                - CTA click events
                - viewing booking
                - inquiry send
                - open-house attendance
                - offer creation (Phase 2)
            
            ---
            
            # **3. Owner Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            Owner lands here to:
            
            - Check how their listing looks publicly
            - Test the viewings CTA
            - Test messaging
            - Click “Edit listing” to return to WF-O2
            
            Owner sees a **small preview banner**:
            
            > “You are viewing your public page — Edit listing”
            > 
            
            Visitors **never** see owner toolbar.
            
            ---
            
            # **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
            
            ```
            Google / Rightmove / Zoopla / QR Sign
                 ↓
              WF-O5 (Public Page)
                 ↓
            Home-Hunter Books Viewing OR Sends Inquiry
                 ↓
            WF-H1 (Calendar Booking Flow)
                 ↓
            Owner sees new booking → WF-O4
                 ↓
            Owner–Hunter conversation → WF-O3
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose**
            
            - Convert high-intent traffic into action.
            - Replace estate agents’ complicated “register interest” with 1-click viewings.
            - Show all essential property info in clean, modern layout.
            - Give confidence through surveys, EPC, and clear description.
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            For Visitors:
            
            - “What’s the price / rent / key info?”
            - “What does it look like inside?”
            - “Where is it?”
            - “Can I book a viewing easily?”
            - “Is there a survey available?” (optional but huge trust factor)
            - “How do I ask a question?”
            
            For Owners:
            
            - “Does my listing look professional?”
            - “Do all documents appear correctly?”
            - “Is the main CTA working?”
            - “Is the map correct?”
            
            ---

                - Swipe on mobile

            - Sticky top bar (mobile):
                - Price

            - **Property Type**
            - **Beds / Baths / Size**
            - **Tenure** (if sale)
            - **Furnished / Unfurnished** (if rental)
            - Status badge (Live, Under Offer, etc.)

                - **Arrange a Visit**

            >

            >

            >

            >

            >

            >

            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            - **🧩 Data Model (Dev) — WF-O5 Public Property Page**
                
                ### Goal: Make it crystal clear what data the Public Page needs, without duplicating the whole backend spec.
                
                ---
                
                ### Goal: Make it crystal clear what data the Public Page needs, without duplicating the whole backend spec.
                
                ### **1. Core Entities**
                
                **places (Property / “Place”)**
                
                - placeID (string, primary key)
                - ownerID
                - slug (for URL, e.g. shoreditch-12-king-street)
                - status (draft, live, under_offer, sold, let_agreed)
                - listingType (sale, rent)
                - price (number)
                - currency (GBP, EUR, …)
                - rentPerMonth (if listingType = rent)
                - depositAmount (optional, rent only)
                - minTermMonths (optional, rent only)
                - beds
                - baths
                - sizeSqm
                - sizeSqft
                - propertyType (flat / house / maisonette / other)
                - tenure (freehold / leasehold / share_of_freehold / commonhold)
                - epcRating (A–G or null)
                - yearBuilt (optional)
                - headline (title text)
                - description (long text)
                - addressFull (internal)
                - addressShort (area, e.g. “Shoreditch, London”)
                - lat, lng
                - addressPrivacyMode (full, area_only)
                - surveyAvailable (bool)
                - epcAvailable (bool)
                - floorplanAvailable (bool)
                - createdAt, updatedAt
                
                **Used by WF-O5:** all visible fields in hero, key facts, description, map, survey/EPC labels.
                
                ---
                
                **media (Photos / Video)**
                
                - mediaID
                - placeID
                - type (photo, video)
                - url
                - sortOrder
                - isPrimary (bool)
                
                **Used by WF-O5:** photo carousel, optional video.
                
                ---
                
                **documents (Public Docs)**
                
                - documentID
                - placeID
                - docType (epc, floorplan, brochure, other)
                - url
                - isPublic (bool)
                - title
                
                **Used by WF-O5:** EPC + floorplan + other docs section.
                
                ---
                
                **surveys (Condition Reports)**
                
                - surveyID
                - placeID
                - origin (owner, home_hunter)
                - status (pending_review, approved, rejected)
                - price (0 if free)
                - publicTitle
                - summary
                - url (PDF or link)
                - isPublicOnPage (bool – controlled by Owner/Admin)
                
                **Used by WF-O5:** “Survey available” badge + “Unlock / Download Survey” area.
                
                ---
                
                **viewing_slots (Availability)**
                
                - slotID
                - placeID
                - ownerID
                - slotType (OPEN_HOUSE, PRIVATE)
                - startTime
                - endTime
                - capacity (int)
                - status (active, full, cancelled)
                
                **Used by WF-O5:** to show **“Upcoming viewings” snippet** and to power the *Arrange a Visit* CTA → WF-H1.
                
                ---
                
                **traffic_metrics (Aggregated Analytics, per place)**
                
                - placeID
                - viewsTotal
                - viewsLast7d
                - ctaArrangeVisitClicks
                - ctaMessageClicks
                - documentViews
                - surveyViews
                - sourceBreakdown (JSON: Rightmove / Zoopla / QR / Direct / etc.)
                
                **Used by WF-O5 (optional):** to show “X people viewed this in the last 7 days” or to feed WF-O1 (Dashboard).
                
                ---
                
                ### **2. Minimal Data Required to Render WF-O5**
                
                To safely render the page, backend should guarantee:
                
                - places:
                    - placeID, slug, status, listingType
                    - price (or rentPerMonth)
                    - beds, baths, sizeSqm or sizeSqft
                    - addressShort
                    - addressPrivacyMode
                - media: at least 1 photo for hero (else show placeholder)
                - documents: optional, may be empty
                - viewing_slots: **at least zero**; if none → CTA shows “Request a time” instead of slot preview
                - surveys: optional
                - traffic_metrics: optional but recommended
                
                If status != live → page should either:
                
                - return 404 (public) and
                - show preview only to logged-in Owner.
                
                ---
                
                ### **3. ID & URL Conventions**
                
                - Public URL: /place/{slug}
                - Backend always resolves slug → placeID.
                - All internal relations use placeID (not slug) to avoid breakage if slug changes.
                
                ---
                
                You can paste this as:
                
                > “Data Model (Dev) — WF-O5 Public Property Page”
                > 
                
                inside your existing WF-O5 and you’re done — no second version, no duplication.
                
            
            ### **Availability Logic**
            
            - Pull viewing_slots where:
                - placeID matches
                - status = active
                - startTime > now
                - capacity not reached (OPEN HOUSE)
            
            If none found:
            
            > “This owner has not published viewing times yet.
            > 
            
            > You can request a viewing instead.”
            > 
            
            → Clicking opens WF-H1 with special mode: “Request a slot”.
            
            ---
            
            ### **Inquiry Logic**
            
            - Inquiry thread creation must be possible **without login**
            - But HH gets a prompt:
            
            > Save your inquiry and track viewings with a free account.
            > 
            
            Uses the **Unified Message Model** from WF-O3.
            
            ---
            
            ### **Owner Preview Mode**
            
            Owner logged in → small ribbon:
            
            ```
            You are viewing your public page.
            [Edit Listing]
            ```
            
            Do not mix owner sidebar here.
            
            ---
            
            ### **Tracking & Reporting**
            
            Event list to send to analytics:
            
            - page_view
            - cta_viewing_clicked
            - cta_message_clicked
            - scroll_depth
            - docs_viewed
            - survey_viewed/purchased (Phase 2)
            
            ---
            
            # **9. KPI Definitions**
            
            WF-O5 feeds Owner KPIs in WF-O1:
            
            - Public page views
            - CTA click rate (Arrange a Visit)
            - Inquiry rate
            - Document view rate
            - Survey purchase interest
            
            Admin also sees these in WF-A9.
            
            ---
            
            # **10. Conversion Funnel (Public Page → Outcome)**
            
            ```
            Landing Visitor
               ↓
            CTA View
               ↓
            Inquiry Sent OR Viewing Booked
               ↓
            Viewing Attended
               ↓
            Offer / Application
            ```
            
            WF-O5 drives the **first two steps**.
            
            ---
            
            # **11. ID Logic**
            
            This page must always connect:
            
            - placeID
            - ownerID
            - hunterID (if logged in)
            - slotID (if coming from calendar preview)
            
            Everything flows outward from here.
            
            ---
            
            # **12. Developer Tooling Overview**
            
            - Image optimization (lazy load)
            - PDF preview handling
            - Map provider:
                - Option A: Mapbox (recommended)
                - Option B: Leaflet + OpenStreetMap
            - URL structure:
                - /place/12-king-street-n1
                - SEO-friendly
                - Automatic redirect to canonical slug

            - Read property info
            - Choose a timeslot
            - Instant-confirmed viewing
            - Mandatory: name + buying position (“Cash / Mortgage Ready / Progressing / Just Browsing”)
            - Optional login
            - Message owner (only after login)

            - Messaging with Owners
            - Carries over into Offer flow
            - Threads per property
            - Seen receipts
            - Report-user (safety)

            - CTA: “Arrange a Viewing”
            - CTA: “Make an Offer”

            - All upcoming & past viewings
            - Reschedule/cancel
            - Sync with Google Calendar (optional)
            - Auto-confirmation + reminders
            - After viewing → “Leave feedback” optional

            - Track all offers made
            - Status:
                - Sent
                - Under Review
                - Accepted
                - Rejected
                - Counter Offer
            - Upload docs (ID, proof of funds, mortgage-in-principle)
            - Safe/verified offer submission

            (We just completed this one)
            
            - Surveys available to unlock
            - Surveys owned
            - Independent reports
            - Purchase via Stripe
            - View/download

            # **5️⃣ HOME-HUNTER DATA MODEL (clean + minimal)**
            
            ### **User (HH)**
            
            - hhID
            - name
            - email
            - phone
            - metadata: country, timezone
            - buyingPosition
            - verificationStatus (Phase 2)
            
            ### **Saved Places**
            
            - placeID
            - savedAt
            
            ### **Viewings**
            
            - viewingID
            - placeID
            - hhID
            - timeslot
            - status: confirmed / rescheduled / cancelled
            
            ### **Inbox**
            
            - threadID
            - createdBy: ownerID or hhID
            - messages[]
            
            ### **Offers**
            
            - offerID
            - placeID
            - hhID
            - amount
            - status
            - uploadedDocs
            
            ### **Surveys**
            
            - surveyID
            - origin: owner/hh
            - price
            - hhAccess[]
            
            ---
            
            # **6️⃣ WHERE EACH PAGE IS TRIGGERED FROM**
            
            ### **🟦 WF-O5 → H1 (Viewings + Offer Path)**
            
            - Viewing booking
            - Offer interest
            - Save place
            
            ### **🟪 Saved Places (H3)**
            
            - Comes from heart-icon on WF-O5
            - Also from “See your saved places” after booking
            
            ### **🟩 Messages (H2)**
            
            - Triggered when HH writes to Owner
            - Or when Owner replies
            
            ### **🟨 Surveys (H6)**
            
            - Triggered from Saved Places
            - Or WF-O5 survey badge
            
            ### **🟧 Viewings (H4)**
            
            - Auto-created through H1
            - Managed in-app
            
            ### **🟥 Offers (H5)**
            
            - Start from WF-O5
            - Or Saved Places
            - Or Inbox

            >

            # **8️⃣ WHAT DESIGNERS NEED TO KNOW**
            
            - Use Dashfolio+ structure
            - Always mobile-first
            - Sidebar collapses on mobile
            - All CTAs in **Yalla Yellow**
            - Copy tone = friendly, clean, useful
            - Keep transitions simple (no animations needed MVP)
            
            ---
            
            # **9️⃣ WHAT DEVELOPERS NEED TO KNOW**
            
            - Same user table as Owners (role = home_hunter)
            - All flows tied back to placeID
            - Minimal backend:
                - viewings
                - messages
                - offers
                - saved places
                - surveys
            - WhatsApp deep links for confirmations
            - Stripe for survey purchases

        ```jsx
        ────────────────────────────────────────

              • Account Settings

        - **🧩 WF-H1 — Home-Hunter Dashboard (Arrange a Visit Flow)**
            
            > This page handles
            > 
            > 
            > **all “contact owner” actions**
            > 
            - Book a viewing
            - Message owner (in-app inbox)
            - Contact via WhatsApp
                
                > It also enforces the
                > 
                > 
                > **Buyer Gate**
                > 
            
            ---
            
            ## **1. Designer Checklist**
            
            - Use existing **Yalla.House header + footer** (frozen).
            - Use **Home-Hunter sidebar** variant (Saved, Offers, Inbox, etc.).
            - Design **property booking panel** on the right side (desktop).
            - Show **three CTAs**:
                - Book a Viewing
                - Message Owner
                - Message on WhatsApp
            - Design **locked vs unlocked** states for each CTA (with lock icon + hint).
            - Create **Buyer Gate modal** with 3 steps:
                - Step 1: Basic details
                - Step 2: Phone verification (OTP)
                - Step 3: Success + redirect
            - Add all **error states** (invalid OTP, timeout, required fields).
            - Mobile layout: booking panel becomes a **full-width sheet** at bottom.
            - Ensure components re-usable: same gate used from property page & inbox.
            
            ---
            
            ## **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            - Enforce check: if (!homeHunter.phoneVerified) → openBuyerGate().
            - After successful gate, **replay original CTA** (message / booking / WhatsApp).
            - Implement **events**:
                - buyer_gate_opened
                - buyer_entered_profile
                - buyer_phone_submitted
                - buyer_phone_verified
                - buyer_gate_completed
                - buyer_contact_owner
                - buyer_book_viewing
            - Implement **API endpoints**:
                - POST /buyer/startVerification
                - POST /buyer/verifyCode
                - PATCH /buyer/profile
            - Integrate with **viewing slots** (open house vs private slot).
            - Store viewing request under viewingsRequested and confirmed under viewingsConfirmed.
            - Respect HomeHunter data model (name, email, phone, buyingPosition, country, funnelStage).
            
            ---
            
            ## **3. Home-Hunter Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            1. Home-Hunter lands on a **public property page** (WF-O5 / Public).
            2. Clicks **Book viewing / Message owner / WhatsApp**.
            3. If not verified → sees Buyer Gate modal (H1).
            4. Completes quick profile + phone verification.
            5. Gets redirected to:
                - Booking confirmation
                - Inbox thread
                - WhatsApp handoff.
            6. From then on, CTAs on all properties behave as **unlocked**.
            
            ---
            
            ## **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
            
            - **Entry points to WF-H1:**
                - From Public Property Page (CTA click)
                - From Saved Places → “Book viewing”
                - From Offers → “Message owner”
                - From Inbox → “Reply” (if not verified yet)
            - **Exit points from WF-H1:**
                - Back to the property with **confirmed booking**
                - To Home-Hunter Inbox with **new thread created**
                - To WhatsApp app / web
            
            WF-H1 is both:
            
            - A **booking UI**
            - And the **central verification gate** for Home-Hunters.
            
            ---
            
            ## **5. Purpose**
            
            - Ensure **no anonymous / low-quality contact** reaches the Owner.
            - Collect **minimum buyer data** for funnels and analytics.
            - Provide a **clean, quick booking flow** that works nicely on mobile.
            - Enable **WhatsApp contact** only after safe verification.
            - Keep the Owner’s inbox and calendar tidy and high-signal.
            
            ---
            
            ## **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            For Home-Hunters:
            
            - “I want to book a viewing quickly, without filling a huge form.”
            - “I want to decide between different time slots (group / private).”
            - “I can use WhatsApp if I prefer — but I understand why you ask for my number.”
            
            For Owners:
            
            - “I only get messages from people with a verified number and basic buying position.”
            - “I can see who is serious vs just browsing.”
            
            For Yalla.House:
            
            - Clean **funnel tracking**.
            - GDPR-safe handling of contact details.
            - Clear path to future **ID/AML verification** if needed.
            
            ---
            
            ## **7. Layout Overview (Desktop)**
            
            **Page type:** Modal flow over **Property Page** or **Booking Sheet**.
            
            ### **A. Screen: Property View + Booking Panel**
            
            **Left (2/3 width):**
            
            - Property image / title snippet (reuse from WF-O5)
            - Short description
            - Key facts (Price, Beds, Area)
            
            **Right (1/3 width): Booking & Contact Box**
            
            - Title: Arrange a visit
            - Subtext: Choose a time that works for you.
            
            **Section 1 — Quick slots**
            
            - Cards for available time ranges, for example:
                - “Sat 12 Oct — 11:00–13:00 (Open house)”
                - “Tue 15 Oct — 18:30 (Private slot)”
            
            **Section 2 — Contact options**
            
            - Button A: **Book Viewing**
                - Primary button
                - If locked → greyed with small lock icon + text
                - If unlocked → normal primary
            - Button B: **Message Owner (Inbox)**
                - Secondary button
                - Same locked/unlocked behaviour
            - Button C: **Message on WhatsApp**
                - Outlined button with WhatsApp icon
                - Same locked/unlocked behaviour
            
            **Below buttons:**
            
            - Tiny note:
                
                > “We ask for a quick profile so owners know who is visiting. No spam. No sharing your data with agents.”
                > 
            
            ---
            
            ## **8. Buyer Gate Modal – Visual Flow**
            
            The gate is a **3-screen modal** that appears over the current page.
            
            ### **8.1 Flow Diagram (Text UI)**
            
            ```
            [ Property Page / Booking Panel ]
                       |
               CTA clicked (Book / Message / WhatsApp)
                       |
               Is buyer.phoneVerified?
                  |             |
                 YES           NO
                  |             |
                  |       ┌───────────────────────┐
                  |       │  Buyer Gate Modal    │
                  |       └─────────┬────────────┘
                  |                 |
                  |         Step 1: Basic profile
                  |                 |
                  |         Step 2: Phone OTP
                  |                 |
                  |        Step 3: Success + back
                  |                 |
                  └───────────> Replay original CTA
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ### **8.2 Modal Step Layouts**
            
            ### **Step 1 — Basic Details**
            
            **Header:**
            
            - Title: Before you continue…
            - Text: Tell the owner a bit about who you are. This only takes 30 seconds.
            
            **Fields:**
            
            - Full Name (text)
            - Email (email field)
            - Country (dropdown, default from IP e.g. “United Kingdom”)
            - Buying Position (dropdown):
                - Cash
                - Mortgage in principle
                - Mortgage in progress
                - Just browsing
            
            **Buttons:**
            
            - Primary: Continue
            - Secondary: Cancel (closes gate, returns to property)
            
            ---
            
            ### **Step 2 — Phone Verification (OTP)**
            
            **Header:**
            
            - Title: Verify your phone number
            - Text: We use this to confirm your viewing and keep scams away.
            
            **Fields:**
            
            - Phone Number (with country code selector)
            - Button: Send code
            
            Once Send code is pressed:
            
            - Show OTP input
            - Show helper text: We’ve sent a 6-digit code to WhatsApp/SMS.
            
            **Errors:**
            
            - Invalid number → red helper: This number looks incorrect.
            - Code mismatch → That code doesn’t match. Try again.
            - Code expired → This code has expired. Request a new one.
            
            **Buttons:**
            
            - Primary: Verify
            - Link: Resend code
            
            ---
            
            ### **Step 3 — Success**
            
            **Header:**
            
            - Title: You’re verified! 🎉
            - Text: You can now book viewings and contact owners directly.
            
            **Body:**
            
            - Summary:
                - Name
                - Phone ✔
                - Buying Position
            
            **Buttons:**
            
            - Primary: Continue
                - On click: returns to the **original CTA action**:
                    - If from Book Viewing → open booking confirmation
                    - If from Message Owner → open new inbox thread
                    - If from WhatsApp → open wa.me link
            
            ---
            
            ## **9. States & Variants**
            
            ### **9.1 CTA Button States**
            
            For each button (Book, Message, WhatsApp):
            
            - **Locked:**
                - Grey background
                - Lock icon left
                - Tooltip: Verify your profile to continue
                - Click → opens gate modal.
            - **Unlocked:**
                - Normal primary/secondary styling
                - No tooltip
                - Click → direct action.
            
            ---
            
            ## **10. Developer Requirements (Logic & Events)**
            
            ### **10.1 Conditions**
            
            Before executing any CTA:
            
            ```
            if (!homeHunter.phoneVerified) {
              openBuyerGateModal({ originCTA: "book_viewing" | "message_owner" | "whatsapp" });
              track("buyer_gate_opened");
            } else {
              runOriginalCTA();
            }
            ```
            
            When Step 1 completed → update profile.
            
            When Step 2 success → set phoneVerified = true, verifiedAt = now(), funnelStage = "gate_completed".
            
            ### **10.2 Events to Fire**
            
            - buyer_gate_opened
            - buyer_entered_profile
            - buyer_phone_submitted
            - buyer_phone_verified
            - buyer_gate_completed
            - buyer_contact_owner
            - buyer_book_viewing
            
            ---
            
            ## **11. Data Model Links**
            
            Uses the **HomeHunter** model (no need to repeat, just reference):
            
            - name
            - email
            - phone
            - phoneVerified
            - buyingPosition
            - country
            - verifiedAt
            - funnelStage
            
            Stores **viewing requests** as viewingsRequested entries.
            
            ---
            
            ## **12. Dummy Content (for Designer)**
            
            ### **Example property:**
            
            - Title: Bright 2-bed flat near Finsbury Park
            - Price: £575,000
            - Tagline: Owner-listed. No agent fees.
            
            ### **Example slots:**
            
            - Sat 12 Oct — 11:00–13:00 (Open house)
            - Tue 15 Oct — 18:30 (Private viewing)
            
            ### **Example microcopy:**
            
            - Under buttons (locked):
                
                > “We ask for a quick profile so owners know who’s visiting. No third-party sharing. No agents.”
                > 
            - Step 1 info text:
                
                > “Owners see your name and buying position so they can prioritise serious viewers.”
                > 
            - Step 2 info text:
                
                > “We never show your number publicly. It’s used only for confirmations and fraud prevention.”
                >

            If you want, next we can:
            
            - Update **WF-O3 — Inquiries** so Owner sees “Verified buyer” + buying position.
            - Or draft the **Home-Hunter Dashboard (H2)** so they can see *“You’re verified”* and manage bookings.
            
            ---
            
            # **1. Designer Checklist**
            
            - Use full-width **mobile-first** layout (most users arrive from Rightmove/Zoopla).
            - Yalla Yellow for CTA buttons and confirmed status.
            - Use Dashfolio+ dark theme with minimal padding.
            - Booking modal/page includes a **3-step micro-form**:
                1. Confirm your name
                2. Your buying position
                3. Confirm booking
            - After submission → show **Success Screen** with:
                - Green “Viewing Confirmed” badge
                - Calendar add-buttons
                - “Create Account to Message Owner” CTA
            - No owner approval UI anywhere.
            
            **UI Notes for Designer**
            
            - Verified buyers see “Verified” badge in their HH sidebar
            - Owner sees verification status in WF-O3 (Inquiries)
            - Admin sees it in A2 & A3
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            ### **Data required**
            
            - hunterID (if logged in)
            - phone number (from WhatsApp redirect or RM phone call redirect)
            - booking form fields:
                - fullName
                - buyingPosition
                - email (optional but recommended)
            
            ### **API actions**
            
            1. Validate slot availability
            2. Create booking (auto-confirmed)
            3. Trigger outbound notifications:
                - WhatsApp
                - Email
            4. Insert system message into O3 thread
            5. Generate “Add to Calendar” link
            6. If HH not logged in → generate tempAccountToken → allow account creation later with pre-filled data.
            
            ---
            
            # **3. Home-Hunter Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            Home-Hunter arrives from:
            
            - Rightmove / Zoopla / OnTheMarket
            - Yalla.House QR sign
            - WhatsApp shared link
            - Search engine
            - Recommendation
            
            Then:
            
            1. Sees Public Property Page (WF-O5)
            2. Taps **“Arrange a Visit”**
            3. Lands on WF-H1
            4. Selects slot (open-house or private)
            5. Completes 10-second form
            6. Booking is **auto-confirmed**
            7. Receives WhatsApp + email
            8. Nudged to create free account to track offers & chat with owner
            
            ---
            
            # **4. User Journey (Where H1 Sits)**
            
            ```
            Public Property Page (WF-O5)
                   ↓  “Arrange a Visit”
                    WF-H1 — Booking Page
                   ↓  Auto-Confirmed
            WhatsApp + Email Confirmation
                   ↓
            Create Account (optional, nudged)
                   ↓
            WF-H2 (Inbox) & H8 (Dashboard)
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose**
            
            - Convert anonymous Rightmove traffic into **qualified viewing bookings**.
            - Capture **minimal but powerful pre-offer data** (name + buying status).
            - Give HH instant confirmation → zero frustration.
            - Push HH to create an account → unlock messaging + offers.
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - How do I book a viewing quickly?
            - Is this time available?
            - Will I get a confirmation right away?
            - How do I contact the owner?
            - Can I change the booking later?
            
            WF-H1 must make it **frictionless**.
            
            ---
            
            # **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
            
            ### **7.1 Top Section: Property Summary**
            
            - Thumbnail image
            - Address (or generalized area depending on privacy setting)
            - Price (Sale or Rent)
            - Beds / Baths / Size
            
            Example:
            
            > 12 King Street, London E1
            > 
            
            > £650,000 · 3 Beds · 92 m²
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.2 Slot Selector**
            
            Two formats:
            
            **A — Open-House Slot (multi-capacity):**
            
            ```
            Saturday · 11:00–13:00
            5 spots already booked
            [ Select Slot ]
            ```
            
            **B — Private Slot (one-only)**
            
            ```
            Sunday · 15:30–16:00
            Private viewing
            [ Select Slot ]
            ```
            
            If slot is full → greyed out, no CTA.
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.3 Micro Form (Mandatory)**
            
            After slot selection:
            
            **Field 1: Name**
            
            Your full name
            
            **Field 2: Buying Position (dropdown)**
            
            - Cash
            - Mortgage Ready
            - Mortgage in Progress
            - Just Browsing
            
            **Field 3: Email (optional but recommended)**
            
            If blank → we rely on phone number only.
            
            **System Note:**
            
            > “Your phone number is already linked via WhatsApp.
            > 
            
            > Add your email to receive reminders.”
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.4 Confirm Button (Primary CTA)**
            
            [ Confirm Viewing ] (Yellow)
            
            On click:
            
            - Booking created
            - Confirmation screen loads
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.5 Confirmation Screen**
            
            > 🎉
            > 
            > 
            > **Your Viewing is Confirmed**
            > 
            
            > Saturday 12 April · 11:00–13:00
            > 
            
            > 12 King Street, London E1
            > 
            
            Buttons:
            
            - [ Add to Google Calendar ]
            - [ Add to Apple Calendar ]
            - [ View Booking ] (opens H8 dashboard if logged in)
            - [ Create Account to Message Owner ]
            
            Also:
            
            > “You’ll receive a WhatsApp reminder before the viewing.”
            > 
            
            ---
            
            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            ### **Booking Rule Set**
            
            - Slot availability → booking auto-created
            - Booking = confirmed
            - For PRIVATE slots:
                - If one exists → slot becomes unavailable
            - For OPEN-HOUSE slots:
                - Increment participants
                - If capacity reached → full
            
            ### **Notification Pack**
            
            Immediately send:
            
            1. **WhatsApp**:
            
            ```
            Your viewing at 12 King Street is confirmed
            Sat 12 Apr, 11:00–13:00.
            Tap to view details: <link>
            — Yalla.House
            ```
            
            1. **Email** (if provided):
            
            ```
            Viewing Confirmed
            When: Sat 12 Apr, 11:00–13:00
            Where: 12 King Street
            Add to Calendar: <link>
            ```
            
            1. **Insert system message** into O3:
            
            > “Viewing booked and auto-confirmed.”
            > 
            1. **Push event** to Owner O4 calendar.
            
            ---
            
            # **9. KPI Definitions (for H1)**
            
            - Booking conversion rate
            - Drop-off after page load
            - Buying position distribution
            - Email capture rate
            - % of logged-in vs anonymous bookings
            
            ---
            
            # **10. Conversion Funnel**
            
            ```
            Page Load
              ↓
            Select Slot
              ↓
            Enter Details
              ↓
            Auto-confirmed
              ↓
            Create Account (optional)
              ↓
            Offer / Application (later)
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **11. ID Logic**
            
            - bookingID
            - hunterID (if new → temp generated)
            - slotID
            - placeID
            - ownerID
            
            ---
            
            # **12. Developer Tooling Overview**
            
            - WhatsApp API via Twilio
            - “Anonymous temp-hunter” creation
            - Merge identity if HH later signs up
            - Log events for Yalla analytics
            
            ---
            
            # **13. Dummy Content**
            
            **Slots:**
            
            > Saturday — 11:00–13:00 — 4/10 spots
            > 
            
            > Sunday — 15:30–16:00 — 1 private
            > 
            
            **Form:**
            
            > Name: Sarah L.
            > 
            
            > Buying Position: Mortgage Ready
            > 
            
            ---
            
            # **14. Rental Logic**
            
            Exactly same flow.
            
            Only change:
            
            - Price → Monthly rent displayed
            - Offers → “Applications” later
            
        - **🧩 WF-H2 — Home-Hunter Inbox (Messaging Hub)**
            
            *(Home-Hunter Workspace)*
            
            ---
            
            # **1. Designer Checklist**
            
            - Use Dashfolio+ layout, dark theme
            - Two-column page:
                - **Left:** conversation list
                - **Right:** open conversation
            - Ensure **Yalla Yellow** only for highlights (new message badge, active tab)
            - Mobile responsive (collapsible list into top drawer)
            - Message bubbles similar to WhatsApp / iMessage, but neutral
            - Add CTA buttons inside conversation (e.g., *Arrange Another Viewing*, *Make an Offer*)
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            - Build inbox as **per-listing conversation threads**:
            
            ```
            conversationID
            listingID
            ownerID
            homeHunterID
            messages[]
            timestamps
            status (new / read)
            ```
            
            - Real-time updates (polling every 15 sec or minimal websockets)
            - Allow attachments (Phase 2)
            - Store all sender metadata (HH → Owner)
            - Use i18n strings for every label
            - Permission check: Only Owner + Home-Hunter in a thread
            - GDPR-safe: show only **masked contact info** until offer stage
            
            ---
            
            # **3. Home-Hunter Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            1. They view a property.
            2. They want to ask questions before booking.
            3. Inbox allows conversation with Owner.
            4. System encourages next steps: **Book a Visit** or **Make an Offer**.
            
            ---
            
            # **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
            
            ```
            WF-H1 Dashboard
                  ↓
            WF-H2 Inbox
                  → From any conversation: Make an Offer / Book Visit / View Listing
            ```
            
            Accessible via Sidebar: **Inbox**
            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose**
            
            This page replaces WhatsApp or email. It keeps all conversation tied to:
            
            - the property
            - the owner
            - the booking
            - the offer
            
            It ensures **clean, auditable communication** protected under Yalla.House policies.
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - Avoid fragmented communication on WhatsApp
            - Give Home-Hunter one place to track all questions
            - Provide conversation history for Owner and Home-Hunter
            - Push user gently toward conversion (booking or offer)
            - Remove the need for direct phone numbers
            - Protect both parties under GDPR-safe chat
            
            ---
            
            # **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
            
            ### **A. Page Layout (Split Screen)**
            
            ```
            Left Panel — Conversation List
            Right Panel — Conversation Window
            ```
            
            ### **B. Conversation List**
            
            - Property thumbnail
            - Street name or alias (if address hidden)
            - Owner name shown as:
                
                → “Owner of 12 King Street” (not full name)
                
            - Timestamp of last message
            - New message badge (●)
            
            ### **C. Conversation Window**
            
            - Property header (address or alias)
            - Message timeline
            - CTA row:
                - Arrange a Visit
                - Make an Offer
                - View Listing
            
            ### **D. Message Input Area**
            
            - Text box
            - Send button
            - Microcopy: “Please keep conversations polite and safe.”
            
            ---
            
            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            - Load only conversations where:
            
            ```
            userID == homeHunterID
            ```
            
            - Unread badge logic:
            
            ```
            messages.filter(m => m.receiverID == currentUser && !m.read).length
            ```
            
            - Soft-delete (hide from user, keep in DB)
            - Anti-abuse filter (Phase 2)
            
            ---
            
            # **9. KPI Definitions**
            
            For Admin and performance dashboards:
            
            - **Response rate** = replies sent / messages received
            - **Time to first response**
            - **Conversion to booking** (CTA clicked after inbox)
            - **Conversion to offer**
            
            ---
            
            # **10. Conversion Funnel (Inbox → Booking/Offer)**
            
            For Home-Hunters:
            
            1. Messages opened
            2. Questions asked
            3. Owner replies
            4. CTA shown in chat
            5. Booking or Offer created
            6. Confirmation + next steps
            
            Expected conversion: **15–25%** to booking.
            
            ---
            
            # **11. Identity Logic (“Masking Contact Info”)**
            
            **We never reveal phone numbers or emails** until:
            
            - Home-Hunter makes an offer, **or**
            - Owner explicitly approves sharing (future feature)
            
            Masking example:
            
            ```
            Owner: “Owner • Verified”
            Home-Hunter: “Buyer • Verified”
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **12. Developer Tooling Overview**
            
            - Messaging stored in DB table messages
            - Notification service → email + WhatsApp
            - Optional AI auto-reply (future)
            
            ---
            
            # **13. Dummy Content**
            
            ### **Conversation List**
            
            ```
            12 King Street         ● New
            Owner replied 2h ago
            
            45 Oak Road
            You: “Is this available?” • 1d ago
            ```
            
            ### **Open Conversation**
            
            ```
            Owner: Hi! Yes the property is available.
            HH: Great, can I book this Saturday?
            Owner: Sure, 11:00 works.
            ```
            
            CTAs:
            
            ```
            [ Arrange a Visit ]  [ Make an Offer ]  [ View Listing ]
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **14. Rental Logic (Integrated)**
            
            No change needed.
            
            Whether listing is **Rent** or **Sale**, the inbox logic is identical.
            
            Only CTA text changes:
            
            - Sale → “Make an Offer”
            - Rent → “Apply to Rent”

            ---
            
            # **1. Designer Checklist**
