            - Grid or vertical list of “Place Cards”.
            - Clear status chips for each place.
            - Mobile-first.
            - Sticky sorting bar (Recommended: “Most Recent / With Viewings / With Offers”).
            - Yellow CTAs (Book viewing / Make offer).
            - Survey badge should stand out visually.
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            Data needed per place:
            
            - placeID
            - previewPhoto
            - addressShort or addressFull (based on privacy)
            - price or rent
            - savedDate
            - viewingStatus (not booked / confirmed / past)
            - offerStatus (none / pending / accepted / rejected)
            - surveyStatus (available / locked / bought)
            - nextViewingSlot (optional)
            - ownerID (internal only)
            
            APIs:
            
            - GET /hh/saved-places
            - POST /savePlace
            - POST /unsavePlace
            - POST /createBooking
            - POST /createOffer (Phase 2)
            - GET surveys metadata
            
            ---
            
            # **3. HH Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            Home-Hunter:
            
            1. Arrives from WF-O5 (Public Page)
            2. Books a viewing or saves the place
            3. Nudged to create account
            4. Lands here (H3 — Hub)
            5. Uses this page to:
                - Compare places
                - See viewing statuses
                - Message owners
                - Make offers
                - Buy surveys
            
            ---
            
            # **4. Where H3 Sits in the System**
            
            ```
            Public Page (WF-O5)
                 ↓ Save Place  OR  Confirm Viewing
            Account Creation (if needed)
                 ↓
            WF-H3 — Home-Hunting Hub
                 ↓
            H2 Inbox   •   H4 Viewings   •   H5 Offers   •   H6 Surveys
            ```
            
            H3 is the **central node** of the HH experience.
            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose**
            
            - Give Home-Hunters a **single cockpit** to manage their search.
            - Prevent them from getting lost (“Which property was which?”).
            - Encourage engagement (offer, survey, messaging).
            - Provide transparency (viewing + offer statuses).
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - Which places am I tracking?
            - Which ones have booked viewings?
            - Which ones have surveys?
            - Which ones did I message the owner about?
            - Which ones might be better value?
            - What’s next (viewing, message, offer)?
            
            ---
            
            # **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
            
            ### **H3.1 Page Header (simple)**
            
            > Your Saved Places
            > 
            
            > “Keep track of viewings, surveys and offers.”
            > 
            
            Sort dropdown (right side):
            
            - Most Recent
            - With Upcoming Viewings
            - Price (high → low)
            - Price (low → high)
            
            ---
            
            ### **H3.2 Saved Place Cards**
            
            Each card shows:
            
            - Cover photo
            - Address (respect privacy setting)
            - Price
            - Beds / Size
            - Status chips
            
            Example:
            
            **Status chips (stacked horizontally):**
            
            - ⭐ Saved
            - ✔ Viewing Confirmed (date)
            - 💬 Unread Messages (2)
            - 📄 Survey Available
            - 🟡 Offer Pending (Phase 2)
            
            ---
            
            ### **H3.3 Card Actions**
            
            **Primary:**
            
            - [View Details] → WF-O5 Public Page
            
            **Secondary:**
            
            - [Arrange a Visit] → WF-H1
            - [Message Owner] → WF-H2 (if logged in)
            - [Buy Survey] (if available)
            - [Make an Offer] (Phase 2)
            
            **Tertiary:**
            
            - [Remove] (unsave)
            
            ---
            
            ### **H3.4 View Empty State**
            
            If HH hasn’t saved any place yet:
            
            > “No saved places yet.”
            > 
            
            > “Browse now and tap ⭐ to save your first one!”
            > 
            
            Button: **[Find a Place]**
            
            ---
            
            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            - Keep saved places synced across devices (HH profile).
            - Viewing statuses must reflect O4 calendar data.
            - Messaging badges come from O3/H2 message logic.
            - Survey badges come from S6/S7 logic.
            - Offer statuses (future) from H5 + O-side.
            - Sorting must be server-powered (avoid slow client sort with 100+ saved places).

            # **9. KPI Definitions**
            
            - Saved → Viewing conversion rate
            - Survey purchase rate per place
            - Offer initiation rate per place
            - Time between viewing and offer
            - Drop-off from saved → forgotten

            ```
                   ↓
            ```

            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose**
            
            - Give HH a simple list of their upcoming/past viewings.
            - Reduce missed appointments.
            - Let them directly contact the owner.
            - Encourage engagement & offers after viewing.
            - Keep them in the Yalla.House ecosystem instead of Google Calendar.
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - When is my next viewing?
            - What’s the address?
            - Is it open-house or private?
            - How do I get there?
            - Can I message/cancel/reschedule?
            - What did I already view?
            - Should I make an offer now?
            
            ---
            
            # **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
            
            ### **7.1 Header**
            
            > Your Viewings
            >

            > 
            
            Filters:
            
            **Upcoming | Past | Cancelled**
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.2 Viewing Cards (Upcoming)**
            
            Each card shows:
            
            - Preview photo
            - Address (full or short)
            - Price / rent
            - Beds & size

                - Sat 12 Apr · 11:00–13:00

            >

            > “You haven’t viewed any places yet.”
            > 
            
            ---
            
            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            ### **Booking Rendering Logic**
            
            - If now < startTime → Upcoming
            - If now > endTime → Past
            - If status == cancelled → Cancelled
            
            ### **Calendar Sync**
            
            - Provide .ics universal file
            - Provide Google Calendar link:
                
                https://calendar.google.com/calendar/render?...
                
            
            ### **Messaging Link**
            
            - Always render conversation thread between hhID and ownerID.
            
            ### **Privacy Logic**
            
            - If Owner hides full address → reveal full address **only after booking**.

            # **9. KPI Definitions**
            
            For Admin analytics:
            
            - Attendance rate
            - Cancellation rate
            - Average time between booking → viewing
            - Multi-viewing frequency
            - Offer rate after viewing (Phase 2)

            > ✔ Confirmed
            > 
            
            > [View Details] [Message Owner] [Add to Calendar]
            > 
            
            ---
            
            # **14. Rental Logic**
            
            Identical.
            
            Only display:
            
            - Rent per month
            - Deposit / min term (optional)
            
            ---
            
        - **🧩 WF-H5 — My Offers / Applications (Home-Hunter)**
            
            ✔ Owner-side future offer handling
            
            ✔ Home-Hunter account flow
            
            ✔ GDPR-safe document handling
            
            ✔ Auto-confirmed viewing → offer pipeline
            
            ✔ For Sale **AND** For Rent logic
            
            ✔ MVP now + Phase 2 upgrades prepped
            
            ✔ Dashfolio+ style and terminology
            
            This is the most sensitive HH page, so the UX must feel **simple, guided, transparent**.
            
            ---
            
            # **1. Designer Checklist**
            
            - Mobile-first timeline layout.
            - Clear “Offer Status” chips:
                - Draft
                - Submitted
                - Viewed by Owner
                - Counter-offer
                - Accepted
                - Declined
            - Separate sections: **For Sale** vs **For Rent**.
            - Yellow CTA for “Make an Offer” or “Apply to Rent”.
            - If no viewing booked yet → nudge:
                
                > “Complete a viewing first for stronger acceptance.”
                > 
            - Upload zone (documents) must look clean + safe.
            - Sticky action bar on mobile after offer submitted.
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            ### **Must handle:**
            
            - offerID
            - hhID
            - ownerID
            - placeID
            - offerAmount (sale)
            - rentOffer (rent — optional, usually fixed)
            - applicationDocs[]
            - proofOfFundsDoc (sale)
            - idDocs[]
            - status:
                - draft
                - submitted
                - viewed
                - counter
                - accepted
                - rejected
            - Timestamps:
                - submittedAt
                - viewedAt
                - responseAt
            
            ### **APIs needed:**
            
            - POST /offer/create
            - POST /offer/update
            - POST /offer/submit
            - POST /offer/upload-doc
            - GET /hh/offers
            - GET /owner/offers
            
            ### **Notifications:**
            
            - Owner notified instantly.
            - Insert system message in O3/H2 inbox.
            
            ---
            
            # **3. HH Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            Typical path:
            
            ```
            WF-O5 Public Page
               ↓
            WF-H1 Book Viewing (auto-confirm)
               ↓
            WF-H4 Attend Viewing
               ↓
            WF-H5 Make Offer / Application
               ↓
            Owner responds (O-side)
               ↓
            Message thread continues (H2)
            ```
            
            H5 becomes their **negotiation dashboard**.
            
            ---
            
            # **4. Where H5 Sits**
            
            ```
            H3 Home-Hunting Hub
                   ↓ “Make Offer”
                   ↓
            H5 Offers / Applications
                   ↓
            H2 Inbox (owner replies)
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose**
            
            - Provide a **safe, simple** place to submit offers.
            - Upload required supporting docs.
            - Track offer progress transparently.
            - Keep buyer engaged inside Yalla.House instead of email.
            - Reduce friction for owners responding to offers.
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - How much should I offer?
            - What documents do I need?
            - What’s the current status?
            - Did the owner see my offer?
            - Has the owner replied?
            - Can I improve or withdraw my offer?
            
            ---
            
            # **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
            
            ## **H5.1 Section Header**
            
            > Your Offers & Applications
            > 
            
            > “Track offers, upload documents, and stay updated.”
            > 
            
            Filters:
            
            - **Active | Accepted | Declined | Drafts**
            
            ---
            
            ## **H5.2 Offer Cards (Sale)**
            
            Each card shows:
            
            - Photo + address
            - Price
            - Offer amount
            - Status chip
            - Last updated
            - Buttons:
                - [View Offer]
                - [Message Owner]
            
            ---
            
            ## **H5.3 Rent Applications Cards**
            
            Show:
            
            - Monthly rent
            - Status
            - Documents uploaded
            - Buttons:
                - [View Application]
                - [Message Owner]
            
            ---
            
            ## **H5.4 Offer / Application Detail Page**
            
            This is where the form sits.
            
            ### **Top Summary**
            
            - Photo + address
            - Price or rent
            - Viewing attended (✔ or ✖)
            
            If not viewed yet:
            
            > “You haven’t viewed this place yet. Offers from viewers are prioritised.”
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ### **Offer Form (Sale)**
            
            Fields:
            
            - Offer Amount
            - Buying Position (auto-filled from account)
            - Optional note to Owner
            - Upload:
                - Proof of Funds
                - ID
                - Mortgage in Principle (optional)
            
            Button:
            
            **[ Submit Offer ]** (Yellow)
            
            After submission:
            
            - Status → **Submitted**
            - Insert system message into O3/H2.
            
            ---
            
            ### **Application Form (Rent)**
            
            Fields:
            
            - Employment Status
            - Household income
            - Move-in date
            - Note to Owner
            
            Uploads:
            
            - ID
            - Proof of income
            - References (optional)
            
            Button:
            
            **[ Submit Application ]**
            
            ---
            
            ## **H5.5 Status Timeline (like Airbnb / portal flows)**
            
            Very important for clarity.
            
            ```
            Offer Submitted ✔  (timestamp)
            Owner Viewed        ••• (pending)
            Counter-offer        (optional)
            Offer Accepted       (green)
            or
            Offer Declined       (red)
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **H5.6 After Acceptance**
            
            CTA to push into next step:
            
            **Sale:**
            
            - “Your offer has been accepted — the owner will provide solicitor details.”
            - “Download Offer Summary (PDF).”
            
            **Rent:**
            
            - “Application accepted — next step: referencing.”
            - “Upload final documents.”
            
            ---
            
            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            - Must timestamp every status change.
            - Must notify Owner & HH via:
                - WhatsApp
                - Email
                - In-app (H2 / O3)
            - Must prevent editing after offer is submitted (except Add Documents).
            - Owner actions auto-update H5 timeline.
            - Document storage (Airtable attachment / S3 later).
            
            ---
            
            # **9. KPI Definitions**
            
            - Offers per listing
            - Time from viewing → offer
            - Offer acceptance rate
            - Application completion rate
            - Document upload completion rate
            
            ---
            
            # **10. Funnel**
            
            ```
            Viewing
              ↓
            H5 Offer Start
              ↓
            Offer Submitted
              ↓
            Owner Viewed
              ↓
            Accepted / Declined
              ↓
            Legal / Referencing (Phase 2)
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **11. ID Logic**
            
            - offerID
            - hhID
            - ownerID
            - placeID
            - status
            - timelineEvents[]
            - docIDs[]
            - offerAmount / rentTerms
            
            ---
            
            # **12. Tooling Overview**
            
            - Airtable: Offers table
            - Link to:
                - Places
                - HHAccounts
                - OwnerAccounts
                - Bookings
            - Twilio for notifications
            - S3/Airtable attachments for documents
            - PDF generation service (Phase 2)

            # **13. Dummy Content**

            # **14. Rental Logic**
            
            - Same structure.
            - Replace price with monthly rent.
            - Replace “Offer Amount” with “Application details”.
            - Replace Proof of Funds with Payslips.
            
            ---
            
        - **🧩** **WF-H6 — Surveys (Home-Hunter Survey Hub)**
            
            ---
            
            > Where Home-Hunters see
            > 
            > 
            > **all surveys**
            > 
            - Surveys they’ve **bought**
            - Surveys they’ve **uploaded** (if we allow this later)
            - Surveys **available to unlock** on places they follow
            
            ---
            
            ## **1. Designer Checklist**
            
            - Mobile-first list of survey cards.
            - Three clear states per place:
                - ✅ **Owned** (bought / uploaded)
                - 🔓 **Available to unlock**
                - ⛔ **Not available** (no survey yet – optional label)
            - Keep layout similar to H3 (Saved Places) so it feels familiar:
                - Property photo + address
                - Price / rent
                - Survey status
                - Clear CTA
            - Yalla Yellow only on primary CTAs:
                - “View Survey”
                - “Unlock Survey”
            - Don’t show scary legalese; keep copy human and helpful:
                - “Independent condition report”
                - “Helps you decide if it’s worth progressing”
            
            ---
            
            ## **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            Data per survey:
            
            - surveyID
            - placeID
            - origin (owner, home_hunter)
            - status (pending_review, approved, rejected)
            - price (0 = free; >0 = paid)
            - currency
            - shortTitle
            - summary
            - createdBy (ownerID or hhID)
            - createdAt
            - fileUrl (PDF or similar)
            - isPublicOnPage (bool – controlled by owner/admin)
            
            HH-specific:
            
            - ownershipStatus:
                - owned (bought or uploaded)
                - available (can buy)
                - none (no survey available, optional)
            
            APIs:
            
            - GET /hh/surveys (list relevant surveys)
            - POST /survey/purchase
            - GET /survey/{surveyID} (view/download, check access)
            
            Payment (MVP option):
            
            - Use Stripe Checkout for paid surveys.
            
            ---
            
            ## **3. HH Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            Home-Hunter:
            
            1. Saves place / books viewing (H3, H4)
            2. Notices “Survey available” badge on O5 / H3
            3. Clicks through to H6 OR buys directly from O5
            4. In H6, sees:
                - Surveys they already own
                - Surveys they can unlock
            5. Opens report → more confidence to:
                - Make an offer
                - Or walk away early
            
            H6 is like their **“Due Diligence Folder”** for all tracked properties.
            
            ---
            
            ## **4. Where H6 Sits in the System**
            
            ```
            H3 Home-Hunting Hub ──► H6 Surveys
                      ▲                 │
                      │                 ▼
                   O5 Public      Offer Flow (H5)
            ```
            
            Surveys can be surfaced from:
            
            - Public Property Page (O5)
            - Saved Places (H3 card)
            - Post-viewing follow-up email / WhatsApp
            
            H6 is the **central place** to manage them.
            
            ---
            
            ## **5. Purpose**
            
            - Give HH a structured area to **review and compare** survey reports.
            - Encourage **survey monetisation** (owner-paid or HH-paid).
            - Reduce wasted time on bad properties.
            - Help serious buyers move faster with data.
            
            ---
            
            ## **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - Does this property have an independent survey?
            - Have I already bought it?
            - Can I see it again easily?
            - Which properties look risky based on reports?
            - Do I want to buy more surveys?
            
            ---
            
            ## **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
            
            ### **7.1 Page Header**
            
            > Your Surveys
            > 
            
            > “View independent condition reports for the places you’re tracking.”
            > 
            
            Filters:
            
            - All
            - Owned
            - Available to Unlock
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.2 Survey Cards**
            
            Each card is tied to a **place**.
            
            **Top row:**
            
            - Property thumbnail
            - Address (short or full)
            - Price / rent
            
            **Middle row: survey info**
            
            - Status chip:
                - ✅ Owned
                - 🔓 Available (£29, example)
            - Origin:
                - “Provided by Owner” OR “Uploaded by another Home-Hunter”
            - Short summary:
                
                > “3-bed house, generally sound condition, minor damp in basement.”
                > 
            
            **Bottom row: CTAs**
            
            If **Owned**:
            
            - [View Survey] (opens PDF/report viewer)
            - [View Place] (go to O5)
            
            If **Available**:
            
            - [Unlock Survey for £29] (Stripe flow)
            - Small text:
                
                > “Buying once gives you lifetime access. Price may be owner-subsidised later.”
                > 
            
            If **None** (optional card):
            
            - Chip: “No survey available yet.”
            - CTA: “Ask Owner” (opens message thread in H2).
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.3 Survey Detail View (Lightweight)**
            
            Could be a modal or a separate page.
            
            Contains:
            
            - Property summary
            - Survey metadata:
                - Date
                - Surveyor name (if available)
                - Type (HomeBuyer, Structural, etc.)
            - Download/View buttons:
                - [Open PDF]
                - [Download]
            
            Optional area: “Key Highlights” if we later add AI summary.
            
            ---
            
            ### **7.4 Empty State**
            
            If no surveys at all:
            
            > “No surveys available yet.”
            > 
            
            > “As more Owners and Home-Hunters share surveys, they’ll show up here.”
            > 
            
            > Button:
            > 
            > 
            > **[View Your Saved Places]**
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ## **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            - Survey visibility rules:
                - Only show status = approved.
                - Respect isPublicOnPage flag.
                - If price > 0:
                    - Hide full file until purchase.
                    - Show only summary/title.
            - Ownership:
                - When HH buys survey → create survey_access record:
                    - hhID, surveyID, placeID, purchaseDate, pricePaid.
                - If HH uploaded/from their own account → auto-owned.
            - Payment:
                - Use Stripe session for purchase.
                - After success → redirect back to H6 with “Owned” state.
            - Messaging integration:
                - From “Ask Owner for Survey” triggers a message in O3/H2:
                    - “Buyer asked if a survey is available for this place.”
            
            ---
            
            ## **9. KPI Definitions**
            
            - Number of surveys available per listing
            - Survey purchase rate
            - Conversion from survey view → offer
            - Refund/issue rate (if any)
            - Revenue from surveys (Owner-paid vs HH-paid splits, later)
            
            ---
            
            ## **10. Funnel**
            
            ```
            Saved Place / Viewing
                   ↓
            Survey Available Badge Seen
                   ↓
            H6 — Survey Overview
                   ↓
            Unlock / View Survey
                   ↓
            Make a Better-Informed Offer (H5)
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **11. ID Logic**
            
            Key IDs used here:
            
            - surveyID
            - placeID
            - hhID
            - surveyAccessID
            - ownerID (survey origin linking)
            
            ---
            
            ## **12. Tooling Overview**
            
            - Airtable tables:
                - Surveys
                - SurveyAccess
            - File storage:
                - Airtable attachments or S3 (later)
            - Payments:
                - Stripe Checkout
            
            ---
            
            ## **13. Dummy Content**
            
            Card example:
            
            > 12 King Street, London E1
            > 
            
            > £650,000 · 3 Beds · 92 m²
            > 
            
            > 🔓
            > 
            > 
            > **Survey available — £29**

            >

            > 
            
            > [View Survey] [View Place]
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ## **14. Rental Logic**
            
            - Less critical but still useful:
                - HMO, safety checks, gas & electric reports
            - For rentals, surveys/cards might instead highlight:
                - Safety certificates
                - Damp / noise issues
                - Block / building condition
            
            Same layout, different text emphasis.

    - **🧩 WF-A1-A9 Wireframes & UX (Admin)** (internal control tools)
        - **ADMIN WIREFRAME LIST ( Logic)**
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A1 — Admin Dashboard (Command Center)**
            
            **Shows everything at a glance:**
            
            - Owners active / Places live
            - Home-hunters active
            - New viewings booked today
            - New inquiries today
            - New surveys uploaded / purchased
            - Integrations health (WhatsApp, Stripe, Calendar)
            - Revenue snapshot
            - Task count (from fulfillment queue)
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A2 — Owner Detail View**
            
            Admin sees everything about an owner:
            
            - Profile
            - Places listed
            - Performance stats
            - Tasks related to the owner
            - Subscription & billing status
            - Interactions timeline
            - Survey-related actions (if owner purchases surveys)
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A3 — Home-Hunter Detail View**
            
            Admin sees:
            
            - HH identity
            - Viewings booked
            - Messages
            - Surveys purchased / uploaded
            - Offers (Phase 2)
            - Flags (fraud/behaviour)
            - Verifications (ID, address, funds)
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A4 — Integrations & Status (Updated)**
            
            Now includes full logic for:
            
            - WhatsApp (Twilio)
            - Stripe
            - Email (Sendgrid)
            - Calendar Sync (Google)
            - Property Feeds (Rightmove, Zoopla)
            - QR tracking cold-start (signboard scans)
                
                **+ error messages + logs + timestamps**
                
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A5 — Tasks & Fulfillment**
            
            Rebuilt after your new logic.
            
            Tasks auto-created for:
            
            - Signboard orders
            - Photo/floorplan orders
            - EPC orders
            - Listing review / quality check
            - Owner support escalations
            - Survey validation
            - “Buyer flagged survey for review”
            
            This is the **“operations HQ”**.
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A6 — Survey Marketplace Oversight (Rebuilt)**
            
            Now it supports:
            
            ### **OWNER SIDE**
            
            - Did the owner upload the survey?
            - Does it meet quality standards?
            - Is it approved by admin?
            - Has any HH bought it?
            
            ### **HOME-HUNTER SIDE**
            
            - HH purchases
            - HH uploads
            - Refund requests
            - Disputes
            - Survey reusability
            - % commission earned
            
            Huge value centre.
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A7 — Support Inbox (Admin + Support Team)**
            
            Admin sees:
            
            - All owner + HH messages (not threads, but support tickets)
            - Auto-responses performance
            - Priority flags
            - Internal notes
            - Resolution workflow
            - SLA tracking
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A8 — Billing & Revenue Console**
            
            Tracks:
            
            - Owner subscription payments
            - Survey payments
            - Add-on services
            - Costs (Rightmove, Twilio, Stripe, photography vendors)
            - Revenue per place
            - Growth metrics
            - P&L preview (simple)
            
            ---
            
            ### **WF-A9 — Analytics & Performance Dashboard**
            
            The “CEO mode” inside admin.
            
            Metrics:
            
            - Owner → HH conversion
            - Viewing → offer rate (later)
            - Survey marketplace revenue
            - Lead source performance
            - Territory performance (UK → DE → more)
            - Funnel breakdown
            - Churn
            - Cost-to-acquire (later)
            - Cost-to-operate per place

        - **🧩  WF-A1 — Admin Dashboard (Global Control Center)**
            
            **(System Overview + Health + Key Metrics)**
            
            ---
            
            # **1. Designer Checklist (Dashfolio+ Ready)**
            
            - Use **Dashfolio+ dashboard base layout**
            - Dark theme background (#161616 / #212121)
            - Text: white + secondary (#CCD4D9)
            - Accent: **Yalla Yellow (#ECE269)**
            - Layout blocks:
                - **Top bar** (title only)
                - **3 KPI cards** (wide)
                - **2-panel lower layout** (left = Users & Listings Feed, right = Alerts)
            - Should look like a “control tower”
            - Must be visually **lightweight** (Admin lives here daily)
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            - Must load instantly (<300ms target)
            - Pull from minimal database calls (summaries only)
            - Fallback states for each widget
            - Every block = modular component (to expand later)
            - Store errors in integration_logs
            - Track admin interactions (for future training of AI assistant)
            
            ---
            
            # **3. Admin Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            This is the **first page** after admin logs in.
            
            Admin uses this page to quickly check:
            
            - Is the system online?
            - Are integrations working?
            - Are there new support messages?
            - Are there new listings / new bookings / new errors?
            
            Think of it as **“Morning Coffee Admin Overview.”**
            
            ---
            
            # **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
            
            ```
            Admin Login → WF-A1 Dashboard → (A2 User View / A5 Support / A4 Integrations)
            ```
            
            WF-A1 is the **hub**.
            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose (What This Page Is For)**
            
            - Give Admin immediate visibility into the platform status
            - Detect issues with Stripe / WhatsApp / Email
            - See new listings, bookings, inquiries
            - See task bottlenecks (EPC needed, photos pending, signboard)
            - Prevent fires before they happen
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - Reduce manual checking
            - Provide early warnings
            - Surface urgent tickets
            - Help forecast demand (owners onboarding → requests → tasks)
            - Show platform health at a glance
            
            ---
            
            # **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
            
            ### **PAGE LAYOUT (BLOCKS)**
            
            ### **A) Header**
            
            - Title: **Admin Dashboard**
            - Sub-label: “System Overview”
            
            ### **B) KPI Cards (Row of 3)**
            
            1️⃣ **Total Owners**
            
            - Huge number
            - “+X new this week”
            
            2️⃣ **Total Home-Hunters**
            
            - For marketplace density
            - “+X new this week”
            
            3️⃣ **System Health Status**
            
            - GREEN = all integrations OK
            - ORANGE = degraded
            - RED = error
            
            ---
            
            ### **C) Activity Feed (Left column)**
            
            *(short scroll list)*
            
            **Latest Owner Actions:**
            
            - “John S. created a new listing — 14 King Street”
            - “New inquiry on 22 Maple Road”
            - “3 bookings scheduled today”
            
            **Latest Home-Hunter Actions:**
            
            - “Sarah L. booked viewing for Sat 11 AM”
            - “Offer submitted on 9 Oak Drive (£615k)”
            
            ---
            
            ### **D) Alerts Panel (Right column)**
            
            Blocks:
            
            - **Integration Alerts**
                - WhatsApp unreachable
                - Stripe webhook failed
                - Email bounce rate >5%
            - **Support Alerts**
                - New ticket
                - “High priority: Listing not updating on portal”
            - **Tasks Alerts**
                - “EPC pending for 12 Willow Lane”
                - “Signboard QR not generated”
            
            ---
            
            ### **E) Footer Text**
            
            “Admin Panel v1.0 — Internal Use Only”
            
            ---
            
            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            | **Component** | **Source** | **Table / Logic** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Owners Count | DB | users with role=owner |
            | Home-Hunters Count | DB | users with role=seeker |
            | System Health | Aggregated | Stripe ping, WhatsApp ping, Email ping |
            | Activity Feed | DB | Combined listings, inquiries, viewings, offers |
            | Alerts | DB | integration_logs, support_tickets, task_items |
            
            **Ping Logic:**
            
            - Every 5 min cron
            - Save status → integration_status
            - Dashboard pulls latest entry
            
            ---
            
            # **9. KPI Definitions**
            
            | **KPI** | **Meaning** | **Notes** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | Total Owners | Registered owners | Includes free accounts |
            | Total Listings | All listings (draft/live/pending) | Used for forecasting |
            | Total Home-Hunters | Registered seekers | Important for liquidity |
            | Viewings Today | Count of bookings | Predicts support load |
            | Support Tickets | Open tickets | If >10 → show warning |
            | Integration Health Score | 0–100 | Weighted across services |
            
            ---
            
            # **10. Conversion Funnel (Admin-Level)**
            
            *(For forecasting workloads)*
            
            **Owners Created → Listings Drafted → Listings Published → Viewings Booked → Offers Received**
            
            The dashboard should show:
            
            - % change week-on-week
            - Bottleneck detection (e.g., many drafts but few published)
            
            ---
            
            # **11. Property ID Logic (Shared Across Platform)**
            
            - placeID = auto-generated UUID
            - Human-readable slug generated from street name:
                - 12-king-street-london
            - Used in public URL:
                - /place/12-king-street-london-4F2A1B
            
            Admin dashboard shows both.
            
            ---
            
            # **12. Developer Tooling Overview**
            
            **Tables involved:**
            
            - users
            - places
            - inquiries
            - viewings
            - offers
            - integration_status
            - support_tickets
            - task_items
            
            **APIs involved:**
            
            - Stripe
            - WhatsApp (Twilio)
            - Email (SendGrid / Resend)
            
            **Cron jobs:**
            
            - Integration health checks
            - Daily cleanup
            - Weekly report (Phase 2)

            - Right column = **scrollable**

            - Use compact cards (Owner has more data than HH—layout must adapt)

                - User core profile

                - Viewings

                - Flags

            - Use role-based hydration to load only relevant sections
            - Timeline = from events_log table
            - All admin actions logged in admin_audit_log
            - Home-Hunter funnel metrics must be computed on load

            - See their offers & viewings
            - See if they are “good” or “bad” users

            ## **LEFT COLUMN — User Profile (Fixed)**
            
            *(colour-coded status)*

            - Avatar
            - Name
            - Email
            - Phone
            - Country
            - Role (**🟦 Owner** / **🟨 Home-Hunter**)

            - Last login
            - Devices: Mobile / Desktop
            - “Trust Score”: **🟢 Good**, **🟡 Medium**, **🔴 Risk**

            - ID verified
            - Address verified
            - KYC level
            - Buttons: **Verify / Reject / Request more docs**
            
            ---

            - ID
            - Proof of address
            - Additional docs (Owner = EPC, Floorplan)
            - Surveys (if Owner uploaded one)

            - Fraud suspicion
            - Multiple failed KYC
            - Spam messaging
            - Notes from support

            - Created account

            - Saved a place
            - Booked viewing
            - Submitted offer
            - Uploaded survey
            - Purchased survey
            - Updated listing
            - Changed price

            | Place | Status | Price/Rent | Views (7d) | Inquiries | Offers | Last Update |

            - **🟡 Inquiry Response Time**
            - **🔴 Overdue Tasks**

            ### **C) Home-Hunter Section (Render ONLY if role=seeker)**
            
            ## **HOME-HUNTER METRICS**
            
            ### **H1 — Viewing Behaviour**
            
            - **Viewings booked**
            - **Viewings attended**
            - **Cancellation rate**
                - 🟢 <20%
                - 🟡 20–40%
                - 🔴 >40%
            
            ### **H2 — Offers / Applications**
            
            | Property | Amount | Status | Date | Position |
            
            - “Position” shows queue rank (1st, 2nd, etc.)
            
            ### **H3 — Inquiry Stats**
            
            | Place | Messages sent | Owner replies | Speed (min) |
            
            ### **H4 — Interest Funnel (critical)**
            
            ```
            Viewed → Saved → Booked → Attended → Offered → Survey → Completion
            ```
            
            Each stage shows a %.
            
            ### **H5 — Surveys (Bought + Sold)**
            
            - Bought:
                - Price
                - From whom
                - Reusable? (Yes/No)
            - Sold (Phase 2):
                - Earnings
                - Buyer count
            
            ### **H6 — Device + Behaviour Tracking**
            
            - Device used
            - Regions searched
            - Time active on site
            - Time between steps
            
            ---
            
            ### **D) Support Thread**
            
            - Complete conversation history
            - Admin internal notes
            
            ---
            
            ### **E) Payment History**
            
            (Owner or HH if survey purchased)

            - email
            - phone

            - country

            - Index columns:
                - email
                - phone
                - role
                - last_active

            - Support staff cannot see sensitive notes
            - Admin must see everything

        - **🧩  WF-A4 — Integrations & Status (Admin)**
            
            **(System Health + API Status + Error Logs)**
            
            ---
            
            # **1. Designer Checklist (Dashfolio+ + Colour Rules)**
            
            Use clear Admin hierarchy:
            
            | **Status** | **Colour** | **Meaning** |
            | --- | --- | --- |
            | 🟢 Green | #2ECC71 | Fully functional |
            | 🟡 Amber | #F1C40F | Degraded / partial |
            | 🔴 Red | #E74C3C | Down / errors |
            | 🔵 Blue | #3498DB | Informational blocks |
            | ⚫ Dark UI | Dashfolio+ background | Base |
            
            UI Blocks to include:
            
            - Top section = **System Overview Strip** (horizontal badges)
            - Card grid for individual integrations
            - Right column for **error logs**
            - Small “Ping Now” button
            - Light, readable table for logs
            
            Consistency:
            
            - Use icons only if needed
            - Yalla Yellow (#ECE269) for active filters or titles
            - Avoid clutter — Admin must diagnose issues quickly
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            - Endpoint: /admin/integrations/status
            - Returns:
                - Status (up/down/degraded)
                - Last successful ping
                - Latency
                - Error count (last 24h)
                - Response message
            - Cron job every 5 minutes pings all services
            - Logs stored in integration_logs
            - Admin “Ping Now” triggers forced diagnostics
            - Must show **root cause message** when available
            - Implement severity levels
            - Must be safe in case a service is 100% down
            
            ---
            
            # **3. Admin Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            Admin uses A4 to:
            
            - Check system reliability
            - Diagnose owner or home-hunter issues
            - Validate webhook delivery
            - Detect outages BEFORE users report them
            - Know when external integrations fail
            - Restart or retry problematic services
            
            This page = **Technical HQ**.
            
            ---
            
            # **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
            
            ```
            Admin Login
             → A1 Dashboard
               → A4 Integrations & Status  (You are here)
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose**
            
            To provide a **real-time, at-a-glance overview** of all:
            
            - Mission-critical APIs
            - Third-party services
            - Webhooks
            - Messaging channels
            - Portals & payment providers
            - Background jobs (cron workers)
            
            This page is critical for **early warning and stability**.
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - Detect outages BEFORE users complain
            - Provide transparent diagnosis
            - Make debugging easy
            - Provide central audit log for all services
            - Show admin if Rightmove/Zoopla pushes are failing
            - Show WhatsApp failures (Twilio)
            - Display Stripe webhook errors
            - Track email deliverability
            - Highlight patterns of degradation
            - Show uptime %
            
            ---
            
            # **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
            
            ### **A) Page Header**
            
            **Integrations & System Status**
            
            Subtext: “Live monitoring of connected services.”
            
            ---
            
            ### **B) System Overview Strip (Top Row)**
            
            Four coloured badges (big + horizontal):
            
            - **Platform Health (score 0–100)**
            - **Errors (24h)**
            - **Active Services**
            - **Background Jobs**
            
            Each badge uses colour based on severity.
            
            ---
            
            ### **C) Services Grid (Main Area)**
            
            Each card is a small module:
            
            ### **1) Stripe (Payments)**
            
            - Status: 🟢 UP
            - Last Ping: 1m ago
            - Webhooks: delivered / failed
            - Latency: 120ms
            - Button: “View Webhooks”
            
            ### **2) WhatsApp / Twilio Messaging**
            
            - Status
            - Last delivery
            - Failed messages count
            - Send test message
            
            ### **3) Email Delivery (SendGrid / Resend)**
            
            - Bounce rate
            - Last 5 errors
            - Templates status
            
            ### **4) Database Health**
            
            - Queries per minute
            - Slow queries
            - Storage
            
            ### **5) Rightmove (Phase 2)**
            
            - Status
            - Last listing push
            - Last error
            
            ### **6) Zoopla (Phase 2)**
            
            - Same fields as above
            
            ### **7) Cron Jobs**
            
            - x jobs running
            - Last run
            - Missed tasks
            
            ### **8) Internal API Gateway**
            
            - Response time
            - Status
            
            ---
            
            ### **D) Error Log Panel (Right Column)**
            
            Table:
            
            | **Time** | **Service** | **Severity** | **Message** |
            | --- | --- | --- | --- |
            | 10:44 | WhatsApp | 🔴 High | “Delivery failed: 500 error” |
            | 09:22 | Stripe | 🟡 Medium | “Webhook retry #2” |
            
            Row colours match severity.
            
            Filters:
            
            - Last 24h
            - Last 7 days
            - By service
            
            ---
            
            ### **E) Buttons**
            
            - **Ping All Services** (yellow)
            - **Export Logs**
            - **Clear Filters**
            
            ---
            
            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            ### **Data sources**
            
            Tables:
            
            - integration_status
            - integration_logs
            - cron_jobs
            - webhook_logs
            - internal_stats
            
            Ping Logic:
            
            - Cron job triggers /ping for all services
            - Save response time, status, error cause
            - Admin view loads latest snapshot
            
            ### **Severity Logic**
            
            - **🟢 OK** → ping <300ms, no errors
            - **🟡 Warning** → slow response or partial failures
            - **🔴 Critical** → timeouts, HTTP errors, repeated retries
            
            ### **Developer Notes**
            
            - Some services are Phase 2 (Rightmove, Zoopla)
            - Hide Phase 2 cards until activated
            - Pre-built placeholders allowed
            - Support staff: read-only view
            
            ---
            
            # **9. KPI Definitions**
            
            | **KPI** | **Meaning** |
            | --- | --- |
            | System Health | Weighted average of all integration statuses |
            | Error Count (24h) | Count of failures across all systems |
            | API Latency | Average response time |
            | Webhook Delivery Rate | Delivered / Total webhooks |
            | Messaging Reliability | From Twilio send vs fail rates |
            | Portal Push Success | For Rightmove/Zoopla (Phase 2) |
            
            ---
            
            # **10. Conversion Logic**
            
            Not direct here.
            
            But A4 informs the Admin **why conversion might drop**:
            
            - WhatsApp down → fewer inquiries
            - Email down → missed confirmations
            - Portal push errors → listings not updating
            
            ---
            
            # **11. Integration ID Logic**
            
            Each integration has:
            
            - integration_id
            - name
            - status
            - last_ping
            - last_error
            - latency
            
            IDs used for debugging/action buttons.
            
            ---
            
            # **12. Developer Tooling Overview**
            
            - Internal endpoints:
                
                /ping/stripe
                
                /ping/email
                
                /ping/whatsapp
                
                /ping/rightmove
                
                /ping/zoopla
                
            - Admin actions logged to admin_audit_log
            - Background workers log to cron_jobs
            - Must be resilient to downed services
            
            ---
            
            # **13. Dummy Content**
            
            ```
            Platform Health: 92/100 (🟢 Good)
            Errors (24h): 12 (🟡 Warning)
            Active Services: 7/7 running
            Background Jobs: All OK
            
            Stripe: 🟢 UP — Last ping 2m ago
            WhatsApp: 🟡 Partial — 3 failed deliveries
            Email: 🟢 OK — Bounce rate 1.2%
            Rightmove: (Phase 2) Not enabled
            Database: 🟢 Stable — 12ms avg
            Cron: 6 jobs OK, 0 missed
            ```

            Rentals use identical integration logic.
            
            Only differences:
            
            - Rental “Applications” generate webhook events (Phase 2)
            - Calendar integrations are identical
            - Pricing/rent pushes to portals will be identical (Phase 2)

            - “Set Priority”
            - “Set Category”

            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            ### **Ticket Lifecycle**
            
            - open → default
            - pending → waiting for user
            - resolved → admin closed
            - reopened → if user messages again
            
            ### **SLA Logic**
            
            - Define by priority
            - Shown as a countdown
            - When expired → auto tag red + email alert
            
            ### **Classification Logic (Phase 2)**
            
            - NLP auto-detects:
                
                “payment”, “cancel”, “booking”, “bug”, “survey”
                
            - Auto-route to correct category
            
            ### **Ingestion Inputs**
            
            - Inbound email → piping
            - Inbound WhatsApp → webhook
            - Owner contact form → API
            - HH contact → API
            
            ### **GDPR**
            
            - Log everything
            - Allow export on request
            - Mask sensitive info

            | Tickets per user | Track frustration |
            | Category frequency | Helps improve product |
            | Reopen rate | Poor solution quality |
            | Resolution time | Support efficiency |

        - **🧩  WF-A7 —  Survey Marketplace Oversight (Admin)**
            
            *(Admin control panel for surveys submitted by Owners & Home-Hunters.)*
            
            ---
            
            # **1. Designer Checklist**
            
            Build a **3-panel layout**:
            
            ### **A) Top Filters (horizontal):**
            
            - Property ID
            - User (Owner or Home-Hunter)
            - Survey Type (RICS / Valuation / Structural / HomeBuyer)
            - Verification status
            - Revenue range
            
            ### **B) Main Table:**
            
            Columns:
            
            | **Column** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Survey ID | Auto-generated |
            | Property Address | From listing |
            | Uploaded by | Owner or HH |
            | Type | RICS, Valuation, Structural, etc. |
            | Status | Uploaded / Pending Verification / Approved / Rejected |
            | Revenue | £XX (sum of purchases) |
            | Purchases | Number of HH who bought |
            | Actions | View / Verify / Reject / Message |
            
            ### **C) Expanded Slide-out Panel**
            
            When clicking a row → open:
            
            - Survey details (PDF viewer embed)
            - Linked property
            - Linked user
            - Verification checklist
            - Internal notes
            - Activity log
            - Payout info
            
            Use **Dashfolio style**, Yalla Yellow only for:
            
            - Verified status
            - CTA buttons
            - Warnings
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            This WF requires:
            
            ### **Database tables**
            
            ```
            surveys
            survey_purchases
            survey_verification
            survey_payouts
            ```
            
            ### **Survey Lifecycle States**
            
            Value of status:
            
            - uploaded
            - pending_verification
            - approved
            - rejected
            - flagged (Phase 2 anti-fraud)
            
            ### **Revenue Calculation**
            
            For Admin dashboard + payouts:
            
            ```
            revenue = SUM(survey_purchases.amount)
            ```
            
            ### **Upload Sources:**
            
            - Owner → Upload under WF-O4 Docs
            - Home-Hunter → Upload under WF-H4 Surveys
            
            ### **Verification Workflow**
            
            Admin must check:
            
            - File validity
            - Property match
            - Date < 12 months
            - No tampering
            
            ### **Purchase Logic**
            
            A survey can be bought by unlimited HH as long as:
            
            - It’s **Approved**
            - The property is **active or sold**
            
            ### **Payout Logic**
            
            Admin decides:
            
            - Payout to uploader (50%)
            - Marketplace fee (50%)
            
            (Payout percentages can be adjusted later.)
            
            ### **Messaging Integration**
            
            Admin can message the uploader from inside this WF.
            
            ---
            
            # **3. Admin Journey Summary**
            
            Admin opens A7 to:
            
            - Verify submitted surveys
            - Approve / reject surveys
            - Handle payout requests
            - Handle disputes
            - Track revenue
            - Identify popular surveys
            - Prevent fraud
            
            This is the **control panel for the survey marketplace**.
            
            ---
            
            # **4. User Journey (Context)**
            
            ```
            Owner / HH submits survey → Admin receives in A7
            Admin verifies or rejects → Status updates
            Survey becomes visible in WF-O5 & WF-H5
            Home-Hunters buy → payouts logged
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose of This Page**
            
            - Centralise all survey operations
            - Ensure quality + authenticity
            - Manage revenue + payouts
            - Maintain trust & safety
            - Keep marketplace running smoothly
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - Prevent fake or outdated surveys
            - Avoid manual back-and-forth via email
            - Make payouts transparent
            - Provide admins with full visibility
            - Help founders analyse the commercial opportunity
            
            ---
            
            # **7. What the Designer Should Build**
            
            ### **TABLE (Main View)**
            
            - Search bar
            - Filters dropdown
            - Sort (date, revenue, status)

            ### **(Phase 2)**
            
            - Payout processed
            - Survey verified
