        - **🧩  WF-A8 — Billing & Revenue (Admin)**
            
            *Handles subscriptions, one-off services, marketplace revenue, and payouts.*
            
            ---
            
            # **1. Designer Checklist (What to build)**
            
            ### **A) Page Layout**
            
            Create a **3-section scroll layout**:
            
            ---
            
            ### **SECTION 1 — Revenue KPIs (Top Highlight Boxes)**
            
            Use Dashfolio+ KPI cards:
            
            - **MRR (Monthly Recurring Revenue)**
            - **One-off Service Revenue (EPC, Photography, Floorplan, Signs)**
            - **Survey Marketplace Revenue**
            - **Payouts Pending (to Owners/HH)**
            - **Owner ARPU (avg revenue per Owner)**
            - **HH ARPU (avg revenue per HH)**
            
            📌 Use Yalla Yellow for “Positive trend ↑”
            
            ---
            
            ### **SECTION 2 — Transactions Table (Stripe + Internal Sources)**
            
            Column list:
            
            | **Column** | **Description** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Date | Timestamp |
            | User | Owner / HH (with link to User Detail WF-A2/A3) |
            | Type | Subscription / Service / Survey Purchase |
            | Source | Stripe / Survey Marketplace / Manual |
            | Amount | £XX |
            | Fee | Stripe fee or Marketplace fee |
            | Net Revenue | Amount – Fee |
            | Status | Paid / Failed / Refunded |
            | Actions | View receipt, resend, adjust |
            
            Must be **filterable** by:
            
            - Date range
            - User type
            - Revenue type
            - Status
            - Country (UK / DE)
            
            ---
            
            ### **SECTION 3 — Payouts (To Owners & Home-Hunters)**
            
            A card/table showing:
            
            | **Payout ID** | **User** | **Survey** | **Amount** | **Status** | **Action** |
            | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
            | PT-0194 | Owner 221 | SRV-2025… | £48 | Pending | Pay Now |
            | PT-0172 | HH 332 | SRV-2024… | £12 | Completed | View |
            
            Status colours:
            
            - **Pending** → Yellow
            - **Completed** → Green
            - **Error** → Red
            
            ---
            
            # **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            ### **Endpoints needed**
            
            - GET /admin/revenue/summary
            - GET /admin/transactions
            - GET /admin/payouts
            - POST /admin/payouts/pay
            - POST /admin/refund
            
            ### **Stripe Integration**
            
            Admin must be able to:
            
            - Pull invoices
            - Pull subscription status
            - Resend receipts
            - See card failures
            - See dunning (retry attempts)
            
            ### **Survey Marketplace**
            
            - Sum survey purchases
            - Handle 50/50 fee split
            - Release payouts manually (MVP)
            - Log payout statuses
            
            ### **Service Sales**
            
            For Owner add-ons:
            
            - EPC
            - Photography
            - Floorplan
            - Sign board
            - Premium Boost visibility
            - RICS pre-negotiated partner services
            
            ---
            
            # **3. Admin Journey Summary**
            
            Admin uses A8 to:
            
            - Track all money flowing IN
            - Track all money flowing OUT
            - Track expected revenue
            - Make manual payouts
            - Review failed payments
            - Handle refunds
            - Review service usage
            - See which revenue stream is growing fastest
            
            This becomes the **financial heartbeat** of Yalla.House.
            
            ---
            
            # **4. User Journey (Context)**
            
            For Owners & HH:
            
            ```
            User buys → Stripe handles payment → Admin sees transaction in A8
            If survey purchased → Survey uploader eligible for payout
            If subscription renews → Recurring entry appears
            If service ordered → Task generated in A4
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **5. Purpose of This Page**
            
            - Centralise all revenue management
            - Avoid manual bookkeeping
            - Provide clarity on performance
            - Allow payouts to survey uploaders
            - Give founders insight into growth
            
            ---
            
            # **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - No more guessing revenue
            - No digging in Stripe manually
            - No losing track of payouts
            - No inconsistent freelancer reporting
            - No bottleneck in financial clarity
            
            ---
            
            # **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
            
            - **KPI cards** → top
            - **Transactions Table** → sortable & filterable
            - **Payout Table** → with action buttons
            - **Receipt modal**
            - Consistent dark theme Dashfolio+
            - No graphs (MVP), only cards + tables
            - Export CSV button
            
            ---
            
            # **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            ### **Must:**
            
            - Show live subscription status
            - Sync Stripe data nightly
            - Show partial refunds
            - Connect “Buy Services” to A4 task board
            
            ### **Should:**
            
            - Implement currency support (auto-convert to base GBP)
            
            ### **Could (optional):**
            
            - Predict next 30-/90-day revenue
            - Show churn rate
            
            ---
            
            # **9. KPI Definitions**
            
            # 
            
            # **(clear & founder-level)**
            
            | **KPI** | **Meaning** |
            | --- | --- |
            | **MRR** | All active recurring subscriptions (Owners) |
            | **One-off Revenue** | EPC, photography, floorplan, signs |
            | **Marketplace Revenue** | Surveys sold (platform share) |
            | **Payouts Pending** | Money owed to uploaders |
            | **ARPU (Owner)** | Avg revenue per Owner |
            | **ARPU (HH)** | Avg revenue per Home-Hunter |
            | **Failed Payments** | Needs admin review |
            | **Refund Rate** | % of refunded transactions |
            
            ---
            
            # **10. Revenue Model Logic (Dev-Ready)**
            
            ```
            total_revenue = subscription_revenue
                           + services_revenue
                           + marketplace_revenue
                           - refunds
                           - payouts
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **11. Transaction ID Logic**
            
            Format:
            
            TX-YYYYMMDD-XXXX
            
            Payout ID:
            
            PT-YYYYMMDD-XXXX
            
            ---
            
            # **12. Tooling Overview**
            
            - **Stripe** (subscriptions, services, refunds)
            - **Supabase/AWS** (survey payout calculations)
            - **Webhook listeners** (renewals, failures)
            - **Internal logs** for adjustments
            - **Role-based access** (Admin only)
            
            ---
            
            # **13. Dummy Content (Designer)**
            
            ### **KPI Cards**
            
            ```
            MRR: £740
            Services Revenue (30d): £1,280
            Marketplace Revenue (30d): £420
            Pending Payouts: £88
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ### **Transactions Table Sample**
            
            ```
            Jan 04 — Owner 331 — Subscription Pro — £12 — Paid
            Jan 04 — Owner 221 — EPC Service — £89 — Paid
            Jan 03 — HH 332 — Survey Purchase SRV-2024… — £20 — Paid
            Jan 02 — Owner 004 — Subscription Pro — £12 — Failed
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ### **Payout Table Sample**
            
            ```
            PT-20250104-0021 — Owner 221 — £48 — Pending
            PT-20241231-0012 — HH 332 — £12 — Completed
            ```
            
            ---
            
            # **14. Rental Logic (Integrated)**
            
            Rentals contribute:
            
            - Subscription revenue (Owners)
            - Services revenue (photography / floorplan / sign)
            - Marketplace revenue when HH buys surveys on rentals too
            
            So **A8 supports BOTH Sale & Rent.**
            
            ---
            
            # **30-Second Dev Summary**
            
            A8 centralises **all financial operations**:
            
            - Stripe subscription + service sales
            - Survey marketplace revenue
            - Payouts
            - Failed payments
            - One dashboard for founders to see revenue health
            
            Admin can pay uploaders, check payments, and export reports.
            
            ---
            
        - **🧩  WF-A9 System Settings** **(Admin)**
            
            Central place for roles, language, legal, pricing config, and advanced controls.
            
            ---
            
            ## **1. Designer Checklist**
            
            - Layout = **simple, non-scary settings page**, split into clear sections with headings:
                - General
                - Roles & Permissions
                - Language & Regions
                - Pricing & Plans
                - Integrations (Keys)
                - Legal & Compliance
                - Advanced (Phase 2)
            - Use:
                - Standard Dashfolio+ form patterns
                - Toggles, dropdowns, text fields
                - Yalla Yellow **only** for:
                    - Save / Apply buttons
                    - Important warnings
            - No heavy visuals, no charts.
            - Emphasise readability and safety: clear labels, short helper text under each control.
            
            ---
            
            ## **2. Developer Checklist**
            
            System Settings must:
            
            - Be **role-protected**:
                - Only **Founder** and **Admin** roles see A9
                - Some sections (e.g. Feature Flags) → **Founder-only**
            - Persist to a system_settings (or similar) table with:
                - Versioning or last-edited log
                - Edited-by (admin id)
                - Updated-at timestamp
            - Use **safe defaults** if settings missing
            - Support multi-tenant or multi-region later
            - Be structured, not “free text JSON chaos”
            
            ---
            
            ## **3. Admin Journey (Short Summary)**
            
            Admin (or Founder) comes here to:
            
            - Manage who can log in and what they can see (roles)
            - Control language availability (UK first, DE later)
            - Set high-level pricing parameters (not every little thing)
            - Manage API keys for 3rd party tools (Stripe, WhatsApp, maps)
            - Ensure legal pages / policies are correctly linked
            - (Later) toggle features on/off as Yalla.House grows
            
            This is the **“control room”** for platform behaviour.
            
            ---
            
            ## **4. User Journey (Where This Page Sits)**
            
            ```
            Admin Login
             → A1 Dashboard
               → A9 System Settings (Founder/Admin only)
            ```
            
            Support staff **never** see A9.
            
            ---
            
            ## **5. Purpose**
            
            - Centralise **configuration** instead of scattering it across code or spreadsheets
            - Give Founders control without always needing a developer
            - Keep **roles, language, legal, and integration keys** in one place
            - Prepare the platform for **expansion (DE)** and **new features**
            
            ---
            
            ## **6. What This Page Should Solve**
            
            - Avoid “who has the Stripe key?” chaos
            - Avoid “we changed pricing in 3 places” problems
            - Make it easy to roll out Germany later
            - Ensure only the right people can see sensitive settings
            - Make audits and compliance easier (GDPR, legal links)
            
            ---
            
            ## **7. What the Designer Should Build in Framer**
            
            ### **SECTION A — General Settings**
            
            Fields (simple form):
            
            - Platform Name: Yalla.House
            - Default Country: UK (dropdown)
            - Default Currency: GBP £
            - Support Email: support@yalla.house
            - Support WhatsApp Link: https://wa.me/...
            
            ---
            
            ### **SECTION B — Roles & Permissions**
            
            Simple matrix-style list (not a full UI builder):
            
            - Roles:
                - Founder
                - Admin
                - Support
                - (Later) Partner, Contractor
            
            Each role with short description.
            
            No need for drag & drop; just a clear **read-only** overview + a small “Manage roles in Phase 2” note.
            
            ---
            
            ### **SECTION C — Language & Regions**
            
            MVP:
            
            - Primary Language: English (UK)
            - Region: United Kingdom
            - Toggle for Germany (Phase 2):
                - [ ]  Enable DE Region (Coming later)
            
            Helper text:
            
            > “MVP: UK only. Later: Germany / multi-language copy management.”
            > 
            
            ---
            
            ### **SECTION D — Pricing & Plans (High-Level Controls)**
            
            Not a full pricing CMS, but some basic settings:
            
            - Base subscription price (Owner Pro Plan) — e.g. £12 / month
            - Commission or margin on survey sales — e.g. 50% marketplace fee
            - Service defaults (info only; actual content on Pricing Page management later).
            
            This helps keep dev logic aligned with business expectations.
            
            ---
            
            ### **SECTION E — Integrations (Keys & IDs)**
            
            Fields with masked values:
            
            - Stripe Public Key / Secret Key
            - WhatsApp (Twilio) API Key
            - Email Provider API Key
            - Address Lookup API Key
            - (Phase 2) Rightmove / Zoopla API placeholders
            
            Designer: use **secure-looking input with “••••••” masking** and a small “Copy” icon.
            
            ---
            
            ### **SECTION F — Legal & Compliance**
            
            Links to:
            
            - Privacy Policy (URL selector)
            - Terms of Service (URL selector)
            - Cookie Policy (URL selector)
            - GDPR & Safety Statement (URL selector)
            - Imprint (DE only – URL)
            
            This section **does not** edit the pages themselves; it just defines which URLs are used in header/footer and emails.
            
            ---
            
            ### **SECTION G — Advanced (Phase 2 / Founder Only)**
            
            Simple toggles (disabled in MVP or just info):
            
            - Feature flags (read-only for now):
                - Survey Marketplace Live
                - Germany Region Enabled
                - Invite-only Mode
            - Audit Log viewer (link to separate admin-only tool page in future)
            
            ---
            
            ## **8. Developer Requirements**
            
            - Settings stored in one table, e.g. system_settings:
            
            ```
            {
              "platform_name": "Yalla.House",
              "default_country": "UK",
              "default_currency": "GBP",
              "support_email": "support@yalla.house",
              "roles": ["founder", "admin", "support"],
              "stripe_public_key": "***",
              "stripe_secret_key": "***",
              "whatsapp_api_key": "***",
              "email_api_key": "***",
              "address_lookup_api_key": "***",
              "legal": {
                "privacy_url": "...",
                "terms_url": "...",
                "cookie_url": "...",
                "gdpr_url": "...",
                "imprint_url": "..."
              },
              "pricing_defaults": {
                "owner_pro_monthly": 12,
                "survey_marketplace_split": 0.5
              }
            }
            ```
            
            - 
            - Must support:
                - GET /admin/settings (read)
                - POST /admin/settings or PATCH (update)
            - All changes logged in admin_audit_log
            - Sensitive fields masked in UI, never logged in clear text
            - Role gating: only founder + admin can access; some sections founder-only
            
            ---
            
            ## **9. KPI Definitions (Light-touch)**
            
            More like “config coverage” than business KPIs:
            
            | **KPI** | **Meaning** |
            | --- | --- |
            | Regions Enabled | e.g. 1 (UK) for MVP |
            | Languages Live | Currently 1 |
            | Active Integrations | Number of keys configured |
            | Last Settings Change | Helps track instability |
            | Who Last Edited | Accountability |
            
            ---
            
            ## **10. Logic & Impact**
            
            - Changing default currency → affects UI display (not Stripe currency logic yet)
            - Changing support email → used in:
                - Footers
                - Notifications
                - Support templates
            - Changing legal URLs → changes links in:
                - Footer
                - Header
                - Account-related emails
            - Feature flags (later) → guard entire routes/components.
            
            ---
            
            ## **11. ID & Versioning Logic**
            
            - Every settings update gets:
                - settings_version_id
                - updated_by_admin_id
                - updated_at
            
            Optional later:
            
            - Rollback to older version if needed.
            
            ---
            
            ## **12. Tooling Overview**
            
            - Uses same Admin UI stack as A1–A8
            - Forms validation on frontend + backend
            - No direct file uploads (links only)
            - For legal pages, tools like Notion/Framer/MDX used **outside** this screen, then linked here.
            
            ---
            
            ## **13. Dummy Content (for designer)**
            
            ```
            General
            - Platform Name: Yalla.House
            - Default Country: UK
            - Default Currency: GBP £
            - Support Email: support@yalla.house
            
            Language & Regions
            - Primary Language: English (UK)
            - Regions Enabled: United Kingdom
            - [ ] Germany (coming soon – disabled)
            
            Pricing & Plans
            - Owner Pro Plan: £12 / month
            - Survey Marketplace Split: 50% platform / 50% uploader
            
            Integrations
            - Stripe: ✅ Configured
            - WhatsApp: ✅ Configured
            - Email: ⚠️ Missing key
            - Address Lookup: ✅ Configured
            
            Legal & Compliance
            - Privacy Policy: /legal/privacy
            - Terms of Service: /legal/terms
            - Cookie Policy: /legal/cookies
            - GDPR & Safety: /legal/gdpr
            - Imprint (DE only): /legal/imprint-de
            ```
            
            ---
            
            ## **14. Rental Logic (Integrated)**
            
            Almost all of A9 is **agnostic** to Sale vs Rent.
            
            Important bit:
            
            - Regions / Legal must adapt when **Germany** and **rental regulations** come in.
            - Pricing & Plans may later have:
                - “Owner Pro – Sales”
                - “Owner Pro – Rent”
            - System Settings must be flexible enough to add another plan type later, but MVP only needs one.
            
            ---
            
            ### **⭐ 30-Second Dev Summary**
            
            WF-A9 is the **configuration brain** of Yalla.House:
            
            - Controls language, roles, legal URLs, support contacts, integration keys, basic pricing defaults.
            - Must be secure, audit-logged, founder/admin only.
            - Does not need fancy UI, just **reliable, clear forms**.
            - Prepares for Germany and for Phase-2-style feature flags.

            # **2️⃣ Content Blocks (Designer-ready)**
            
            ## **HERO SECTION**
            
            **Headline:**
            
            **Sell or rent your place without commission.**
            
            **Subheadline:**
            
            Transparent plans. No surprises. Pay only for what you need.
            
            **Primary CTA:**
            
            🔶 **List Your Place**
            
            ---
            
            # **3️⃣ The Three Packages (Simple + Strong)**
            
            ### **Package A — Self-Service (£0 + optional add-ons)**
            
            **Best for:** sellers confident to manage everything
            
            **Includes:**
            
            - Listing wizard
            - Professional listing on Yalla.House
            - Booking system
            - Inquiries dashboard
            - Buyer messaging
            - Add-on services available
            
            CTA: **List with Self-Service**

            - Published on Rightmove
            - Published on Zoopla
            - Phone routing
            - Enhanced analytics
            - Priority support
            
            CTA: **Boost My Listing**

            - 360° property scan
            - Professional photography
            - Floorplan included
            - “We manage your listing” setup
            - Signboard with QR code
            
            CTA: **Go Premium**

            - **🧩WF-P4-L1 — Privacy Policy (Stand-Alone Page)**
                
                # **Yalla.House Privacy Policy**
                
                *Last updated: 2025*
                
                (Version 1.0 — suitable for MVP launch, UK + EU compliant)
                
                ---
                
                # **1. Introduction**
                
                Welcome to **Yalla.House** (“we”, “us”, “our”).
                
                We provide a platform that helps Owners list places, Home-Hunters book viewings, send offers, communicate, and (optionally) access professional services.
                
                We take privacy extremely seriously. This Privacy Policy explains:
                
                - What personal data we collect
                - How and why we use it
                - When we share it
                - Your rights under GDPR
                - How to contact us
                
                If you have any questions, contact:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                ---
                
                # **2. Who We Are (Data Controller)**
                
                **Yalla.House Ltd**
                
                Registered in England & Wales
                
                Company No.: [Insert once formed]
                
                Registered Address: [Insert once formed]
                
                Email: **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                We are the **Data Controller** for all personal information processed through the platform.
                
                ---
                
                # **3. What Personal Data We Collect**
                
                We collect only the minimum necessary data for the platform to operate.
                
                ### **A. Account Data (Owner + Home-Hunter)**
                
                - Name
                - Email address
                - Phone number
                - Password (hashed — never readable by us)
                - Country
                - Login logs (IP truncated/anonymised)
                
                ### **B. Owner Data (when listing a place)**
                
                - Property address
                - Photos, floorplans, EPC
                - Listing details (price, type, description)
                - Availability for viewings
                - Messages exchanged with Home-Hunters
                
                ### **C. Home-Hunter Data (when interacting with listings)**
                
                - Viewing bookings
                - Buying position (cash / mortgage-ready / browsing)
                - Messages to Owners
                - Offers made
                - Uploaded documents (optional, for verified offers)
                
                ### **D. Surveys Marketplace Data**
                
                If participating:
                
                - Uploaded surveys
                - Survey purchase records
                - Payment history (processed by Stripe, not stored by us)
                
                ### **E. Usage Data (analytics-safe)**
                
                - Page interactions
                - Session counts
                - Device type (mobile/desktop)
                - Funnel performance (views → inquiries → viewings → offers)
                
                We do **not** use fingerprinting or invasive tracking.
                
                ---
                
                # **4. How We Use Personal Data**
                
                We use your personal data only for the following purposes:
                
                ### **Platform Functionality**
                
                - Create and manage user accounts
                - Display listings
                - Manage messages
                - Handle bookings
                - Facilitate offers
                
                ### **Payments**
                
                - Process payments through Stripe
                - Issue receipts and invoices
                
                ### **Security**
                
                - Prevent fraud
                - Detect unusual activity
                - Protect users and the platform
                
                ### **Communications**
                
                - Send booking confirmations
                - Send operational updates
                - Send reminders (viewing reminders, offer status, etc.)
                
                ### **Legal Compliance**
                
                - Accounting and tax requirements
                - Law enforcement requests (where legally required)
                
                ---
                
                # **5. Legal Basis for Processing**
                
                We process your data under the following bases:
                
                | **Purpose** | **Legal Basis (GDPR)** |
                | --- | --- |
                | Running your account, listings, bookings | Contract (Art. 6(1)(b)) |
                | Payments | Contract + Legal obligation |
                | Messaging | Legitimate interest |
                | Analytics | Legitimate interest (privacy-safe) |
                | Marketing emails (optional) | Consent |
                | Safety & fraud prevention | Legitimate interest |
                
                ---
                
                # **6. Sharing Your Data**
                
                We only share data with **essential service providers**:
                
                ### **A. Stripe (Payments)**
                
                - Processes subscription and service payments
                - We do NOT store card details
                
                ### **B. Twilio / WhatsApp**
                
                - Sends verification codes
                - Sends booking updates
                
                ### **C. Email Provider**
                
                - Sends confirmations and OTPs
                
                ### **D. Cloud Hosting (EU)**
                
                - Secure encrypted data storage
                
                ### **We NEVER:**
                
                ❌ Sell personal data
                
                ❌ Share data with advertisers
                
                ❌ Use third-party analytics that require personal data (e.g., Google Analytics with IP retention)
                
                ---
                
                # **7. International Transfers**
                
                If data leaves the UK/EU (rare), it is protected by:
                
                - Standard Contractual Clauses (SCCs)
                - UK International Data Transfer mechanisms
                - Approved safeguards
                
                ---
                
                # **8. Data Security**
                
                We apply industry-grade controls:
                
                - Encryption in transit (TLS 1.2+)
                - Encryption at rest
                - Strict role-based access controls
                - Admin 2FA (Phase 2)
                - Backup & recovery procedures
                - Annual penetration testing**
                
                ---
                
                # **9. Data Retention**
                
                We keep personal data only for the minimum period allowed.
                
                ### **Automatically deleted or anonymised:**
                
                | **Data Type** | **Retention** | **Notes** |
                | --- | --- | --- |
                | Account identity (deleted user) | Removed immediately | GDPR |
                | Listings (property data) | Retained | Non-personal |
                | Messages | Anonymised | Sender replaced by “deleted user” |
                | Viewing logs | Anonymised | For funnel metrics |
                | Offers | Anonymised | For price analytics |
                | Surveys marketplace records | 6 years | Required for accounting |
                | Payment records | 6 years | Required by HMRC |
                | Error logs | 90 days | Security |
                | Support requests | 12 months | Quality & auditing |
                
                ---
                
                # **10. Your GDPR Rights**
                
                You have full GDPR rights:
                
                ### **✔ Access**
                
                Request a copy of everything we hold.
                
                ### **✔ Correction**
                
                Fix inaccurate details.
                
                ### **✔ Deletion**
                
                Delete your account any time.
                
                ### **✔ Portability**
                
                Download your data in standard format.
                
                ### **✔ Restriction / Objection**
                
                Stop certain types of processing.
                
                ### **✔ Withdraw Consent**
                
                Stop marketing at any time.
                
                Contact:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                ---
                
                # **11. Cookies & Tracking**
                
                Yalla.House uses only essential cookies:
                
                ### **We do NOT use:**
                
                ❌ Tracking cookies
                
                ❌ Third-party advertising cookies
                
                ❌ Cross-site fingerprinting
                
                A separate **Cookie Policy** contains details.
                
                ---
                
                # **12. Children’s Data**
                
                We do not knowingly collect or process data from individuals under 16.
                
                Accounts belonging to minors are deleted upon detection.
                
                ---
                
                # **13. Changes to This Policy**
                
                We update this Privacy Policy when needed.
                
                When updates are significant, we will notify users via email.
                
                ---
                
                # **14. Contact**
                
                If you have concerns or requests:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                Or contact the UK ICO: https://ico.org.uk/
                
                ---
                
                # **✔ Privacy Policy Ready**
                
                Fully aligned with:
                
                - GDPR
                - Data Protection Act
                - Yalla.House’s data model
                - Marketplace, Owners, Home-Hunters, Surveys
                - Our plan to expand to Germany

                **Yalla.House — Terms of Service**

                ---
                
                # **1. Introduction**
                
                These Terms of Service (“Terms”) govern your access to and use of the **Yalla.House** platform (“the Platform”).
                
                By using Yalla.House, you agree to these Terms.
                
                If you do not agree, please do not use the Platform.
                
                ---
                
                # **2. Who We Are**
                
                **Yalla.House Ltd**
                
                Registered in England & Wales
                
                Company No.: **[Insert once formed]**
                
                Registered Address: **[Insert]**
                
                Email: **support@yalla.house**
                
                Yalla.House is a **technology service**, not an estate agent.
                
                We provide tools that allow:
                
                - Owners to list a place
                - Home-Hunters to book viewings
                - Users to communicate
                - Users to purchase optional property-related services
                
                We do **not** negotiate, represent, or act on behalf of buyers or sellers.
                
                ---
                
                # **3. What Yalla.House Is (and Is Not)**
                
                ### **✔ Yalla.House IS:**
                
                - A property listing platform
                - A scheduling tool
                - A messaging system
                - A document-handling and survey marketplace
                - A payment-enabled service hub (via Stripe)
                
                ### **❌ Yalla.House IS NOT:**
                
                - An estate agency
                - A legal advisor
                - A financial advisor
                - A surveyor or valuation service
                - A party to any sale, rent, or offer
                
                All agreements between Owner and Home-Hunter are **strictly between those parties**.
                
                ---
                
                # **4. Your Account**
                
                You must provide accurate and truthful information when creating an account.
                
                You are responsible for:
                
                - Keeping your account secure
                - All actions taken under your login
                - Not sharing your password or verification codes
                
                If suspicious activity is detected, Yalla.House may temporarily lock or close the account.
                
                ---
                
                # **5. Eligibility**
                
                To use the Platform, you must:
                
                - Be at least 18 years old
                - Have legal capacity to enter contracts
                - Use the Platform only for lawful purposes
                
                We may suspend accounts that violate these Terms.
                
                ---
                
                # **6. Services Provided**
                
                ## **A. For Owners**
                
                The Platform allows Owners to:
                
                - Create listings
                - Upload photos, floorplans, and documents
                - Receive inquiries
                - Manage viewings
                - Receive offers
                - Access paid services (e.g., photos, floorplans, EPCs)
                - Participate in the Survey Marketplace
                
                ## **B. For Home-Hunters**
                
                The Platform allows Home-Hunters to:
                
                - View listings
                - Book viewings
                - Send messages
                - Make offers
                - Upload documents (optionally)
                - Buy surveys where available
                
                ## **C. For All Users**
                
                The Platform includes:
                
                - Scheduling services
                - Messaging tools
                - Account dashboards
                - Survey marketplace
                - Identity verification (optional, Phase 2)
                
                ---
                
                # **7. Payments**
                
                Payments for subscription plans, service packages, or surveys are handled securely through:
                
                **Stripe Payments Europe Ltd**
                
                Yalla.House does not store or handle card details.
                
                ### **Refunds:**
                
                Refund eligibility depends on the service type:
                
                - **Subscriptions**: non-refundable once the billing period has started
                - **One-off services**: refundable only before work has begun
                - **Survey purchases**: non-refundable once unlocked
                
                Disputes must be raised via **support@yalla.house**.
                
                ---
                
                # **8. Messaging & Bookings**
                
                Users agree not to use the Platform to:
                
                - Harass, abuse, or threaten others
                - Send spam or promotional messages
                - Misrepresent their identity
                - Circumvent the Platform to avoid fees
                - Schedule fraudulent bookings
                
                We reserve the right to limit messaging access if abused.
                
                ---
                
                # **9. Offers & Transactions**
                
                Offers made through Yalla.House are **non-binding expressions of interest**.
                
                They do not form a legal contract.
                
                A final sale, tenancy, or agreement occurs **outside the Platform**, between:
                
                - Owner
                - Home-Hunter
                - Their respective lawyers/solicitors
                
                Yalla.House is not responsible for:
                
                - Contract negotiations
                - Accuracy of listings
                - Fraud between users
                - Failed deals
                - Resulting losses or damages
                
                ---
                
                # **10. User Responsibilities**
                
                ### **Owners must:**
                
                - Provide accurate listing information
                - Ensure they have authority to list the property
                - Keep availability up to date
                - Respond to inquiries promptly
                - Comply with local property laws and disclosures
                
                ### **Home-Hunters must:**
                
                - Provide truthful information when booking or offering
                - Attend scheduled viewings or cancel responsibly
                - Not abuse the survey marketplace
                - Comply with relevant laws (anti-money laundering, KYC, etc.)
                
                ---
                
                # **11. Third-Party Services**
                
                Your use of Yalla.House may rely on services provided by:
                
                - Stripe
                - Twilio / WhatsApp
                - Email providers
                - Mapping services
                - Surveyor providers
                - Hosting and analytics platforms
                
                Their terms apply separately.
                
                ---
                
                # **12. Content Ownership**
                
                ### **You retain ownership of:**
                
                - Photos
                - Listings
                - Surveys you upload
                - Messages
                - Documents
                
                ### **You grant Yalla.House a license to:**
                
                - Store
                - Display
                - Process
                - and transmit this content **for the purpose of running the Platform**
                
                We do not claim ownership of your material.
                
                ---
                
                # **13. Prohibited Activities**
                
                You may NOT use the Platform to:
                
                - Post misleading or fraudulent listings
                - Intentionally mis-price a place
                - Upload harmful files
                - Reverse-engineer the Platform
                - Attempt to bypass payment systems
                - Access accounts that are not yours
                - Conduct illegal activity

                ### **Yalla.House is NOT liable for:**
                
                - Loss of income
                - Missed deals
                - Incorrect listing information
                - User fraud
                - Property defects
                - Damages caused by relying on uploaded surveys
                - Downtime or data loss
                
                Total liability is capped at the amount paid by you to Yalla.House in the previous 12 months.

            - **🧩WF-P4-L3 Cookie Policy**
                
                # **Yalla.House — Cookie Policy**
                
                *Last updated: 2025*
                
                Version 1.0 — UK GDPR + PECR compliant
                
                ---
                
                ## **1. Introduction**
                
                This Cookie Policy explains how **Yalla.House Ltd** (“we”, “us”, “our”) uses cookies and similar technologies on our website and platform.
                
                We believe in **privacy-first design**.
                
                This means we use only the minimum cookies required for the website and platform to function.
                
                If you have questions, contact:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                ---
                
                ## **2. What Are Cookies?**
                
                Cookies are small text files stored on your device when you visit a website.
                
                They help websites remember:
                
                - your login session
                - your preferences
                - required technical functions
                
                Some cookies are strictly necessary. Others are optional.
                
                Yalla.House uses *almost no optional cookies*.
                
                ---
                
                ## **3. Types of Cookies We Use**
                
                ### **✔**
                
                ### **A. Strictly Necessary Cookies (Required)**
                
                These cookies are essential for the platform to work.
                
                We use them for:
                
                - session management
                - secure login
                - fraud prevention
                - message and booking functionality
                - Stripe payments
                
                You **cannot disable** these cookies because the platform will not function without them.
                
                Examples:
                
                - session_id
                - auth_token
                - csrf_token
                - Stripe payment cookies
                
                ### **✔**
                
                ### **B. Functional Cookies (Minimal Use)**
                
                Used to remember basic preferences, such as:
                
                - language preference
                - dashboard theme (Dashfolio+)
                
                These cookies **do not track** you across sites.
                
                Examples:
                
                - lang_pref
                - ui_theme
                
                ### **✔**
                
                ### **C. Analytics Cookies (Privacy-Safe Only)**
                
                We use **privacy-friendly, cookieless analytics** by default (e.g., Plausible).
                
                This means:
                
                - no personal data
                - no IP addresses
                - no cookies
                - no user-level tracking
                
                If we add optional cookies later (Phase 2), they will require consent.
                
                ### **❌**
                
                ### **D. No Advertising Cookies**
                
                We do **not** use:
                
                - Google Ads cookies
                - Facebook pixel
                - Remarketing trackers
                - Third-party behavioural profiling
                
                Zero advertising cookies.
                
                Zero cross-site tracking.
                
                ---
                
                ## **4. Third-Party Cookies**
                
                Some external providers place essential cookies:
                
                ### **✔ Stripe**
                
                Used for secure payments. Required by law for fraud protection.
                
                ### **✔ Twilio / WhatsApp**
                
                Used for login verification and operational messaging.
                
                ### **✔ Framer (if embedded components are used)**
                
                May set minimal functional cookies necessary for UI rendering.
                
                ---
                
                ## **5. Cookie Duration**
                
                | **Type** | **Duration** |
                | --- | --- |
                | Session cookies | Deleted when you close your browser |
                | Functional cookies | 30–180 days |
                | Stripe cookies | 12–24 months (PCI compliance) |
                | Analytics (cookieless) | N/A |
                
                ---
                
                ## **6. How to Control Cookies**
                
                You can control cookies through your browser:
                
                - Chrome: Settings → Privacy → Cookies
                - Safari: Preferences → Privacy
                - Firefox: Options → Privacy
                
                Blocking **strictly necessary cookies** will break the platform.
                
                ---
                
                ## **7. Legal Basis**
                
                Under GDPR + PECR:
                
                | **Cookie Type** | **Legal Basis** |
                | --- | --- |
                | Strictly necessary | Legitimate Interest |
                | Functional | Legitimate Interest |
                | Analytics | Legitimate Interest (cookieless) |
                | Advertising | Not used |
                
                ---
                
                ## **8. Updates to This Policy**
                
                We may update this Cookie Policy as our services evolve.
                
                Significant changes will be notified via email or platform notification.
                
                ---
                
                ## **9. Contact**
                
                For questions or concerns:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                📍 Address: [Insert when company formed]
                
                ---
                
            - **🧩WF-P4-L4 — GDPR & Safety (Stand-Alone Page)**
                
                # **GDPR & Safety Page**
                
                *Clear. Professional. Fully GDPR-compliant. Ready for your Legal Hub (WF-P4).*
                
                ---
                
                # **Yalla.House — GDPR & Safety Statement**
                
                *Last Updated: 2025*
                
                Version 1.0
                
                ---
                
                # **1. Introduction**
                
                At **Yalla.House**, safety and privacy are core values.
                
                We are committed to complying with:
                
                - UK GDPR
                - EU GDPR (for EU users)
                - Data Protection Act 2018
                - PECR
                - TMG §5 for Germany (when expanded)
                
                This page summarises:
                
                - How we protect your data
                - How we secure communication
                - How we verify users (optional)
                - How surveys and documents are handled
                - What safety controls exist for Owners and Home-Hunters
                
                This page does **not replace** the Privacy Policy — it complements it.
                
                ---
                
                # **2. Who We Are**
                
                **Data Controller:**
                
                Yalla.House Ltd
                
                Registered in England & Wales
                
                Company No.: **[Insert once formed]**
                
                Address: **[Insert]**
                
                Email: **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                ---
                
                # **3. Data Minimisation**
                
                We only collect the minimum data required to provide the service.
                
                ### **We do NOT collect:**
                
                - unnecessary personal data
                - behavioural tracking across websites
                - advertising identifiers
                - sensitive data (ethnicity, religion, health, etc.)
                
                ### **We ONLY process:**
                
                - Account info
                - Listing info
                - Booking + offer info
                - Messages
                - Optional documents for verification (Phase 2)
                - Surveys
                
                Nothing more.
                
                ---
                
                # **4. Data Security**
                
                We use industry-grade protection:
                
                ### **Technical Measures**
                
                ✔ Encryption in transit (TLS 1.2+)
                
                ✔ Encryption at rest
                
                ✔ Database access control
                
                ✔ Passwords hashed with bcrypt
                
                ✔ Regular backups
                
                ✔ Isolated production environment
                
                ✔ Monitoring and anomaly detection
                
                ### **Organisational Measures**
                
                ✔ Role-based access (Support sees less than Admin)
                
                ✔ No external contractors get direct DB access
                
                ✔ Mandatory 2FA for Admins (Phase 2)
                
                ✔ Annual penetration testing (Phase 2)
                
                ---
                
                # **5. Your Rights Under GDPR**
                
                You have full control of your data:
                
                - Access
                - Correction
                - Deletion
                - Restriction
                - Portability
                - Objection
                - Withdraw consent
                
                To exercise your rights:
                
                📧 **privacy@yalla.house**
                
                ---
                
                # **6. Data Retention (How Long We Keep Data)**
                
                We follow strict GDPR-compliant retention limits:
                
                | **Data Type** | **Retention** | **Notes** |
                | --- | --- | --- |
                | Account data | Until deletion | Deleted when account removed |
                | Listings | Permitted indefinitely | Not personal data |
                | Messages | Anonymised after deletion | Sender replaced with “deleted user” |
                | Viewings | Anonymised | For platform analytics |
                | Offers | Anonymised | For pricing metrics |
                | Surveys | 6 years | Required for financial compliance |
                | Payments | 6 years | HMRC regulation |
                | Logs | 90 days | Security only |
                
                Full matrix already provided separately.
                
                ---
                
                # **7. Surveys & Document Safety**
                
                The Survey Marketplace requires special handling.
                
                ### **When Owners Upload Surveys**
                
                - Stored encrypted
                - Reviewed manually (no sensitive personal data allowed)
                - Made available only when purchased
                - Access is logged for security
                
                ### **When Home-Hunters Upload Documents**
                
                (e.g., proof of funds / ID verification, optional Phase 2)
                
                - Only visible to the Owner after approval
                - Auto-deletion after the offer completes or 90 days
                - Never shared with third parties
                
                ---
                
                # **8. Messaging & Communication Safety**
                
                Messages inside Yalla.House are:
                
                - Encrypted in transit
                - Logged only for safety
                - Monitored for abuse using automated detection
                - Not accessible by non-admin staff
                
                Abusive behaviour results in account restriction or removal.
                
                ---
                
                # **9. Viewing Safety (Physical Safety)**
                
                For Owners & Home-Hunters:
                
                ### **We strongly recommend:**
                
                - Not sharing full personal details before a viewing
                - Always attending viewings in pairs when concerned
                - Using the platform’s messaging system (not private numbers)
                - Cancelling suspicious bookings
                - Reporting abusive users via **support@yalla.house**
                
                Yalla.House may suspend accounts for unsafe behaviour.
                
                ---
                
                # **10. Fraud Prevention**
                
                We apply multiple fraud controls:
                
                - Suspicious-activity detection
                - Rate-limited messaging
                - Identity verification (Phase 2 optional)
                - Document verification for serious offers
                - Monitoring for survey abuse
                - Manual review of flagged activity
                
                ---
                
                # **11. Data Transfers**
                
                Data is stored in the UK/EU.
                
                If transferred abroad, it is protected by:
                
                - Standard Contractual Clauses
                - UK Addendum
                - Approved security measures
                
                We never transfer data to unsafe jurisdictions.
                
                ---
                
                # **12. Children’s Safety**
                
                The platform is **not for users under 16**.
                
                We delete any detected minor accounts.
                
                ---
                
                # **13. Contact & Complaints**
                
                📧 privacy@yalla.house
                
                Or contact the UK ICO: https://ico.org.uk/
                
                ---
                
            
            ---

---

- **GDPR DELETION WORKFLOW**
    
    ### **Developer Implementation Guide + Legal Logic**
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 0. Trigger Events (when deletion starts)**
    
    Deletion begins when ONE of these happens:
    
    1. **User clicks “Delete Account”**
    2. **User submits GDPR deletion request via Support**
    3. **Admin initiates a deletion (verified request)**
    4. **Automatic deletion trigger** (e.g., 24 months inactivity — optional later)
    
    → The workflow must start with a **2-step confirmation** to avoid accidental deletions.
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 1. Identify User + Run Pre-Check**
    
    Before deleting, the system must:
    
    ### **1. Verify identity**
    
    - Login required OR
    - Email confirmation code
    - Admin request requires supervisor approval (Phase 2)
    
    ### **2. Check dependencies**
    
    ```
    IF user has live listing → Block deletion
    IF user has an active subscription → Block deletion
    IF user has open financial transactions → Block deletion (legal)
    IF user has pending dispute → Block deletion (legal)
    ```
    
    System returns:
    
    > “You must unpublish your listing first.”
    > 
    
    > “You have an active Stripe subscription.”
    > 
    
    > “There is an unresolved payment.”
    > 
    
    If nothing prevents deletion → continue.
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 2. PERSONAL DATA DELETION PROCESS**
    
    Yalla.House deletes **identity-linked data**, but keeps **analytics**, **property data**, and **pricing data** (anonymised).
    
    ### **Developer rule:**
    
    > Delete anything that identifies the person.
    > 
    
    > Keep anything that describes the property.
    > 
    
    ### **2.1 Delete Account Identity**
    
    - Name
    - Email
    - Phone number
    - Profile info
    - Buyer position
    - KYC fields
    - Communication preferences
    
    ➡ **Fully delete (hard delete)**
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 3. Delete OWNER personal data**
    
    > Only personal data is deleted.
    > 
    
    > Property data stays (legal + strategic advantage).
    > 
    
    ### **Delete (personal):**
    
    - Owner name from listing
    - Owner phone/email
    - Owner preferences
    - Owner message history (or anonymise)
    - Owner calendar preferences
    
    ### **Retain (allowed + important):**
    
    - Address
    - Photos (unless containing person)
    - Floorplans
    - EPC
    - Property description
    - Property size/type
    - Price history → **retain but anonymise source**
    - Viewing stats
    - Offer history → anonymise
    - Survey marketplace metadata
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 4. Delete HOME-HUNTER personal data**
    
    ### **Delete:**
    
    - Identity (name/email/phone)
    - Saved places (or unlink user ID)
    - Inbox messages (or anonymise sender)
    - Offers → anonymise (keep number & price)
    - Viewings → anonymise (keep aggregation only)
    
    ### **Retain:**
    
    - Market interest signals (anonymous)
    - Survey purchases → **keep for 6 years** (legal) but remove name
    - Analytics (views, clicks, funnels)
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 5. Clean SYSTEM DATA (Logs + Billing)**
    
    ### **Keep (required):**
    
    - Stripe invoices → 6 years (HMRC law)
    - Payment history → 6 years
    - Survey marketplace payouts → 6 years
    - Audit logs → 12 months
    
    ### **Delete:**
    
    - Authentication logs older than 12 months
    - Webhook error logs older than 90 days
    - Session cookies
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 6. ANONYMISATION RULES**
    
    Anything used for analytics must be **unlinkable** to a real person.
    
    ### **Replace user ID with:**
    
    ```
    anon_user_82df90c
    ```
    
    Or:
    
    ```
    buyer_deleted
    ```
    
    ### **Fields to strip:**
    
    - IP address
    - Email hash
    - Any ID used across systems
    - Any message content
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 7. SYSTEM-WIDE CASCADE DELETE**
    
    This is the technical heart.
    
    When a user is deleted:
    
    ```
    DELETE FROM Users WHERE user_id = X
    
    UPDATE Listings SET owner_id = NULL WHERE owner_id = X
    UPDATE Listings SET owner_contact = NULL WHERE owner_id = X
    
    UPDATE Messages SET sender_id = NULL, sender_name = 'deleted user'
    UPDATE Viewings SET user_id = NULL
    UPDATE Offers SET user_id = NULL
    UPDATE Surveys SET buyer_id = NULL
    ```
    
    Everything else (property data, market analytics) remains untouched.
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 8. CONFIRMATION & EXPORT**
    
    Before final deletion:
    
    ### **Step A — Offer export:**
    
    User can download ALL personal data:
    
    - Messages
    - Offers
    - Bookings
    - Account info
    
    > GDPR requires this (Art. 20 — “Right to portability”).
    > 
    
    ### **Step B — Confirm deletion:**
    
    > “Your account will be permanently deleted in 7 days.”
    > 
    
    ### **Step C — Final purge:**
    
    After **7-day grace period**:
    
    - All personal data destroyed
    - All links severed
    - Anonymous data kept
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 9. POST-DELETION NOTICES**
    
    - Show confirmation page
    - Send final deletion email
    - Log deletion event in audit logs (12 months)
    
    ---
    
    # **🔹 10. Internal Requirement**
    
    This workflow must be replicated in:
    
    ✔ Admin Panel → “Delete User (GDPR-safe)”
    
    ✔ Support Inbox → “Process GDPR Request”
    
    ✔ Auto-process in backend
    
    ---
    
    # 
    
- **Big-Picture System Architecture**
    
    ```jsx
                    ┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
                    │               CLIENT LAYER              │
                    ├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
                    │  A) Public Web (Framer + Dashfolio+)    │
                    │     - Home / Services / About / Legal   │
                    │     - Public Property Page (WF-O5)      │
                    │                                         │
                    │  B) Owner Workspace (Framer)            │
                    │     - Dashboard (WF-O1)                 │
                    │     - My Listings (WF-O2)               │
                    │     - Inquiries (WF-O3)                 │
                    │     - Calendar (WF-O4)                  │
                    │                                         │
                    │  C) Home-Hunter Workspace (Framer)      │
                    │     - HH Dashboard / Inbox / Saved      │
                    │     - Booking flow (WF-H1+)             │
                    │                                         │
                    │  D) Admin Console (Framer / Internal)   │
                    │     - A1–A9 Admin Screens               │
                    └─────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                      │
                                      │ HTTPS / JSON (REST or GraphQL)
                                      ▼
            ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │                    APPLICATION LAYER                      │
            ├───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
            │  API Gateway / Backend (Node.js / Nest / similar)         │
            │                                                           │
            │  • Auth Service                                           │
            │  • Owner Service (Listings, Surveys, Billing refs)        │
            │  • Home-Hunter Service (Saved Places, Offers, Surveys)    │
            │  • Messaging Service (Inquiries, threads)                 │
            │  • Booking & Calendar Service                             │
            │  • Survey Marketplace Service                             │
            │  • Billing & Plans Service (Stripe integration)           │
            │  • Integrations Hub (Rightmove/Zoopla/OTM – Phase 2)     │
            │  • Notifications Service (Email + WhatsApp)               │
            │  • Admin/Reporting Service                               │
            │                                                           │
            │  (MVP) minimal services: Auth, Owner, HH, Messaging,      │
            │        Booking, Billing, Notifications, Admin-lite        │
            └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                      │
                                      │ Internal service calls / queues
                                      ▼
            ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
            │                          DATA LAYER                       │
            ├───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
            │  1. PRIMARY APP DATABASE (SQL – e.g. Postgres)            │
            │     • Users (Owner, Home-Hunter, Admin)                   │
            │     • Places (Listings)                                   │
            │     • Viewings / Bookings                                │
            │     • Inquiries / Messages                               │
            │     • Offers                                             │
            │     • Surveys (metadata)                                 │
            │     • Subscriptions / Plans (Stripe IDs)                 │
            │                                                           │
            │  2. FILE STORAGE (Object Store – e.g. S3 / GCS)           │
            │     • Photos                                             │
            │     • Floorplans                                         │
            │     • EPC PDFs                                           │
            │     • Survey PDFs                                        │
            │                                                           │
            │  3. ANALYTICS STORE (Warehouse / events DB)              │
            │     • Anonymised events (views, clicks, funnels)         │
            │     • Channel attribution (RM, Zoopla, Signboard, etc.)  │
            │     • Revenue + cost metrics (owner-level & global)      │
            └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                      │
                         ┌────────────┴────────────┐
                         ▼                         ▼
            ┌───────────────────────────┐ ┌─────────────────────────────┐
            │  EXTERNAL INTEGRATIONS    │ │  OBSERVABILITY & SECURITY   │
            ├───────────────────────────┤ ├─────────────────────────────┤
            │ • Stripe (billing)        │ │ • Logging (app + audit)     │
            │ • WhatsApp / Twilio       │ │ • Error tracking             │
            │ • Email provider          │ │ • Performance monitoring     │
            │ • Maps / Geocoding        │ │ • Access logs / admin 2FA   │
            │ • Rightmove / Zoopla /    │ │ • GDPR deletion workflows    │
            │   OnTheMarket (Phase 2)   │ │   (personal vs analytics)    │
            └───────────────────────────┘ └─────────────────────────────┘
    
    ```
    
    - **Big-picture diagram (ASCII)**
        
        ```
                        ┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
                        │               CLIENT LAYER              │
                        ├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
                        │  A) Public Web (Framer + Dashfolio+)    │
                        │     - Home / Services / About / Legal   │
        ```
