        ```
                        │     - Booking flow (WF-H1+)             │
                        │                                         │
                        │  D) Admin Console (Framer / Internal)   │
                        │     - A1–A9 Admin Screens               │
                        └─────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                          │
                                          │ HTTPS / JSON (REST or GraphQL)
                                          ▼
                ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
                │                    APPLICATION LAYER                      │
                ├───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
                │  API Gateway / Backend (Node.js / Nest / similar)         │
                │                                                           │
                │  • Auth Service                                           │
                │  • Owner Service (Listings, Surveys, Billing refs)        │
                │  • Home-Hunter Service (Saved Places, Offers, Surveys)    │
                │  • Messaging Service (Inquiries, threads)                 │
                │  • Booking & Calendar Service                             │
                │  • Survey Marketplace Service                             │
                │  • Billing & Plans Service (Stripe integration)           │
                │  • Integrations Hub (Rightmove/Zoopla/OTM – Phase 2)     │
                │  • Notifications Service (Email + WhatsApp)               │
                │  • Admin/Reporting Service                               │
                │                                                           │
                │  (MVP) minimal services: Auth, Owner, HH, Messaging,      │
                │        Booking, Billing, Notifications, Admin-lite        │
                └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                          │
                                          │ Internal service calls / queues
                                          ▼
                ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
                │                          DATA LAYER                       │
                ├───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
                │  1. PRIMARY APP DATABASE (SQL – e.g. Postgres)            │
                │     • Users (Owner, Home-Hunter, Admin)                   │
                │     • Places (Listings)                                   │
                │     • Viewings / Bookings                                │
                │     • Inquiries / Messages                               │
                │     • Offers                                             │
                │     • Surveys (metadata)                                 │
                │     • Subscriptions / Plans (Stripe IDs)                 │
                │                                                           │
                │  2. FILE STORAGE (Object Store – e.g. S3 / GCS)           │
                │     • Photos                                             │
                │     • Floorplans                                         │
                │     • EPC PDFs                                           │
                │     • Survey PDFs                                        │
                │                                                           │
                │  3. ANALYTICS STORE (Warehouse / events DB)              │
                │     • Anonymised events (views, clicks, funnels)         │
                │     • Channel attribution (RM, Zoopla, Signboard, etc.)  │
                │     • Revenue + cost metrics (owner-level & global)      │
                └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
                                          │
                             ┌────────────┴────────────┐
                             ▼                         ▼
                ┌───────────────────────────┐ ┌─────────────────────────────┐
                │  EXTERNAL INTEGRATIONS    │ │  OBSERVABILITY & SECURITY   │
                ├───────────────────────────┤ ├─────────────────────────────┤
                │ • Stripe (billing)        │ │ • Logging (app + audit)     │
                │ • WhatsApp / Twilio       │ │ • Error tracking             │
                │ • Email provider          │ │ • Performance monitoring     │
                │ • Maps / Geocoding        │ │ • Access logs / admin 2FA   │
                │ • Rightmove / Zoopla /    │ │ • GDPR deletion workflows    │
                │   OnTheMarket (Phase 2)   │ │   (personal vs analytics)    │
                └───────────────────────────┘ └─────────────────────────────┘
        ```
        
    - **Data Flow (Quick Owner + Home-Hunter Story)**
        
        ### **Owner Flow (simplified)**
        
        1. **Owner hits “List Your Place” on Header**
            
            → goes to WF-O2 “New Place” wizard (Step 1 Basics).
            
        2. Fills postcode, address, listing type → Backend Owner Service creates draft place + listing.
        3. Continues through Price / Extras → data saved into primary DB.
        4. Hits “Publish” → Listing visible on Public Property Page (WF-O5).
        5. Views funnel + channel breakdown on WF-O1 Dashboard (via Analytics Store).
        6. Gets bookings → Booking Service writes viewings, Messaging Service starts threads.
        7. Upgrades to a higher package → Stripe subscription → Billing Service → Admin A8 sees it.
        
        ### **Home-Hunter Flow (simplified)**
        
        1. Sees listing on Rightmove → clicks “More Info / Book a Viewing” → lands on WF-O5.
        2. Chooses slot → Booking Service creates viewing, auto-confirms if slot free.
        3. Receives WhatsApp + email confirmation with link to create account (optional).
        4. If they create account → they see:
            - “Upcoming Viewings”
            - “Saved Places”
            - “My Offers”
        5. They can buy a survey → Survey Marketplace Service + Stripe + Surveys DB.
        
        ### **Admin Flow (simplified)**
        
        1. Logs into Admin console.
        2. Sees A1 Dashboard:
            - Active listings, active users, channel performance.
        3. Clicks A2 User Detail → sees per-user metrics, lifetime value, success rate.
        4. A4 Integrations shows any broken feeds (portals, WhatsApp, email).
        5. A6 Tasks & Fulfilment – signboard orders, EPC to schedule, manual actions.
        6. A7 Surveys – verify new uploads, approve payouts.
        
        ---
        
        If you like, next step could be:
        
        - **“Developer Execution Plan v2”**: concrete tasks based on this architecture (what to build first, second, third), or
        - A **simplified “one-slide” version** for pitching / freelancers.
        
        Tell me if you’d like **Dev Plan**, **Pitch Slide**, or **Both**.
        
    - **Component list (with MVP vs Phase 2 flags)**
        
        ### **CLIENT LAYER**
        
        **Public Web (Framer, Dashfolio+)**
        
        - **MVP**:
            - Home, Services & Pricing, About, Legal Hub, Support
            - Public Property Page (WF-O5) with “Arrange a Visit” + “Message Owner”
        - **Phase 2**:
            - Blog/SEO content
            - Market reports (data product later)
        
        **Owner Workspace (Sidebar + Header frozen)**
        
        - Dashboard (WF-O1) – KPIs + funnels + source pie chart
        - My Listings (WF-O2) – listing table + “New Place” wizard
        - Inquiries (WF-O3) – unified inbox
        - Calendar (WF-O4) – slots for open house & 1:1 viewings
        - Account Settings (via WF-ACC)
        
        **Home-Hunter Workspace**
        
        - HH Dashboard (H1/H8) – upcoming visits, saved places, offers
        - Inbox (H2) – messaging with Owners / system
        - Saved Places & Offers (H3/H5 merged funnel)
        - Surveys (H4/H6) – list purchased & available surveys
        - Account Settings (WF-ACC shared)
        
        **Admin Console**
        
        - A1 Dashboard – global KPIs + alerts
        - A2 User Detail View – Owners & HH metrics combined
        - A3 Owners & HH lists
        - A4 Integrations & Status (Stripe, WhatsApp, email, portals)
        - A5 Support Inbox
        - A6 Tasks & Fulfilment (signboards, EPC, photos, etc.)
        - A7 Surveys Marketplace Oversight
        - A8 Billing & Revenue
        - A9 System Settings (roles, language, feature flags – Phase 2 heavy)
        
        ---
        
        ### **APPLICATION LAYER (Backend Services)**
        
        You don’t have to build microservices from day 1; this can be **one monolith with clear modules**.
        
        **1. Auth & Identity Service (MVP)**
        
        - Login/logout, password reset
        - Role: Owner / Home-Hunter / Admin
        - Future: 2FA, KYC hooks
        
        **2. Owner Service (MVP)**
        
        - CRUD for Places (listings)
        - New Place “wizard” flow (O2 4-step progress)
        - Status changes (Draft, Live, Under Offer, Sold, Let)
        - Owner KPIs aggregation for Dashboard
        
        **3. Home-Hunter Service (MVP)**
        
        - Saved Places
        - Offers
        - Viewing booking history
        - Survey purchase references
        
        **4. Messaging Service (MVP)**
        
        - Threads: Owner ↔ Home-Hunter
        - Status: New, Replied, Archived, Offer-related
        - GDPR deletion → anonymise sender
        
        **5. Booking & Calendar Service (MVP)**
        
        - Owner time slots (open house vs 1:1)
        - Booking confirmation logic:
            - Default = auto-confirm if slot is free
            - Owner reschedule → triggers message + new slot suggestion
        - Integration with Google Calendar (Phase 2)
        
        **6. Survey Marketplace Service (Phase 1 lite, Phase 2 full)**
        
        - Upload / verify / price surveys
        - Owners: attach survey to place, set profit share
        - Home-Hunters: browse / unlock survey
        - Admin: A7 oversight + payouts
        
        **7. Billing & Plans Service (MVP)**
        
        - Stripe customer + subscription IDs
        - Track which Owner has which plan + one-off services
        - Expose data to Admin A8 and Owner Billing/Settings
        
        **8. Integrations Hub (Phase 2)**
        
        - Rightmove / Zoopla / OnTheMarket feeds
        - Direction:
            - Owner → we push listing
            - Portals → click/call leads → we track channel
        - Signboard QR routing (channel = “Signboard”)
        
        **9. Notifications Service (MVP)**
        
        - Email: booking confirmations, reminders, account events
        - WhatsApp: links to WF-O5/H1 for bookings
        - Configurable in WF-ACC (notifications section)
        
        **10. Admin/Reporting Service (MVP → Phase 2)**
        
        - Aggregates data for A1/A8
        - Owner/HH-level metrics for A2/A3
        - Global funnels + channel performance
        
        ---
        
        ### **DATA LAYER**
        
        **Primary App DB (e.g. Postgres)**
        
        - users (roles, locale, notification prefs)
        - places (non-personal property data)
        - listings (status + owner link)
        - viewings (bookings, slots)
        - messages
        - offers
        - surveys (metadata)
        - subscriptions / invoices (with Stripe IDs, not card data)
        
        **File Storage**
        
        - Put all files under structured prefixes:
            - /places/{placeId}/photos/...
            - /places/{placeId}/docs/epc.pdf
            - /surveys/{surveyId}.pdf
        
        **Analytics Store (Events)**
        
        - Separate from primary DB
        - Events: VIEW_PLACE, CLICK_BOOK, CREATE_OFFER, SURVEY_PURCHASED
        - Fields: timestamp, placeId, channel, device, *anonymised userId*
        - Used for Owner Dashboard, Admin Analytics, future data products.
        
        ---
        
        ### **INTEGRATIONS**
        
        **Stripe (MVP)**
        
        - Subscriptions: Package A/B/C monthly
        - One-off services: photos, EPC, signboards, survey unlock
        - Webhooks into Billing Service and Admin A8.
        
        **WhatsApp (via Twilio or similar)**
        
        - Owner: booking notifications
        - Home-Hunter: booking confirmation + reschedule links
        - Support: “Message us on WhatsApp” from public pages
        
        **Email Provider**
        
        - Transactional emails (SendGrid/Postmark etc.)
        
        **Maps/Geocoding**
        
        - Convert postcode/address to map location & region stats
        - Power WF-O5 map + location info.
        
        **Portals (Phase 2)**
        
        - Rightmove / Zoopla / OTM feed handler
        - Channel tracking for Owner Dashboard + Admin.
    1. **How data flows (Owner / Home-Hunter / Admin)**

    ## 
    
- **Developer Execution Plan v2**
    
    
    ---
    
    - 
    
- 1. **Services & Surveys End-to-End Flow Diagram**
    
    
- Visual Flow Diagram
    
    Below is a **combined Owner + Home-Hunter journey map**, using:
    
    - **Owner WFs**: O1–O5
    - **Home-Hunter WFs**: H1–H5
    - Plus the shared public page (WF-O5) and shared data (Place, Viewing, Offer, Survey, Messages).
    
    You can paste this straight into Notion under **“1. Product → Journey Maps → Combined Owner + Home-Hunter”**.
    
    ---
    
    ## **1. Swimlane Overview – Owner vs Home-Hunter vs System**
    
    ### **Legend**
    
    - **O#** = Owner Wireframes
    - **H#** = Home-Hunter Wireframes
    - **Public** = no login, anyone
    - **Shared Objects** = Place, Viewing, Inquiry/Message, Offer, Survey
    
    ---
    
    ### **🧑‍💼 OWNER LANE (SELLER)**
    
    ```
    [1] Owner signs up / logs in
        → O1 — Dashboard
    
    [2] Creates first Place
        → O2 — My Listings (first-time flow)
        - Address, type, price, tenure, photos
        - Status: Draft → Live
    
    [3] Listing goes live
        → O2 + O1
        - O1 shows KPIs (views, inquiries, upcoming viewings)
        - O2 shows Live status
    
    [4] Public Property Page active
        → O5 — Public Property Page
        - Link shared to portals, WhatsApp, QR sign board
    
    [5] Buyer activity flows in:
        - New inquiries
        - Viewing requests
        - Offers (later phase)
    
        → O3 — Inquiries (Owner Messaging Hub)
        → O4 — Calendar (Owner Viewings Manager)
        → O1 — Dashboard KPIs update
    
    [6] Owner reviews offers + interest
        → O3 / O1
        - Sees buyers, their position and verification status
        - Compares offers, messages, behaviour
    
    [7] Owner accepts offer / agrees next steps
        → O3 / O1
        - Marks offer as accepted (Phase 2)
        - Starts sales process with chosen buyer
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### **🧑‍🧑 HOME-HUNTER LANE (BUYER)**
    
    ```
    [1] Discovers listing
        - Rightmove / Zoopla / OnTheMarket
        - QR on sign
        - Direct Yalla link
        → O5 — Public Property Page (Public)
    
    [2] From O5, can:
        - Arrange a Visit
        - Message Owner
        - Make an Offer (if ready)
        - Save Place
    
        This creates a temporary buyer profile (token-based).
    
    [3] Lands in H1 — Visit & Messages
        - Sees booked visit (if arranged)
        - Sees thread with Owner
        - Call-to-actions:
          - Make Offer
          - Unlock/Upload Survey
          - View Full Property Page (back to O5)
    
    [4] Sidebar becomes active (Home-Hunter Workspace):
        - H2 — Activity (all viewings + messages)
        - H3 — My Places (Saved → Seen → Booked → Visited → Offer Made)
        - H4 — My Surveys (Upload / Unlock / Earn)
        - H5 — Account & Verification (Trusted Buyer Profile)
    
    [5] If they book more viewings / message more owners:
        - H2 collects all viewings + inbox
        - H3 tracks all places (Yalla + external)
    
    [6] If they want to make an offer:
        - Start on H1 (Make Offer)
        - If not verified → H5 (Account & Verification)
        - After verification → offer saved + shown:
          - To Owner: via O3 / O1
          - To Buyer: via H3 (Offer Made column)
    
    [7] If they commission a survey:
        - Upload in H4
        - Decide if others can unlock (cashback)
        - Other buyers see survey on O5 + H1
        - Buyer can later see earnings on H4
    
    [8] They continue hunting:
        - Use H3 as “Home-Hunting Cockpit”
        - Use H2 as “Day-to-day Activity”
        - Use H5 to stay “Trusted Buyer”
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### **🧠 SYSTEM / SHARED OBJECTS LANE**
    
    ```
    PLACE
    - Created + edited in O2 — My Listings
    - Displayed to public in O5
    - Referenced in all H-pages (H1, H2, H3, H4)
    
    VIEWINGS
    - Created when HH books on O5 / H1
    - Managed by Owner in O4
    - Shown to HH in H1 + H2 + H3
    
    INQUIRIES / MESSAGES
    - Created when HH messages from O5 or H1
    - Owner side: O3 — Inquiries
    - Buyer side: H1 (thread) and H2 (Inbox)
    
    OFFERS (Phase 2)
    - Created from H1 or H3
    - Buyer side: tracked in H3
    - Owner side: viewed in O3 + surfaced in O1
    
    SURVEYS
    - Uploaded by HH in H4
    - Attached to Place
    - Exposed on O5 and H1 as “Survey available”
    - Unlocks generate survey transactions
    
    VERIFICATION / “TRUSTED BUYER”
    - Stored on H5
    - Status influences:
      - Owner view of buyer in O3 / O1
      - Offer priority / labelling
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **2. High-Level Combined Journey (Condensed Version)**
    
    You can use this as the **top summary block** in Notion:
    
    ```
    1. Owner lists a Place (O2) → goes Live → O5 becomes public.
    2. Home-Hunters discover the Place via external portals / QR / links → O5.
    3. From O5, they:
       - Arrange a Visit → H1 → H2/H3 later
       - Message Owner → H1 → O3 for Owner
       - Make an Offer → H1 + H5 for verification
    4. Owner monitors all activity:
       - O1 Dashboard → KPIs, offers, viewings
       - O3 Inquiries → messages + buyer info
       - O4 Calendar → viewings schedule
    5. Home-Hunter uses:
       - H1 → property-specific workspace
       - H2 → all viewings + messages
       - H3 → “My Places” funnel across all properties
       - H4 → surveys upload/unlock
       - H5 → Trusted Buyer Profile (verification)
    6. Offers and surveys flow between both sides:
       - Owner sees structured offers and survey insights
       - Home-Hunters get organised search + cashback opportunities
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **3. How to Position This for a Designer / Dev**
    
    If you want one sentence per role:
    
    - **Owner POV:**
        
        “I list once, Yalla funnels all serious buyers into one clean dashboard where I can see viewings, messages, and verified offers.”
        
    - **Home-Hunter POV:**
        
        “I can finally keep track of all the places I like (even from other portals), my viewings, my messages, my offers, and even reuse surveys — all in one place.”
        
    - **System POV:**
        
        “Everything pivots around the Place and H1/O5. Owner WFs manage supply, Home-Hunter WFs manage demand, and shared objects (viewings, offers, surveys, messages) sit in between.”

- • **Admin Sitemap** (3–5 pages max for MVP)
    
    ---
    
    # **ADMIN SITEMAP — MVP (3–5 Pages)**
    
    *“Everything internal staff needs to see, fix or unblock — nothing more.”*
    
    ---
    
    # **A1 — Admin Dashboard (Platform Overview)**
    
    **Purpose:** Quick internal pulse of the entire platform.
    
    ### **Sections:**
    
    - **Live Places:** number of active listings
    - **New Signups:** last 7 days (Owners / Home-Hunters)
    - **Today’s Viewings:** count + quick access
    - **New Inquiries:** last 24h
    - **New Surveys:** last 7 days
    - **Abuse / Flagged Content** (if any)
    - **System Health:** API uptime / error logs (simple)
    
    ### **Why this page matters:**
    
    Fast way for support/admin to spot issues before users notice.
    
    ---
    
    # **A2 — Places Manager (All Listings)**
    
    **Purpose:** Admin view across *all* properties + ability to intervene.
    
    ### **Table Columns:**
    
    - Place ID
    - Address / Title
    - Owner Name + Email
    - Type (Sale / Rent)
    - Status (Draft / Live / Under Offer / Sold / Let Agreed)
    - Created Date
    - Actions:
        - **View Public Page**
        - **View Owner Workspace (read-only)**
        - **Suspend / Unsuspend Listing**
    
    ### **Admin Actions:**
    
    - Suspend listing (fraud / violation)
    - Mark as “flagged” (needs review)
    - Edit title/photo (only for emergencies)
    
    ---
    
    # **A3 — Users Manager (Owners + Buyers)**
    
    **Purpose:** Central directory of all users for support + safety.
    
    ### **Tabs:**
    
    ✔ **Owners**
    
    ✔ **Home-Hunters**
    
    ✔ **Admins**
    
    ### **Columns:**
    
    - User ID
    - Name
    - Email
    - Role (Owner/Home-Hunter/Admin)
    - Verification status (Home-Hunter only)
    - 
        
        # **of Places (Owner)**
        
    - 
        
        # **of Offers Made (Buyer)**
        
    - 
        
        # **of Surveys Uploaded (Buyer)**
        
    - Actions:
        - **Open user in read-only mode**
        - **View their places / viewings**
        - **Temporarily block account**
        - **Reset password (force email reset)**
    
    ### **Why this page matters:**
    
    Support + fraud mitigation + recovery tool.
    
    ---
    
    # **A4 — Viewings & Messages Monitor**
    
    **Purpose:** One page where admin can see all live activity in case of disputes, harassment, or support tickets.
    
    ### **Sections:**
    
    ### **A4.1 — All Viewings List**
    
    - Viewing ID
    - Place
    - Buyer Name
    - Date/Time
    - Status (Requested/Confirmed/Cancelled)
    - Actions:
        - **Edit** (reschedule)
        - **Cancel** (owner/home-hunter request)
    
    ### **A4.2 — All Inquiries & Messages**
    
    - Inquiry ID
    - Place
    - Owner
    - Buyer
    - Last Message
    - Status (New/Replied/Archived)
    - Action:
        - **Open thread (read-only)**
    
    *(Admin can only read, not send messages.)*
    
    ### **Why this page matters:**
    
    Protect users and solve issues instantly.
    
    ---
    
    # **A5 — Surveys Moderation**
    
    **Purpose:** Control the quality and safety of uploaded surveys.
    
    ### **Table:**
    
    - Upload ID
    - Place
    - Buyer who uploaded
    - Date uploaded
    - File size / type
    - Public visibility (yes/no)
    - Earnings to date
    - Status: Approved / Rejected / Pending
    
    ### **Actions:**
    
    - **Approve**
    - **Reject** (with reason)
    - **Force-hide**
    - **Download** for review
    
    ### **Why this page matters:**
    
    Ensures no fraudulent or dangerous files get shared.
    
    ---
    
    # **Minimal But Powerful MVP**
    
    This admin sitemap is intentionally:
    
    - **small** (5 pages max)
    - **high leverage** (touches all key flows)
    - **easy to build** (most views = read-only tables)
    - **secure** (admin sees everything, but can edit very little)
    - **scalable** (can expand to “Offers Manager”, “Transactions”, etc.)
    
    ---
    
    # **🔐 Role Permissions (Admin)**
    
    - Can view **all data** (read-only except where explicitly editable)
    - Can suspend listings
    - Can block users
    - Can approve survey uploads
    - Cannot message users on their behalf
    - Cannot spoof buyer/owner (no impersonation in MVP)

    ### **✔ Admin Wireframe A2**
    
    ### **✔ Admin Wireframe A3**
    
    ### **✔ Admin Wireframe A4**
    
    ### **✔ Admin Wireframe A5**
    
    All in the **same structured format** as the Owner + HH WFs.

    ### **✔ Developer Summary for Admin features**

    Which one do you want next?
    
- • **1-page “Admin Brief for Developers**
- • **WF-A1: Platform Overview (Admin Dashboard)** in the same style as O1/H1
- **Yalla.House — Product Pitch (Designer/Developer Version)**
    
    *“The platform where Owners list once, and Home-Hunters get fully organised. Zero agents. Zero chaos. ”Yalla.House is the control center for selling — and the cockpit for home-hunting. Where owners manage everything effortlessly, and home-hunters finally stay organised. (or so..)* 
    
    ---
    
    ## **For Owners (Sellers / Landlords)**
    
    Owners get a **command center** where everything about their listing is automated and organised:
    
    - **One place to manage** their listing (photos, price, documents)
    - **All inquiries in one inbox**, no matter if buyers come from Rightmove, Zoopla, QR signs, WhatsApp or email
    - **Auto-synced viewing calendar** with smart slots (private + group viewings)
    - **Real-time KPIs:** views, inquiries, booking rate, offer rate
    - **Buyer intelligence:** see buyer type (Cash / Mortgage Ready / Browsing), their viewed/visited history, plus verification level
    - **Private messaging hub** (no personal phone number exposed)
    - **Clear offer management** (Phase 2): compare offers, timestamps, buyer readiness
    
    **Owner Experience:**
    
    *“I listed my place once, and Yalla organized all buyers, viewings, messages, and offers for me. No agent needed.”*
    
    ---
    
    ## **For Home-Hunters (Buyers / Tenants)**
    
    Home-Hunters finally get a **proper workspace** — something portals and estate agents don’t give them:
    
    ### **A. H1: Property Workspace**
    
    When clicking a listing (from Rightmove/Zoopla, or QR sign), the Home-Hunter lands in a clean, mobile-first page where they can:
    
    - Arrange a Visit
    - Ask a Question
    - Save the Place
    - Start an Offer
    - Upload/View Surveys
    - Navigate back to full Public Page
    
    ### **B. H2: Activity (Calendar + Messages)**
    
    All viewings and all conversations in one place — across all properties.
    
    ### **C. H3: My Places (Shopping Funnel)**
    
    A funnel that tracks the whole journey:
    
    **Saved → Seen → Booked → Visited → Offer Made → Accepted (future)**
    
    (They can even track **external** properties they saw elsewhere.)
    
    ### **D. H4: Surveys**
    
    A world-first feature:
    
    - Upload your paid survey
    - Others can unlock it
    - Get cashback if your survey is reused
    
    ### **E. H5: Trusted Buyer Profile**
    
    Upload ID, proof of funds, mortgage-in-principle, and be labelled as:
    
    🟢 **Cash Buyer**
    
    🟡 **Mortgage Ready**
    
    🟣 **In Progress**
    
    🟤 **Browsing Only**
    
    Owners see this directly.
    
    **Home-Hunter Experience:**
    
    *“Finally I can keep track of my search, my viewings, my offers, and my surveys. No more chaos.”*
    
    ---
    
    # **Where both sides meet**
    
    Everything flows through the **Public Property Page (WF-O5)**:
    
    - Mobile-first
    - Strong CTAs: *Arrange Visit*, *Message Owner*, *Save*
    - Time slots generated by Owner’s calendar
    - Survey visibility
    - Similar places
    - Map, photos, docs
    
    The page is always accessible to both roles.
    
    ---
    
    # **Why This Works**
    
    Yalla.House solves chaos on both ends:
    
    ### **⭐ Owners**
    
    Don’t want 40 WhatsApp messages, agent calls, no-shows, and duplicated questions.
    
    ### **⭐ Home-Hunters**
    
    Are exhausted by:
    
    - losing track of places
    - dealing with flaky agents
    - repeating the same questions
    - unclear offer processes
    - surveys that become worthless when an offer fails
    
    ### **⭐ The Platform (System)**
    
    Unifies everything behind **one data model**:
    
    - Place
    - Viewing
    - Inquiry/Message
    - Offer
    - Survey
    - Buyer Profile
    
    All pages are just different lenses on these 6 objects.
    
    ---
    
- **High-Level Architecture**
    
    ---
    
    **Architecture style:**
    
    - Web app (Framer/React front-end)
    - Backend API (REST or GraphQL)
    - Relational DB (Postgres/MySQL)
    - Object storage for files (surveys, docs, photos)
    - Optional: Background worker / queue for async tasks (emails, reminders, payouts)
    
    ### **Core domains**
    
    1. **Identity & Accounts**
    2. **Places & Listings**
    3. **Home-Hunter Activity (Viewings, Messages, Offers)**
    4. **Surveys & Earnings**
    5. **Analytics & Events**
    6. **Integrations (Calendar, Portals, Payments, Email/SMS/WhatsApp)**
    7. **i18n & Settings**
    
    ---
    
    ## **2. Core Services / Modules**
    
    ### **2.1 Auth & Identity Service**
    
    - Handles:
        - Owner accounts
        - Home-Hunter accounts
        - Temporary token sessions for buyers (no full account yet)
    - Features:
        - Email + password / magic link
        - Token-based access to WF-H1 (“visit & messages” without login)
        - Role management: owner, homeHunter, admin
    - Later:
        - Social login (Google, Apple)
        - Multi-factor auth (optional)
    
    ---
    
    ### **2.2 Place & Listing Service**
    
    **Objects:**
    
    - Place (core property object)
    - Listing (portal-specific representation if needed later)
    - PlaceMedia (photos, floorplans)
    - PlaceDocs (EPC, title docs, etc.)
    
    **Owner-facing pages:**
    
    - O2 — My Listings (create, edit, draft/live)
    - O5 — Public Property Page (read-only public)
    
    **Responsibilities:**
    
    - Create / update / delete Place (by Owner)
    - Status transitions: draft → live → under_offer → sold (or rental equivalents)
    - Attach media and documents
    - Expose public read API for WF-O5
    - Provide “summary view” for dashboards (O1 & H3)
    
    ---
    
    ### **2.3 Home-Hunter Activity Service**
    
    This is where most of the “demand side” lives.
    
    **Objects:**
    
    - BuyerProfile (Home-Hunter profile)
    - BuyerPlaces (relationship of buyer ↔ place; stores funnel state)
    - Viewing
    - Inquiry
    - Message
    - Offer (Phase 2+)
    
    **Pages:**
    
    - H1 — Visit & Messages (property context)
    - H2 — Activity (all viewings + global inbox)
    - H3 — My Places (Saved → Seen → Booked → Visited → Offer Made)
    
    **Responsibilities:**
    
    - Manage viewing lifecycle:
        - requested → confirmed → completed / cancelled
    - Manage messaging threads:
        - Internal chat between Buyer and Owner
    - Maintain Home-Hunter funnel:
        - Auto-set seen when user opens O5/H1
        - saved, booked, visited, offer_made based on actions
    - Offer submission:
        - Store amount, status, link to BuyerProfile + Place
        - Integrate with verification data (from H5)
    
    ---
    
    ### **2.4 Surveys Service**
    
    **Objects:**
    
    - SurveyReport
    - SurveyTransaction
    
    **Pages:**
    
    - H4 — My Surveys
    - Integrated into:
        - O5 — Public Property Page (Survey card)
        - H1 — Visit & Messages (Survey CTA)
    
    **Responsibilities:**
    
    - Store uploaded survey PDFs securely
    - Link surveys to Place + uploader (BuyerProfile)
    - Handle unlock/paywall:
        - Only allow access if user purchased or is Owner
    - Revenue share:
        - Track earnings for uploader
        - Track platform revenue
    
    **Later:**
    
    - Automatic redaction pipeline
    - Duplicate detection (per Place)
    
    ---
    
    ### **2.5 Verification / “Trusted Buyer Profile” Service**
    
    **Objects:**
    
    - BuyerVerification (ID, proof of address, proof of funds, MiP)
    - BuyerSettings (notifications, language, etc.)
    
    **Page:**
    
    - H5 — Account & Verification
    
    **Responsibilities:**
    
    - Store document metadata (secure URLs)
    - Maintain verification score / completion %
    - Provide “Verification snapshot” to:
        - Owner views (O3 Inquiries, O1 Dashboard offers)
        - Offer ranking logic
    
    ---
    
    ### **2.6 Analytics & Events Service**
    
    No heavy BI for MVP, but:
    
    **Objects:**
    
    - Event (generic table for tracking: view, save, inquiry, booking, offer, survey unlock)
    - Aggregated stats per:
        - Place
        - Owner
        - Buyer (optional)
    
    **Responsibilities:**
    
    - Feed Owner dashboard (O1 KPIs):
        - Views
        - Inquiries
        - Viewings
        - Offers
    - Optionally feed:
        - Price comparison
        - “Interest level” on O5 (view count, saves, etc.)
    
    ---
    
    ### **2.7 Integrations Service**
    
    **Calendar**
    
    - Owner side: O4 — Calendar
    - Buyer side: H2/H1 — “Add to calendar”
    - MVP: generate iCal + Google Calendar link
    - Later: true sync with Google/Microsoft APIs
    
    **Email / SMS / WhatsApp**
    
    - Send:
        - Viewing confirmations
        - Message notifications
        - Offer updates
        - Survey unlock receipts
    - Critical: include magic link tokens to WF-H1/H2
    
    **Payments**
    
    - Stripe for:
        - Survey unlocks
        - Future: owner packages, premium buyer tools
    
    **Portals (future)**
    
    - Export listings to Rightmove / Zoopla / OTM
    - Simple: feed/cron job or manual upload in early MVP
    
    ---
    
    ### **2.8 i18n & Language Support**
    
    Cross-cutting concern:
    
    - All UI strings: language keys (e.g. hh.activity.title)
    - Store chosen language on:
        - BuyerSettings
        - OwnerSettings
    - API responses can be language-agnostic (IDs, enums), UI handles translation
    - URLs remain mostly English; text is localised
    
    ---
    
    ## **3. Core Data Model (Condensed)**
    
    ### **Identity**
    
    ```
    User {
      id
      role: 'owner' | 'homeHunter' | 'admin'
      email
      phone
      passwordHash (if password mode)
      createdAt
    }
    
    BuyerProfile {
      id
      userId?         // null if token-only MVP
      name
      email
      phone
      buyingPosition  // enum: cash, mip, in_progress, browsing
      createdAt
    }
    
    OwnerProfile {
      id
      userId
      name
      email
      phone
      companyName?
    }
    ```
    
    ### **Places & Listings**
    
    ```
    Place {
      id
      ownerId
      title
      address
      postcode
      lat
      lng
      type          // flat, house, etc.
      listingType   // sale, rent
      status        // draft, live, under_offer, sold, let_agreed
      price         // for sale or rent
      currency
      tenure?       // freehold, leasehold, etc.
      createdAt
    }
    
    PlaceMedia {
      id
      placeId
      type         // photo, floorplan, epc
      url
      order
    }
    
    PlaceDoc {
      id
      placeId
      type         // epc, title_deed, etc.
      url
      isPublic
    }
    ```
    
    ### **Buyer Activity**
    
    ```
    BuyerPlace {
      id
      buyerProfileId
      placeId?       // null for external
      externalUrl?
      status         // saved, seen, booked, visited, offer_made
      notes
      rating
      createdAt
    }
    
    Viewing {
      id
      placeId
      buyerProfileId
      startTime
      endTime
      type          // private, group
      status        // requested, confirmed, completed, cancelled
      createdAt
    }
    
    Inquiry {
      id
      placeId
      buyerProfileId
      status        // new, replied, archived, has_viewing, has_offer
      createdAt
    }
    
    Message {
      id
      inquiryId
      senderType    // owner, buyer, system
      body
      createdAt
    }
    
    Offer {
      id
      placeId
      buyerProfileId
      amount
      currency
      status        // pending, accepted, rejected, withdrawn
      createdAt
    }
    ```
    
    ### **Surveys**
    
    ```
    SurveyReport {
      id
      placeId
      uploaderBuyerId
      type          // homebuyer, structural, valuation, other
      surveyedAt
      fileUrl       // secure
      isPublic      // true = can be purchased
      earningsToDate
      createdAt
    }
    
    SurveyTransaction {
      id
      surveyId
      buyerProfileId
      amount
      currency
      createdAt
    }
    ```
    
    ### **Verification**
    
    ```
    BuyerVerification {
      buyerProfileId
      idDocumentUrl?
      addressProofUrl?
      proofOfFundsUrl?
      mortgageMIPUrl?
      solicitorName?
      solicitorEmail?
      solicitorPhone?
      verificationScore   // 0–100
      updatedAt
    }
    
    BuyerSettings {
      buyerProfileId
      language
      notifyMessages
      notifyViewings
      notifyOffers
      notifyMarketing
    }
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ## **4. Frontend Routing Thoughts**
    
    You can standardise routes like:
    
    - Public:
        - /place/:placeId → WF-O5 (Public Property Page)
    - Owner:
        - /owner/dashboard → O1
        - /owner/places → O2
        - /owner/inquiries → O3
        - /owner/calendar → O4
    - Home-Hunter:
        - /visit/:token → H1 (Visit & Messages)
        - /hh/activity → H2
        - /hh/places → H3
        - /hh/surveys → H4
        - /hh/account → H5
    
    Tokens for WF-H1/H2 should encode or look up:
    
    - buyerProfileId
    - placeId
    - viewingId (optional)
    - expiry
    
    ---
    
    ## **5. Event Flow Examples (MVP)**
    
    ### **5.1 Booking a Viewing**
    
    1. User on /place/:placeId (O5) clicks **Arrange Visit**
    2. Form collects: name, email, phone, buying position, slot
    3. Backend:
        - Creates BuyerProfile (or reuses existing)
        - Creates Viewing
        - Creates/updates BuyerPlace status = booked
        - Sends email/SMS with magic link → /visit/:token
    4. Owner side:
        - viewings appear in O4
        - O1 KPIs update (viewings count)
    
    ---
    
    ### **5.2 Sending a Message**
    
    1. From O5 or H1, user writes message
    2. Backend:
        - Finds or creates Inquiry
        - Adds Message
        - Updates Inquiry.status = 'new' or 'replied'
        - Notifies Owner via email/SMS
    3. Owner responds from O3
    4. Buyer sees reply in H1/H2
    
    ---
    
    ### **5.3 Uploading a Survey**
    
    1. From H1/H4, user uploads PDF
    2. Backend:
        - Stores file in object store
        - Creates SurveyReport (with placeId and uploaderBuyerId)
        - Optionally marks isPublic = true for unlock
    3. On O5/H1:
        - API indicates surveyAvailable = true
        - UI shows “Unlock Survey” tile
    
    ---
    
    ## **6. MVP vs Phase 2 (Tech Side)**
    
    **MVP:**
    
    - Core services:
        - Identity
        - Places
        - Viewings & Inquiries & Messages
        - Basic BuyerPlaces funnel
        - Surveys (file upload, manual share, simple unlock)
    - Integrations:
        - Email
        - SMS/WhatsApp via one provider
        - iCal export for calendar
    - Basic analytics:
        - Per-place counters
    
    **Phase 2+:**
    
    - Offers + ranking by verification
    - Full survey monetisation with automated payouts
    - Real calendar sync (Google/Microsoft)
    - Portal feeds (Rightmove/Zoopla/OTM integration)
    - More advanced analytics dashboards
    - Auction mode / transparent offer logic
    - Multi-currency + Germany localisation
    
    ---
    
- **System Overview / Wireframes & UX**
    
    ### 🔄 Global Implementation Notes (Post-Architecture Alignment)
    
    These apply across all existing wireframes and do **not** replace them – they clarify how everything connects technically.
    
    1. **Channels Tracking (Global)**
        - Every public entry point (Rightmove, Zoopla, OTM, QR sign, Yalla direct, Social) must be tracked as a `channel` on:
            - property page visits
            - inquiries
            - viewing bookings
            - offers
        - Used by Admin Analytics (WF-A1, WF-A9).
    2. **Events & Analytics (Global)**
        - Key events emitted:
            - `owner_signup`, `place_created`, `place_published`, `viewing_booked`, `offer_made`, `deal_done`,
            `survey_uploaded`, `survey_purchased`, `subscription_started`, `subscription_cancelled`.
        - Owner / Home-Hunter wireframes don’t change visually – they just **emit events** for Admin analytics.
    3. **Billing Hooks (Global)**
        - All money flows through the Billing Service (Stripe) + Costs (Airtable).
        - Owner-side pages (O1–O4) **never compute money themselves** – they just:
            - show “plan name”, features, and success/failure state
            - call billing endpoints when a plan or add-on is chosen.
        - Admin Billing (WF-A8) is the **source of truth** for revenue, costs, and profit.
    4. **Survey Marketplace (Global)**
        - Public Property Page (WF-O5) only shows:
            - “Survey available”
            - price
            - CTA → purchase.
        - All logic (approval, pricing, payouts, analytics) lives in:
            - WF-A6 (Admin) + Billing + Analytics.
    5. **Viewing Logic (Global)**
        - All bookings (owner or Home-Hunter side) create a `viewing` record.
        - Group vs private slots handled at backend level; UI only reflects availability.
        - Viewings feed:
            - Owner Calendar (WF-O4)
            - Home-Hunter calendar
            - Admin analytics (WF-A1, WF-A9)
            - Support Inbox (WF-A7) when issues occur.
    6. **Home-Hunter Workspace (Global Summary)**
        - Home-Hunter has:
            - My Viewings (past & upcoming)
            - My Saved Places
            - My Offers
            - My Documents / Verification
            - My Surveys (if purchased)
        - Admin Buyer Detail (WF-A5) is the mirror view of this data for Admin/Founder.
- generate a **glossary of all entities and endpoints**.
- Page descriptions
- Terminology system
- **Global Language Support**
    
    > “For MVP we ship English-only, but follow this spec so we can add German, etc. later without rewriting the product.”
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ## **🌍 Global Language Support — MVP i18n Standard**
    
    **Goal for MVP:**
    
    - **UI language:** English only
    - **Architecture:** Fully ready for future German / other languages
    - **Principle:** *No hard-coded UI text. English translation files are the master source of truth.*
    
    ---
    
    ### **1. MVP i18n Principles**
    
    1. **English-only UI (for now)**
        - All screens, hints, errors, buttons in English.
        - No visible language toggle yet.
    2. **All UI text must come from translation files**
        - Use files like:
            - /locales/en.json (required)
            - /locales/de.json (optional / partial for later)
        - Components call a translate function:
            - t("dashboard.kpis.views")
            - t("owner.myListings.title")
    3. **Database stays language-neutral**
        - Enums and internal values are always in English tech form:
            - status = "live", "draft", "under_offer"
            - source = "yard_sign", "yalla_direct"
        - UI maps these values to human labels via translation keys:
            - owner.listingStatus.live → “Live” (later “Aktiv”)
            - analytics.source.yard_sign → “Yard Sign” (later “Schild vor dem Haus”)
    4. **Store locale, even if we only use English now**
        - Add locale to Owner model, e.g. en-GB, de-DE.
        - MVP default: en-GB for everyone.
        - Later: use it for formatting + language switching.
    5. **Locale-aware formatting for numbers, dates, and currency**
        - Prices and dates must be formatted via helper functions, not manually:
            - formatPrice(value, currency, locale)
            - formatDate(value, locale)
        - This avoids pain later when adding de-DE.
    6. **Validation and error messages also use translation keys**
        - No hard-coded "This field is required" etc.
        - Use keys like:
            - validation.required
            - validation.invalidPrice
    
    ---
    
    ### **2. MVP i18n Developer Tasks**
    
    **Task 1 — Add locale to Owner**
    
    - Add field Owner.locale (string).
    - Default: en-GB on sign-up.
    - No UI toggle needed for MVP.
    
    ---
    
    **Task 2 — Set up translation infrastructure**
    
    - Add translation files:
        - /locales/en.json — must contain all production strings.
        - /locales/de.json — can be empty / partial for now.
    - Implement t(key) helper to read from these files.
    - All new UI components must use t(key) for visible text.
    
    ---
    
    **Task 3 — Enforce “no hard-coded UI text” rule**
    
    - Any visible string in components (labels, titles, CTAs, error messages, tooltips, chart legends) must come from t(key).
    - Code reviews should reject new hard-coded English strings in JSX/TSX.
    
    ---
    
    **Task 4 — Enum → label mapping via i18n**
    
    - For fields like status, source, eventType, map database values to UI labels using translation keys:
        - Example keys:
            - owner.listingStatus.live
            - owner.listingStatus.draft
            - analytics.source.yard_sign
            - analytics.eventType.view
    - Never store translated strings in database or events.
    
    ---
    
    **Task 5 — Locale-aware formatting helpers**
    
    - Implement helpers:
        - formatPrice(value, currency, locale)
        - formatNumber(value, locale)
        - formatDate(value, locale)
    - All price/number/date outputs in Dashboard, Listings, Analytics must use these helpers.
    
    ---
    
    **Task 6 — MVP Translation File Template**
    
    Example /locales/en.json (short):
    
    ```
    {
      "dashboard.viewsBySource.title": "Where your views are coming from",
      "dashboard.kpis.views": "Views",
      "dashboard.kpis.inquiries": "Inquiries",
      "dashboard.kpis.viewings": "Viewings",
      "dashboard.kpis.offers": "Offers",
      "owner.myListings.title": "My Listings",
      "owner.dashboard.header.onlineSince": "Online since {{value}}",
      "analytics.source.yard_sign": "Yard Sign",
      "analytics.source.yalla_direct": "Direct",
      "validation.required": "This field is required"
    }
    ```
    
    Example /locales/de.json (can be partial, later):
    
    ```
    {
      "dashboard.viewsBySource.title": "Woher Ihre Aufrufe kommen"
    }
    ```
    
    Everything else falls back to English until fully translated.
    
    ---
    
    ### **3. MVP i18n Quick Checklist (for every feature)**
    
    Before a feature is “done”, developer must confirm:
    
    - No hard-coded UI strings — everything uses t(key).
    - All new keys added to /locales/en.json.
    - Database enums remain English technical values.
    - Prices, numbers, dates use formatting helpers.
    - Feature works with locale = "en-GB" today.
    - It will not break when /locales/de.json gets filled later.
    
    ---
    
- Navigation structures (headers + sidebars)
- User journeys (booking, inquiry, offer)
- Permission matrix (which role sees what)
    
    ---
    
    ## **Permission Matrix — Roles & Access (MVP)**
    
    This matrix defines **who can see and do what** across the system for MVP.
    
    It covers four main roles:
    
    - **Owner** – lists and manages places.
    - **Home-hunter** – searches, inquires, books viewings, sends offers/applications.
    - **Admin** – internal Yalla.House control.
    - **Public Visitor** – not logged in, just browsing the public property page.
    
    This applies to:
    
    - **Owner Workspace** (WF-O1–O4)
    - **Public Property Page** (WF-O5)
    - Future: Home-hunter Workspace & Admin Workspace.
    
    ---
    
    ### **1. Roles Overview**
    
    | **Role** | **Description** |
    | --- | --- |
    | Owner | Person who lists a place for sale or rent. Has access to the Owner Workspace (Dashboard, My Listings, Inquiries, Calendar, Settings). |
    | Home-hunter | Person interested in finding a place. Can browse public listings and send inquiries. Later: has their own workspace. |
    | Admin | Internal Yalla.House / NoAgent staff. Can assist Owners, moderate content, and see aggregated analytics. |
    | Public Visitor | Not logged in. Can browse public listings and send a basic inquiry. |
    
    ---
    
    ### **2. High-Level Permission Matrix (By Area)**
    
    ### **2.1 Owner Workspace Pages**
    
    | **Area / Page** | **Owner** | **Home-hunter** | **Admin** | **Public Visitor** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | **WF-O1 — Dashboard** | ✅ Full access (own data) | ❌ No access | ✅ View all Owners’ dashboards (optional Phase 2) | ❌ No access |
    | **WF-O2 — My Listings** | ✅ Create / edit own places | ❌ No access | ✅ View / edit any place | ❌ No access |
    | **WF-O3 — Inquiries** | ✅ See & reply to inquiries for own places | ❌ No access | ✅ See & assist with any inquiry (support role) | ❌ No access |
    | **WF-O4 — Calendar** | ✅ Manage viewings for own places | ❌ No access | ✅ View / adjust events (with Owner consent) | ❌ No access |
    | **Settings (Owner)** | ✅ Own account only | ❌ No access | ✅ Limited admin view (billing, status) | ❌ No access |
    
    ---
    
    ### **2.2 Public-Facing Property Page (WF-O5)**
    
    | **Action / Element** | **Owner** | **Home-hunter** | **Admin** | **Public Visitor** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | View public property page | ✅ (own & preview) | ✅ (all public places) | ✅ (any place) | ✅ |
    | View price, beds, size, description | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ |
    | View EPC, floorplan (public docs only) | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ | ✅ |
    | View Owner contact details (email/phone) | ❌ Shown only inside Owner workspace | ❌ No direct Owner email/phone | ❌ No direct | ❌ No direct |
    | Send inquiry (contact owner) | N/A | ✅ (via form) | N/A | ✅ (via form, basic) |
    | Book viewing (request) | N/A | ✅ (if enabled) | N/A | ✅ (if enabled) |
    
    > Note:
    > 
    > 
    > **Owner**
    > 
    
    ---
    
    ### **3. Entity-Level Permissions**
    
    Below is a **more detailed view per entity**, matching the data model we defined (Place, Inquiry, Message, BuyerProfile, etc.).
    
    ### **3.1**
    
    ### **Owner**
    
    ### **Entity**
    
    | **Action** | **Owner** | **Home-hunter** | **Admin** | **Public Visitor** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Create Owner account | ✅ (self-signup) | ❌ | ✅ (backoffice) | N/A |
    | View own profile | ✅ | ❌ | ✅ (limited) | ❌ |
    | Edit own profile | ✅ | ❌ | ✅ (limited: e.g. suspend account) | ❌ |
    
    ---
    
    ### **3.2**
    
    ### **Place**
    
    ### **(Listing)**
    
    | **Action** | **Owner** | **Home-hunter** | **Admin** | **Public Visitor** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Create new place | ✅ Own only | ❌ | ✅ (assist Owner) | ❌ |
    | Edit place details (address, price, etc.) | ✅ Own places only | ❌ | ✅ Any place | ❌ |
    | Upload media/documents for place | ✅ Own places only | ❌ | ✅ (support) | ❌ |
    | Change status (Draft/Live/Under Offer) | ✅ Own places only | ❌ | ✅ (with Owner consent) | ❌ |
    | View in Owner Workspace | ✅ Own places only | ❌ | ✅ All places | ❌ |
    | View on public page (WF-O5) | ✅ (preview + live) | ✅ If status = public | ✅ | ✅ If status = public |
    
    ---
    
    ### **3.3**
    
    ### **Inquiry**
    
    | **Action** | **Owner** | **Home-hunter** | **Admin** | **Public Visitor** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Create inquiry (send message) | ❌ | ✅ (via public page or workspace) | ❌ (only on behalf of someone) | ✅ (via public page) |
    | View inquiry | ✅ Own places only | ✅ Own inquiries only (future workspace) | ✅ Any inquiry | ❌ |
    | Reply to inquiry | ✅ For own places | ✅ (reply to Owner in their thread) | ✅ Assist Owner/Buyer | ❌ |
    | Change inquiry status (new/replied/etc.) | ✅ For own inquiries (on own places) | ❌ | ✅ Any inquiry | ❌ |
    | See buyer contact (email, phone) | ✅ For inquiries on own places | ✅ See own email/phone | ✅ As needed for support | ❌ |
    
    ---
    
    ### **3.4**
    
    ### **Message**
    
    | **Action** | **Owner** | **Home-hunter** | **Admin** | **Public Visitor** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Send message | ✅ (inside WF-O3) | ✅ (via inquiry/conversation) | ✅ (if acting as support) | ❌ |
    | View messages in a thread | ✅ For inquiries on own places | ✅ For own inquiries | ✅ For any inquiry (support) | ❌ |
    | Mark as read | ✅ Own view only | ✅ Own view only | ✅ (for moderation tools) | ❌ |
    
    ---
    
    ### **3.5**
    
    ### **BuyerProfile**
    
    ### **&**
    
    ### **BuyerInteractionStatus**
    
    | **Action** | **Owner** | **Home-hunter** | **Admin** | **Public Visitor** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | View basic buyer info (name, email, phone) | ✅ For buyers who inquired on own places | ✅ See own details only | ✅ For support / moderation | ❌ |
    | Favourite buyer (place-specific) | ✅ Via WF-O3 | ❌ | ✅ (for support, if needed) | ❌ |
    | Block buyer (place-specific) | ✅ Via WF-O3 | ❌ | ✅ (override / unblock) | ❌ |
    
    ---
    
    ### **3.6**
    
    ### **TrafficEvent**
    
    ### **(Analytics / Tracking)**
    
    | **Action** | **Owner** | **Home-hunter** | **Admin** | **Public Visitor** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | View raw events | ❌ (no raw logs) | ❌ | ✅ (for debugging/analytics) | ❌ |
    | View aggregated stats (KPIs, charts) | ✅ For own places only | ❌ | ✅ Across all places | ❌ |
    
    Owner only sees **summaries**, never IPs or device IDs.
    
    ---
    
    ### **4. Calendar & Viewings**
    
    ### **3.7**
    
    ### **Viewing**
    
    ### **/ Calendar Events**
    
    | **Action** | **Owner** | **Home-hunter** | **Admin** | **Public Visitor** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | Request a viewing | N/A | ✅ (via WF-O5 or workspace) | N/A | ✅ (via WF-O5) |
    | Create confirmed viewing event | ✅ (convert request → event) | ❌ | ✅ (if assisting Owner) | ❌ |
    | View upcoming viewings (Owner calendar) | ✅ Own places only | ✅ Own booked viewings (future) | ✅ As support | ❌ |
    | Cancel / reschedule viewing | ✅ Own places (with notice) | ✅ For own bookings (future) | ✅ Assist both sides | ❌ |
    
    ---
    
    ### **5. Documents & File Vault**
    
    ### **3.8**
    
    ### **Document**
    
    ### **(EPC, floorplan, ownership etc.)**
    
    | **Document Type** | **Owner** | **Home-hunter / Public** | **Admin** |
    | --- | --- | --- | --- |
    | EPC (public) | ✅ Upload / view | ✅ View (if public) | ✅ View |
    | Floorplan (public) | ✅ Upload / view | ✅ View (if public) | ✅ View |
    | Ownership proof | ✅ Upload / view (private) | ❌ No access | ✅ View (for verification only) |
    | Lease documents | ✅ Upload / view (private) | ❌ No access | ✅ View |
    | Safety certificates | ✅ Upload / view (private) | ❌ No access | ✅ View |
    
    ---
    
    ### **6. Summary Rules (Pasteable Principles)**
    
    You can add this as a short summary block under the matrix:
    
    - **Public & Home-hunters** see **only** what’s needed to evaluate a place and contact the Owner.
    - **Owners** see everything about:
        - Their own places,
        - Inquiries and messages tied to those places,
        - Buyer contact details **only when that buyer has inquired about their place**.
    - **Admins** can see everything, but:
        - They are mainly used for troubleshooting, moderation, and support.
        - Any admin-only actions must be logged (Phase 2).
    - **No one** (except Admin) ever sees raw tracking data; Owners only see aggregated analytics.
    
    ---
    
    If you want, next I can:
    
    - Add a **short GDPR & Safety note** that you can attach to this matrix (esp. for messaging & buyer data), or
    - Create a **Home-hunter Workspace mini permission view**, so it’s ready when we build their wireframes.
- **GDPR & Safety Checklist**
    
    It is split into:
    
    - **A. Public Website Requirements**
    - **B. Owner Workspace Requirements**
    - **C. Data Model & Backend Requirements**
    - **D. Messaging & Email Requirements**
    - **E. Documentation Requirements**
    
    ---
    
    # **✅ GDPR & Safety Checklist (MVP)**
    
    This checklist ensures Yalla.House meets minimum GDPR, UX-safety and user-trust requirements across all wireframes (WF-O1 to WF-O5).
    
    ---
    
    # **A. PUBLIC WEBSITE (WF-O5 — Property Page)**
    
    ### **A.1 Inquiry Form**
    
    - Add short GDPR note under the “Message Owner” or “Arrange a Visit” button
        
        **Text:**
        
        *“By sending this inquiry you agree that your contact details will be shared with the Owner of this place for the purpose of answering your question or arranging a visit. You can request deletion at any time.”*
        
    - Add link to **Privacy Policy**
    - Do NOT show Owner’s direct email or phone publicly
    - Only show a secure message form
    
    ### **A.2 Viewing Booking Form**
    
    - Add short note:
        
        *“Your details will only be used to manage this viewing.”*
        
    
    ---
    
    # **B. OWNER WORKSPACE (WF-O3 — Inquiries)**
    
    ### **B.1 Visibility & UI**
    
    - Owners may ONLY see buyer details for inquiries on **their own places**
    - Display buyer email + phone (if provided) — never show to other Owners
    - Add a small banner at top of page:
        
        **Text:**
        
        *“You may only use buyer contact information for responding to this inquiry or arranging a viewing. Do not export or reuse this data for unrelated marketing.”*
        
    
    ### **B.2 Buyer Controls**
    
    - “⭐ Favourite buyer” button
    - “🚫 Block buyer” button
    - Block applies **per place** (MVP)
    - Owner cannot export email lists or download CSVs
    
    ---
    
    # **C. BACKEND & DATA MODEL**
    
    ### **C.1 Data Permissions**
    
    - Buyer contact details visible to:
        - Owner (for their listings)
        - Admin (for support)
    - No other sharing allowed
    
    ### **C.2 Logs**
    
    - Log every message send/open event (not personal data, just eventId, placeId, buyerId, timestamp)
    
    ### **C.3 GDPR Data Rights**
    
    Implement basic endpoints:
    
    - Request data deletion (Buyer)
    - Delete inquiry + messages on request
    - Export buyer’s message history on request
    
    ### **C.4 Storage**
    
    - Store buyer contact safely in DB
    - Hash or redact unused fields
    - Ensure HTTPS everywhere
    
    ---
    
    # **D. MESSAGING & EMAILS**
    
    ### **D.1 Buyer Email (Confirmation)**
    
    - Footer line:
        
        *“We share your inquiry and contact details only with the Owner of this place. You can ask us to delete your data at any time.”*
        
    
    ### **D.2 Owner Email (New Inquiry Notification)**
    
    - Footer line:
        
        *“Use this buyer’s details only to respond to their inquiry. Do not store or reuse for unrelated marketing.”*
        
    
    ### **D.3 Platform Messages**
    
    - AI suggestions must NOT include personal data
    - No automated messages without user action (MVP)
    
    ---
    
    # **E. DOCUMENTATION & INTERNAL**
    
    ### **E.1 Privacy Policy Page**
    
    Include:
    
    - What data is collected in an inquiry
    - Why it is shared with Owners
    - How Buyers request deletion
    - How long inquiry messages are stored
    - Admin access rules
    
    ### **E.2 Permission Matrix**
    
    Add rule:
    
    - “Buyer personal data is visible only to the Owner of the place they inquired about, and Admin for support.”
    
    ### **E.3 Developer Notes**
    
    - All UI text must come from i18n strings (not hard-coded)
    - System must be translatable later
    - Separate technical event logs from personal data
    
    ---
    
    #

## Below is the full, consolidated Product section.

- **System Architecture + Flows” diagram** (Owner + Home-Hunter + Admin
    1. **High-level architecture diagram (text/ASCII)**
    2. **Core user flows (Owner, Home-Hunter, Admin)**
    3. **Data & tracking flows (billing, analytics, surveys)**
    
    ---
    
    ## **1️⃣ High-Level System Architecture (Component Diagram)**
    
    You can imagine this as a 3-layer diagram:
    
    ```
    ┌───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
    │                    FRONTEND (Client Apps)                │
    │                                                           │
    │  • Owner Workspace (Framer / Dashfolio+)                  │
    │  • Home-Hunter Workspace (Framer / Dashfolio+)            │
    │  • Public Pages (Landing, Services, About, Property Page) │
    │  • Admin Console (Framer / protected routes)              │
    │                                                           │
    └──────────────────────────────┬────────────────────────────┘
                                   │ HTTPS / JSON (REST-ish)
    ┌──────────────────────────────┴────────────────────────────┐
    │                   BACKEND / CORE SERVICES                │
    │                                                           │
    │  • API Gateway / Backend App                              │
    │      - Auth & Roles (Owner / Home-Hunter / Admin / Founder)
    │      - CRUD for Places, Users, Viewings, Offers, Surveys  │
    │      - Inbox / Messaging service                          │
    │      - Calendar service (internal)                        │
    │      - Task & Fulfillment engine                          │
    │      - Recommendation engine (AI rules / future ML)       │
    │                                                           │
    │  • Billing Service                                        │
    │      - Talks to Stripe (subs, add-ons, surveys)           │
    │      - Maps payments ⮕ Owners, Places, Services           │
    │                                                           │
    │  • Integration Service                                    │
    │      - Portal feeds (Rightmove, Zoopla, OTM)              │
    │      - WhatsApp / Twilio                                  │
    │      - Email delivery                                     │
    │      - Calendar (Google etc.)                             │
    │      - Map API                                            │
    │                                                           │
    │  • Survey Marketplace Service                             │
    │      - Survey file store + metadata                       │
    │      - Upload / approval / pricing                        │
    │      - Purchase + access control                          │
    │                                                           │
    │  • Analytics & Logging                                    │
    │      - Event tracking (signups, listings, viewings, etc.) │
    │      - Daily/Monthly aggregates for WF-A9                 │
    │      - Error & integration logs for WF-A3                 │
    │                                                           │
    └──────────────────────────────┬────────────────────────────┘
                                   │
    ┌──────────────────────────────┴────────────────────────────┐
    │                 DATA & EXTERNAL INTEGRATIONS             │
    │                                                           │
    │  • Primary Database                                       │
    │      - Users (Owners, Home-Hunters, Admin)                │
    │      - Places (listings)                                  │
    │      - Inquiries, Messages, Viewings, Offers              │
    │      - Tasks, Support Tickets                             │
    │      - Surveys (metadata)                                 │
    │                                                           │
    │  • File Storage                                           │
    │      - Photos, floorplans, EPC, surveys                   │
    │                                                           │
    │  • Stripe (Billing & Payments)                            │
    │  • Airtable (Costs, ops bookkeeping, integrations costs)  │
    │  • Portals: Rightmove, Zoopla, OTM (feeds)                │
    │  • Twilio / WhatsApp                                      │
    │  • Email provider                                         │
    │  • Calendar (Google etc.)                                 │
    │  • Map / Geocoding API                                    │
    │                                                           │
    └───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
    ```
    
    **RBAC (Roles) is enforced in the BACKEND**, not only UI:
    
    - Owner (full access to their places, inquiries, viewings, offers, docs)
    - Home-Hunter (access to their bookings, offers, saved places, docs)
    - Admin (Ops + Support; no API keys, limited profit view)
    - Founder (full system access, forecasts, profit, keys, pricing)
    
    ---
    
    ## **2️⃣ Core User Flows**
    
    ### **2.1 Owner Flow – “List My Place & Manage Selling/Renting”**
    
    **Goal:** Owner signs up, lists a place, goes live on portals, manages inquiries & viewings.
    
    ```
    [Owner Browser (Framer)]
        ↓
        Auth Service (Sign up / Sign in)
        ↓
        WF-O2: My Listings (First-time flow)
            - Capture essentials: email, address, listing type, price
            - Create Place (status = Draft)
        ↓
    Backend:
        - Save Place in DB
        - Generate propertyID
        - Geocode address for map
        - Create default calendar slots (optional)
        - Track analytics event: "listing_created"
        ↓
    Owner continues setup:
        - Add photos, description, beds/baths
        - Upload EPC, floorplan (if available)
        ↓
    Owner clicks “Publish”
        ↓
    Backend:
        - Validate minimum requirements
        - Mark Place as Live
        - Send to Integration Service → portal feeds
        - Create QR Code asset for sign
        - Track “listing_published”
        ↓
    Portals:
        - Rightmove/Zoopla/OTM show listing
        - “Call” button points to NoAgent number / WhatsApp flow
        - “Email/contact” link points to NoAgent public property page (WF-O5)
        ↓
    Home-Hunters:
        - Visit Public Property Page
        - Click “Arrange a visit” / “Message owner”
        ↓
    Backend:
        - Create Inquiry
        - Notify Owner via Inbox + WhatsApp/email
        - Show in WF-O3 (Owner Inquiries)
    ```
    
    Then:
    
    - Owner uses **WF-O3 (Inquiries)** to answer buyers
    - Owner uses **WF-O4 (Calendar)** to manage slots (group + private)
    - Offers appear in Owner workspace + Admin WF-A2 for review
    - When deal done: **Place status → Under Offer → Sold / Rented**
    
    ---
    
    ### **2.2 Home-Hunter Flow – “Discover, Book Viewing, Make Offer”**
    
    **Goal:** Home-Hunter sees place (from portal or sign), books viewing, uploads docs, makes offer.
    
    ```
    Channel entry:
        - Rightmove / Zoopla / OTM listing link
        - QR Code from sign outside the house
        - Yalla.House direct page / referral
        ↓
    Public Property Page (WF-O5 / Public)
        - Show photos, price, description, map, documents (public)
        - CTAs: [Arrange a visit] [Message owner]
        ↓
    Click "Arrange a visit"
        ↓
    Booking Flow (WF-H1 / booking panel):
        - Pick timeslot (group or private)
        - Confirm channel (WhatsApp or email)
        - Required: Name, buying position, email, phone
        ↓
    Backend:
        - Create / link Home-Hunter account
        - Create Viewing record
        - Send confirmation to Home-Hunter (WhatsApp/email)
        - Sync with Owner calendar
        - Track event: "viewing_booked"
        ↓
    Viewing happens (offline)
        ↓
    Home-Hunter later:
        Logs in → Home-Hunter Workspace (Calendar + My Places)
        - sees viewing history
        - can mark favourites
        - can upload docs (ID, mortgage-in-principle)
        - can make offer
        ↓
    Offer creation:
        - Select Place
        - Choose amount
        - Attach docs
        - Confirm offer terms (cash / mortgage, timing)
        ↓
    Backend:
        - Store Offer
        - Notify Owner
        - Show in:
            - WF-O3 (Inquiries / Offers)
            - WF-A2 (Owner Detail View)
            - WF-A5 (Buyer Detail View)
        - Track event: "offer_made"
    ```
    
    If surveys exist:
    
    - Home-Hunter sees “Survey available (£X)” on property page
    - Payment via Stripe → unlock survey → event: “survey_purchased”
    
    ---
    
    ### **2.3 Admin Flow – “Monitor, Support, Fix, Optimise”**
    
    Admin lives mostly in **WF-A1..A9**:
    
    ```
    Admin logs in → WF-A1 Admin Dashboard
        - Sees KPIs, system health, owners at risk, tasks
        ↓
    Clicks an issue:
        - Owner underperforming → WF-A2 Owner Detail
        - Integration error → WF-A3 Integrations & Error Logs
        - Tasks → WF-A4 Tasks & Fulfillment
        - Buyer verification → WF-A5 Buyer Detail
        - Surveys → WF-A6 Survey Oversight
        - Support messages → WF-A7 Support Inbox
        - Billing → WF-A8 Billing Overview
        - Strategy view → WF-A9 Analytics Dashboard
    ```
    
    Admin flows:
    
    - Creates/assigns tasks (signs, EPC, support, verification)
    - Fixes portal sync issues (retry / update feed)
    - Reviews surveys and sets price
    - Monitors support SLAs
    - Monitors subscriptions + revenue
    - Follows AI recommendations (price adjustments, upsells, churn prevention)
    
    Founder has the same UI **plus**:
    
    - Full profit, cost, expansion forecasting (WF-A8, WF-A9 + future forecasting page)
    - Integration keys & pricing controls
    
    ---
    
    ## **3️⃣ Data & Tracking Flows**
    
    ### **3.1 Billing & Cost Flow**
    
    ```
    Owner action:
        - subscribes to plan
        - buys add-on (photo, EPC, floorplan)
        - survey purchased by buyer (linked to owner/place)
        ↓
    Frontend:
        - Calls Billing Service
        ↓
    Billing Service:
        - Creates Stripe Checkout session / subscription
        - Waits for Stripe webhooks
        ↓
    Stripe:
        - invoice.paid / payment_failed / subscription_updated
        ↓
    Billing Service (webhook handler):
        - Updates Owner billing record
        - Updates Place revenue (if per-listing)
        - Logs transaction (for WF-A8)
        - Emits analytics events (for WF-A9)
        ↓
    Airtable (Costs):
        - Rightmove / Zoopla / Twilio / hosting / surveys payout
        - Either: imported automatically OR entered semi-manually
        ↓
    Admin Billing (WF-A8):
        - Combines Stripe Income + Airtable Costs
        - Shows Revenue, Costs, Profit per Owner / per Place / per Month
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### **3.2 Analytics & Events Flow**
    
    Everything interesting in the system generates **events**:
    
    - owner_signup
    - place_created
    - place_published
    - viewing_booked
    - offer_made
    - offer_accepted
    - survey_uploaded
    - survey_purchased
    - subscription_started
    - subscription_cancelled
    - support_ticket_created
    
    Flow:
    
    ```
    Frontend (Owner/Home-Hunter/Admin)
        ↓
    Backend API:
        - processes action
        - writes event to `analytics_events` table or queue
        ↓
    Analytics Worker (batch):
        - aggregates per day / per country / per channel
        - updates `analytics_daily_summary` table
        ↓
    WF-A1:
        - shows current snapshot KPIs
    WF-A9:
        - shows trends, funnels, comparisons
    ```
    
    ---
    
    ### **3.3 Survey Marketplace Flow**
    
    ```
    Owner / Surveyor:
        - Uploads survey → WF-O2 / WF-A6
        ↓
    Survey Service:
        - Stores file
        - Creates survey record (status = pendingApproval)
        ↓
    Admin (WF-A6):
        - Reviews survey
        - Approves + sets price
        - Status = available
        ↓
    Home-Hunter:
        - Sees "Survey available (£X)" on WF-O5
        - Buys via Stripe
        ↓
    Billing Service:
        - records survey sale
        - records future payout if external surveyor
        ↓
    Survey Service:
        - grants read/download access to buyer
        - emits `survey_purchased` event for analytics
    ```
    
    ---
    
- **1–2 page “Product Vision**
- **Developer Handover Pack**
- **Wireframes & UX (Public)**
